The Odyssey, by Homer
=====================

Transcription Note
------------------
Transcribed by This Could Be Better.

This text was transcribed from an electronic copy hosted on http://www.perseus.tufts.edu/, which itself was adapted from the book _The Odyssey with an English Translation_, by A.T. Murray, Ph.D, which in turn was originally published by Harvard University Press in 1919.  That book, like all books published in or before (as of this writing) 1925, is now within the public domain in the United States of America, and so any copyright restrictions no longer apply.  And of course the original version, being thousands of years older, is firmly in the public domain as well.  Thus, to the best of the transcriber's understanding, this work can be legally copied and modified by anyone without restriction, at least within the United States or other territories with similar copyright laws.

The transcriber does not understand spoken or written Greek, much less Homeric Greek, and so any errors should not necessarily be attributed to the authors of any of the preceding works.  This transcription was undertaken to remedy the transcriber's frustration with the difficulty of locating a simple, complete copy of the original, untranslated work, with no added complications, for study.



Transliteration Note
--------------------
This text was transliterated from the original Greek into Latin characters by This Could Be Better.

The transliteration was performed using the automated transliteration tool currently available at:

	https://thiscouldbebetter.github.io/Source/TextTransliterator/Source/TextTransliterator.html.

The original Greek text has an impressive variety of diacritical marks, which presumably represent an equally impressive variety of distinct sounds.  For purposes of this transliteration, however, all such variations have been ignored.  It is hoped that this loss of precision will not hinder further translation efforts.



The Odyssey
===========

Book 1
------

andra moi ennepe, mousa, polutropon, os mala polla
plagkhthee, epei Troiees ieron ptoliethron epersen:
pollohn d᾽ anthrohpohn iden astea kai noon egnoh,
polla d᾽ o g᾽ en pontoh pathen algea on kata thumon,
arnumenos een te psukheen kai noston etairohn.
all᾽ oud᾽ ohs etarous errusato, iemenos per:
autohn gar sfetereesin atasthalieesin olonto,
neepioi, oi kata bous Uperionos Eeelioio
eesthion: autar o toisin afeileto nostimon eemar.
tohn amothen ge, thea, thugater Dios, eipe kai eemin.

enth᾽ alloi men pantes, osoi fugon aipun olethron,
oikoi esan, polemon te pefeugotes eede thalassan:
ton d᾽ oion nostou kekhreemenon eede gunaikos
numfee potni᾽ eruke Kalupsoh dia theaohn
en spessi glafuroisi, lilaiomenee posin einai.
all᾽ ote dee etos eelthe periplomenohn eniautohn,
toh oi epeklohsanto theoi oikonde neesthai
eis Ithakeen, oud᾽ entha pefugmenos eeen aethlohn
kai meta oisi filoisi. theoi d᾽ eleairon apantes
nosfi Poseidaohnos: o d᾽ asperkhes meneainen
antitheoh Oduseei paros een gaian ikesthai.

all᾽ o men Aithiopas metekiathe teeloth᾽ eontas,
Aithiopas toi dikhtha dedaiatai, eskhatoi androhn,
oi men dusomenou Uperionos oi d᾽ aniontos,
antioohn taurohn te kai arneiohn ekatombees.
enth᾽ o g᾽ eterpeto daiti pareemenos: oi de dee alloi
Zeenos eni megaroisin Olumpiou athrooi eesan.
toisi de muthohn eerkhe pateer androhn te theohn te:
mneesato gar kata thumon amumonos Aigisthoio,
ton r᾽ Agamemnonidees teeleklutos ektan᾽ Orestees:
tou o g᾽ epimneestheis epe᾽ athanatoisi meteeuda:
"

oh popoi, oion dee nu theous brotoi aitioohntai:
ex eemeohn gar fasi kak᾽ emmenai, oi de kai autoi
sfeesin atasthalieesin uper moron alge᾽ ekhousin,
ohs kai nun Aigisthos uper moron Atreidao
geem᾽ alokhon mneesteen, ton d᾽ ektane nosteesanta,
eidohs aipun olethron, epei pro oi eipomen eemeis,
Ermeian pempsantes, euskopon argeifonteen,
meet᾽ auton kteinein meete mnaasthai akoitin:
ek gar Orestao tisis essetai Atreidao,
oppot᾽ an eebeesee te kai ees imeiretai aiees.
ohs efath᾽ Ermeias, all᾽ ou frenas Aigisthoio
peith᾽ agatha froneohn: nun d᾽ athroa pant᾽ apetisen.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"oh pater eemetere Kronidee, upate kreiontohn,
kai lieen keinos ge eoikoti keitai olethroh:
ohs apoloito kai allos, otis toiauta ge rezoi:
alla moi amf᾽ Oduseei daifroni daietai eetor,
dusmoroh, os dee deetha filohn apo peemata paskhei
neesoh en amfirutee, othi t᾽ omfalos esti thalassees.
neesos dendreeessa, thea d᾽ en dohmata naiei,
Atlantos thugateer oloofronos, os te thalassees
pasees benthea oiden, ekhei de te kionas autos
makras, ai gaian te kai ouranon amfis ekhousin.
tou thugateer dusteenon oduromenon katerukei,
aiei de malakoisi kai aimulioisi logoisin
thelgei, opohs Ithakees epileesetai: autar Odusseus,
iemenos kai kapnon apothrohskonta noeesai
ees gaiees, thaneein imeiretai. oude nu soi per
entrepetai filon eetor, Olumpie. ou nu t᾽ Odusseus
Argeiohn para neeusi kharizeto iera rezohn
Troiee en eureiee; ti nu oi toson ohdusao, Zeu;
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee nefeleegereta Zeus:
"teknon emon, poion se epos fugen erkos odontohn.
pohs an epeit᾽ Oduseeos egoh theioio lathoimeen,
os peri men noon esti brotohn, peri d᾽ ira theoisin
athanatoisin edohke, toi ouranon eurun ekhousin;
alla Poseidaohn gaieeokhos askeles aiei
Kuklohpos kekholohtai, on ofthalmou alaohsen,
antitheon Polufeemon, oou kratos esti megiston
pasin Kuklohpessi: Thoohsa de min teke numfee,
Forkunos thugateer alos atrugetoio medontos,
en spessi glafuroisi Poseidaohni migeisa.
ek tou dee Oduseea Poseidaohn enosikhthohn
ou ti katakteinei, plazei d᾽ apo patridos aiees.
all᾽ ageth᾽, eemeis oide perifrazohmetha pantes
noston, opohs eltheesi: Poseidaohn de metheesei
on kholon: ou men gar ti duneesetai antia pantohn
athanatohn aekeeti theohn eridainemen oios.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"oh pater eemetere Kronidee, upate kreiontohn,
ei men dee nun touto filon makaressi theoisin,
nosteesai Oduseea polufrona onde domonde,
Ermeian men epeita diaktoron argeifonteen
neeson es Ohgugieen otrunomen, ofra takhista
numfee euplokamoh eipee neemertea bouleen,
noston Odusseeos talasifronos, ohs ke neeetai:
autar egohn Ithakeend᾽ eseleusomai, ofra oi uion
mallon epotrunoh kai oi menos en fresi theioh,
eis agoreen kalesanta karee komoohntas Akhaious
pasi mneesteeressin apeipemen, oi te oi aiei
meel᾽ adina sfazousi kai eilipodas elikas bous.
pempsoh d᾽ es Sparteen te kai es Pulon eemathoenta
noston peusomenon patros filou, een pou akousee,
eed᾽ ina min kleos esthlon en anthrohpoisin ekheesin.
"

ohs eipous᾽ upo possin edeesato kala pedila,
ambrosia khruseia, ta min feron eemen ef᾽ ugreen
eed᾽ ep᾽ apeirona gaian ama pnoiees anemoio:
eileto d᾽ alkimon egkhos, akakhmenon oxei khalkoh,
brithu mega stibaron, toh damneesi stikhas androhn
eerohohn, toisin te kotessetai obrimopatree.
bee de kat᾽ Oulumpoio kareenohn aixasa,
stee d᾽ Ithakees eni deemoh epi prothurois Oduseeos,
oudou ep᾽ auleiou: palamee d᾽ ekhe khalkeon egkhos,
eidomenee xeinoh, Tafiohn eegeetori Mentee.
eure d᾽ ara mneesteeras ageenoras. oi men epeita
pessoisi proparoithe thuraohn thumon eterpon
eemenoi en rinoisi boohn, ous ektanon autoi:
keerukes d᾽ autoisi kai otreeroi therapontes
oi men oinon emisgon eni kreeteersi kai udohr,
oi d᾽ aute spoggoisi polutreetoisi trapezas
nizon kai protithen, toi de krea polla dateunto.

teen de polu prohtos ide Teelemakhos theoeidees,
eesto gar en mneesteersi filon tetieemenos eetor,
ossomenos pater᾽ esthlon eni fresin, ei pothen elthohn
mneesteerohn tohn men skedasin kata dohmata theiee,
timeen d᾽ autos ekhoi kai dohmasin oisin anassoi.
ta froneohn, mneesteersi metheemenos, eisid᾽ Atheeneen.
bee d᾽ ithus prothuroio, nemesseethee d᾽ eni thumoh
xeinon deetha thureesin efestamen: egguthi de stas
kheir᾽ ele dexitereen kai edexato khalkeon egkhos,
kai min fohneesas epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

khaire, xeine, par᾽ ammi fileeseai: autar epeita
deipnou passamenos mutheeseai otteo se khree.
"

ohs eipohn eegeith᾽, ee d᾽ espeto Pallas Atheenee.
oi d᾽ ote dee r᾽ entosthen esan domou upseeloio,
egkhos men r᾽ esteese ferohn pros kiona makreen
dourodokees entosthen euxoou, entha per alla
egkhe᾽ Odusseeos talasifronos istato polla,
auteen d᾽ es thronon eisen agohn, upo lita petassas,
kalon daidaleon: upo de threenus posin eeen.
par d᾽ autos klismon theto poikilon, ektothen allohn
mneesteerohn, mee xeinos anieetheis orumagdoh
deipnoh adeeseien, uperfialoisi metelthohn,
eed᾽ ina min peri patros apoikhomenoio eroito.
kherniba d᾽ amfipolos prokhooh epekheue ferousa
kalee khruseiee, uper argureoio lebeetos,
nipsasthai: para de xesteen etanusse trapezan.
siton d᾽ aidoiee tamiee paretheeke ferousa,
eidata poll᾽ epitheisa, kharizomenee pareontohn:
daitros de kreiohn pinakas paretheeken aeiras
pantoiohn, para de sfi tithei khruseia kupella:
keerux d᾽ autoisin tham᾽ epohkheto oinokhoeuohn.

es d᾽ eelthon mneesteeres ageenores. oi men epeita
exeiees ezonto kata klismous te thronous te,
toisi de keerukes men udohr epi kheiras ekheuan,
siton de dmohai pareneeneon en kaneoisin,
kouroi de kreeteeras epestepsanto potoio.
oi d᾽ ep᾽ oneiath᾽ etoima prokeimena kheiras iallon.
autar epei posios kai edeetuos ex eron ento
mneesteeres, toisin men eni fresin alla memeelei,
molpee t᾽ orkheestus te: ta gar t᾽ anatheemata daitos:
keerux d᾽ en khersin kitharin perikallea theeken
Feemioh, os r᾽ eeeide para mneesteersin anagkee.
ee toi o formizohn aneballeto kalon aeidein.

autar Teelemakhos prosefee glaukohpin Atheeneen,
agkhi skhohn kefaleen, ina mee peuthoiath᾽ oi alloi:
"xeine fil᾽, ee kai moi nemeseeseai otti ken eipoh;
toutoisin men tauta melei, kitharis kai aoidee,
rei᾽, epei allotrion bioton neepoinon edousin,
aneros, ou dee pou leuk᾽ ostea puthetai ombroh
keimen᾽ ep᾽ eepeirou, ee ein ali kuma kulindei.
ei keinon g᾽ Ithakeende idoiato nosteesanta,
pantes k᾽ areesaiat᾽ elafroteroi podas einai
ee afneioteroi khrusoio te estheetos te.
nun d᾽ o men ohs apolohle kakon moron, oude tis eemin
thalpohree, ei per tis epikhthoniohn anthrohpohn
feesin eleusesthai: tou d᾽ ohleto nostimon eemar.
all᾽ age moi tode eipe kai atrekeohs katalexon:
tis pothen eis androhn; pothi toi polis eede tokeees;
oppoiees t᾽ epi neeos afikeo: pohs de se nautai
eegagon eis Ithakeen; tines emmenai eukhetoohnto;
ou men gar ti se pezon oiomai enthad᾽ ikesthai.
kai moi tout᾽ agoreuson eteetumon, ofr᾽ eu eidoh,
eee neon methepeis ee kai patrohios essi
xeinos, epei polloi isan aneres eemeteron doh
alloi, epei kai keinos epistrofos een anthrohpohn.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"toigar egoh toi tauta mal᾽ atrekeohs agoreusoh.
Mentees Agkhialoio daifronos eukhomai einai
uios, atar Tafioisi fileeretmoisin anassoh.
nun d᾽ ohde xun neei kateeluthon eed᾽ etaroisin
pleohn epi oinopa ponton ep᾽ allothroous anthrohpous,
es Temeseen meta khalkon, agoh d᾽ aithohna sideeron.
neeus de moi eed᾽ esteeken ep᾽ agrou nosfi poleeos,
en limeni Reithroh upo Neeioh uleeenti.
xeinoi d᾽ alleelohn patrohioi eukhometh᾽ einai
ex arkhees, ei per te geront᾽ eireeai epelthohn
Laerteen eeroha, ton ouketi fasi polinde
erkhesth᾽, all᾽ apaneuthen ep᾽ agrou peemata paskhein
greei sun amfipoloh, ee oi brohsin te posin te
partithei, eut᾽ an min kamatos kata guia labeesin
erpuzont᾽ ana gounon alohees oinopedoio.
nun d᾽ eelthon: dee gar min efant᾽ epideemion einai,
son pater᾽: alla nu ton ge theoi blaptousi keleuthou.
ou gar poh tethneeken epi khthoni dios Odusseus,
all᾽ eti pou zohos kateruketai eurei pontoh
neesoh en amfirutee, khalepoi de min andres ekhousin
agrioi, oi pou keinon erukanoohs᾽ aekonta.
autar nun toi egoh manteusomai, ohs eni thumoh
athanatoi ballousi kai ohs teleesthai oioh,
oute ti mantis eohn out᾽ oiohnohn safa eidohs.
ou toi eti deeron ge filees apo patridos aiees
essetai, oud᾽ ei per te sideerea desmat᾽ ekheesin:
frassetai ohs ke neeetai, epei polumeekhanos estin.
all᾽ age moi tode eipe kai atrekeohs katalexon,
ei dee ex autoio tosos pais eis Oduseeos.
ainohs men kefaleen te kai ommata kala eoikas
keinoh, epei thama toion emisgometh᾽ alleeloisin,
prin ge ton es Troieen anabeemenai, entha per alloi
Argeiohn oi aristoi eban koilees eni neeusin:
ek tou d᾽ out᾽ Oduseea egohn idon out᾽ em᾽ ekeinos.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"toigar egoh toi, xeine, mal᾽ atrekeohs agoreusoh.
meeteer men te me feesi tou emmenai, autar egoh ge
ouk oid᾽: ou gar poh tis eon gonon autos anegnoh.
ohs dee egoh g᾽ ofelon makaros nu teu emmenai uios
aneros, on kteatessin eois epi geeras etetme.
nun d᾽ os apotmotatos geneto thneetohn anthrohpohn,
tou m᾽ ek fasi genesthai, epei su me tout᾽ ereeineis.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"ou men toi geneeen ge theoi nohnumnon opissoh
theekan, epei se ge toion egeinato Peenelopeia.
all᾽ age moi tode eipe kai atrekeohs katalexon:
tis dais, tis de omilos od᾽ epleto; tipte de se khreoh;
eilapinee eee gamos; epei ouk eranos tade g᾽ estin:
ohs te moi ubrizontes uperfialohs dokeousi
dainusthai kata dohma. nemesseesaito ken aneer
aiskhea poll᾽ oroohn, os tis pinutos ge metelthoi.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"xein᾽, epei ar dee tauta m᾽ aneireai eede metallas,
mellen men pote oikos od᾽ afneios kai amumohn
emmenai, ofr᾽ eti keinos aneer epideemios eeen:
nun d᾽ eterohs ebolonto theoi kaka meetioohntes,
oi keinon men aiston epoieesan peri pantohn
anthrohpohn, epei ou ke thanonti per ohd᾽ akakhoimeen,
ei meta ois etaroisi damee Trohohn eni deemoh,
eee filohn en khersin, epei polemon tolupeusen.
toh ken oi tumbon men epoieesan Panakhaioi,
eede ke kai oh paidi mega kleos eerat᾽ opissoh.
nun de min akleiohs arpuiai aneereipsanto:
oikhet᾽ aistos apustos, emoi d᾽ odunas te goous te
kallipen. oude ti keinon oduromenos stenakhizoh
oion, epei nu moi alla theoi kaka keede᾽ eteuxan.
ossoi gar neesoisin epikrateousin aristoi,
Doulikhioh te Samee te kai uleeenti Zakunthoh,
eed᾽ ossoi kranaeen Ithakeen kata koiraneousin,
tossoi meeter᾽ emeen mnohntai, trukhousi de oikon.
ee d᾽ out᾽ arneitai stugeron gamon oute teleuteen
poieesai dunatai: toi de fthinuthousin edontes
oikon emon: takha dee me diarraisousi kai auton.
"

ton d᾽ epalasteesasa proseeuda Pallas Atheenee:
"oh popoi, ee dee pollon apoikhomenou Oduseeos
deuee, o ke mneesteersin anaidesi kheiras efeiee.
ei gar nun elthohn domou en prohteesi thureesi
staiee, ekhohn peeleeka kai aspida kai duo doure,
toios eohn oion min egoh ta proht᾽ enoeesa
oikoh en eemeteroh pinonta te terpomenon te,
ex Efurees anionta par᾽ Ilou Mermeridao--
ohkheto gar kai keise thoees epi neeos Odusseus
farmakon androfonon dizeemenos, ofra oi eiee
ious khriesthai khalkeereas: all᾽ o men ou oi
dohken, epei ra theous nemesizeto aien eontas,
alla pateer oi dohken emos: fileeske gar ainohs--
toios eohn mneesteersin omileeseien Odusseus:
pantes k᾽ ohkumoroi te genoiato pikrogamoi te.
all᾽ ee toi men tauta theohn en gounasi keitai,
ee ken nosteesas apotisetai, eee kai ouki,
oisin eni megaroisi: se de frazesthai anohga,
oppohs ke mneesteeras apohseai ek megaroio.
ei d᾽ age nun xuniei kai emohn empazeo muthohn:
aurion eis agoreen kalesas eerohas Akhaious
muthon pefrade pasi, theoi d᾽ epi marturoi estohn.
mneesteeras men epi sfetera skidnasthai anohkhthi,
meetera d᾽, ei oi thumos eformatai gameesthai,
aps itoh es megaron patros mega dunamenoio:
oi de gamon teuxousi kai artuneousin eedna
polla mal᾽, ossa eoike filees epi paidos epesthai.
soi d᾽ autoh pukinohs upotheesomai, ai ke pitheeai:
nee᾽ arsas ereteesin eeikosin, ee tis aristee,
erkheo peusomenos patros deen oikhomenoio,
een tis toi eipeesi brotohn, ee ossan akousees
ek Dios, ee te malista ferei kleos anthrohpoisi.
prohta men es Pulon elthe kai eireo Nestora dion,
keithen de Sparteende para xanthon Menelaon:
os gar deutatos eelthen Akhaiohn khalkokhitohnohn.
ei men ken patros bioton kai noston akousees,
ee t᾽ an trukhomenos per eti tlaiees eniauton:
ei de ke tethneeohtos akousees meed᾽ et᾽ eontos,
nosteesas dee epeita fileen es patrida gaian
seema te oi kheuai kai epi kterea ktereixai
polla mal᾽, ossa eoike, kai aneri meetera dounai.
autar epeen dee tauta teleuteesees te kai erxees,
frazesthai dee epeita kata frena kai kata thumon
oppohs ke mneesteeras eni megaroisi teoisi
kteinees eee doloh ee amfadon: oude ti se khree
neepiaas okheein, epei ouketi teelikos essi.
ee ouk aieis oion kleos ellabe dios Orestees
pantas ep᾽ anthrohpous, epei ektane patrofoneea,
Aigisthon dolomeetin, o oi patera kluton ekta;
kai su, filos, mala gar s᾽ orooh kalon te megan te,
alkimos ess᾽, ina tis se kai opsigonohn eu eipee.
autar egohn epi neea thoeen kateleusomai eedee
eed᾽ etarous, oi pou me mal᾽ askhaloohsi menontes:
soi d᾽ autoh meletoh, kai emohn empazeo muthohn.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"xein᾽, ee toi men tauta fila froneohn agoreueis,
ohs te pateer oh paidi, kai ou pote leesomai autohn.
all᾽ age nun epimeinon, epeigomenos per odoio,
ofra loessamenos te tetarpomenos te filon keer,
dohron ekhohn epi neea kiees, khairohn eni thumoh,
timeeen, mala kalon, o toi keimeelion estai
ex emeu, oia filoi xeinoi xeinoisi didousi.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"mee m᾽ eti nun kateruke, lilaiomenon per odoio.
dohron d᾽ otti ke moi dounai filon eetor anohgee,
autis anerkhomenoh domenai oikonde feresthai,
kai mala kalon elohn: soi d᾽ axion estai amoibees.
"

ee men ar᾽ ohs eipous᾽ apebee glaukohpis Atheenee,
ornis d᾽ ohs anopaia dieptato: toh d᾽ eni thumoh
theeke menos kai tharsos, upemneesen te e patros
mallon et᾽ ee to paroithen. o de fresin eesi noeesas
thambeesen kata thumon: oisato gar theon einai.
autika de mneesteeras epohkheto isotheos fohs.

toisi d᾽ aoidos aeide periklutos, oi de siohpee
eeat᾽ akouontes: o d᾽ Akhaiohn noston aeide
lugron, on ek Troiees epeteilato Pallas Atheenee.
tou d᾽ uperohiothen fresi suntheto thespin aoideen
kouree Ikarioio, perifrohn Peenelopeia:
klimaka d᾽ upseeleen katebeeseto oio domoio,
ouk oiee, ama tee ge kai amfipoloi du᾽ eponto.
ee d᾽ ote dee mneesteeras afiketo dia gunaikohn,
stee ra para stathmon tegeos puka poieetoio,
anta pareiaohn skhomenee lipara kreedemna:
amfipolos d᾽ ara oi kednee ekaterthe parestee.
dakrusasa d᾽ epeita proseeuda theion aoidon:
"

Feemie, polla gar alla brotohn thelkteeria oidas,
erg᾽ androhn te theohn te, ta te kleiousin aoidoi:
tohn en ge sfin aeide pareemenos, oi de siohpee
oinon pinontohn: tautees d᾽ apopaue᾽ aoidees
lugrees, ee te moi aiei eni steethessi filon keer
teirei, epei me malista kathiketo penthos alaston.
toieen gar kefaleen potheoh memneemenee aiei,
andros, tou kleos euru kath᾽ Ellada kai meson Argos.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"meeter emee, ti t᾽ ara fthoneeis erieeron aoidon
terpein oppee oi noos ornutai; ou nu t᾽ aoidoi
aitioi, alla pothi Zeus aitios, os te didohsin
andrasin alfeesteesin, opohs etheleesin, ekastoh.
toutoh d᾽ ou nemesis Danaohn kakon oiton aeidein:
teen gar aoideen mallon epikleious᾽ anthrohpoi,
ee tis akouontessi neohtatee amfipeleetai.
soi d᾽ epitolmatoh kradiee kai thumos akouein:
ou gar Odusseus oios apohlese nostimon eemar
en Troiee, polloi de kai alloi fohtes olonto.
all᾽ eis oikon iousa ta s᾽ autees erga komize,
iston t᾽ eelakateen te, kai amfipoloisi keleue
ergon epoikhesthai: muthos d᾽ andressi meleesei
pasi, malista d᾽ emoi: tou gar kratos est᾽ eni oikoh.
"

ee men thambeesasa palin oikonde bebeekei:
paidos gar muthon pepnumenon entheto thumoh.
es d᾽ uperoh᾽ anabasa sun amfipoloisi gunaixi
klaien epeit᾽ Oduseea filon posin, ofra oi upnon
eedun epi blefaroisi bale glaukohpis Atheenee.

mneesteeres d᾽ omadeesan ana megara skioenta,
pantes d᾽ eereesanto parai lekheessi klitheenai.
toisi de Teelemakhos pepnumenos eerkheto muthohn:
"

meetros emees mneesteeres uperbion ubrin ekhontes,
nun men dainumenoi terpohmetha, meede boeetus
estoh, epei tode kalon akouemen estin aoidou
toioud᾽ oios od᾽ esti, theois enaligkios audeen.
eeohthen d᾽ agoreende kathezohmestha kiontes
pantes, in᾽ umin muthon apeelegeohs apoeipoh,
exienai megarohn: allas d᾽ alegunete daitas,
uma kteemat᾽ edontes, ameibomenoi kata oikous.
ei d᾽ umin dokeei tode lohiteron kai ameinon
emmenai, andros enos bioton neepoinon olesthai,
keiret᾽: egoh de theous epibohsomai aien eontas,
ai ke pothi Zeus dohsi palintita erga genesthai:
neepoinoi ken epeita domohn entosthen oloisthe.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes odax en kheilesi funtes
Teelemakhon thaumazon, o tharsaleohs agoreuen.

ton d᾽ aut᾽ Antinoos prosefee, Eupeitheos uios:
"Teelemakh᾽, ee mala dee se didaskousin theoi autoi
upsagoreen t᾽ emenai kai tharsaleohs agoreuein:
mee se g᾽ en amfialoh Ithakee basileea Kroniohn
poieeseien, o toi geneee patrohion estin.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Antino᾽, ee kai moi nemeseeseai otti ken eipoh;
kai ken tout᾽ etheloimi Dios ge didontos aresthai.
ee fees touto kakiston en anthrohpoisi tetukhthai;
ou men gar ti kakon basileuemen: aipsa te oi doh
afneion peletai kai timeeesteros autos.
all᾽ ee toi basileees Akhaiohn eisi kai alloi
polloi en amfialoh Ithakee, neoi eede palaioi,
tohn ken tis tod᾽ ekheesin, epei thane dios Odusseus:
autar egohn oikoio anax esom᾽ eemeteroio
kai dmohohn, ous moi leeissato dios Odusseus.
"

ton d᾽ aut᾽ Eurumakhos Polubou pais antion eeuda:
"Teelemakh᾽, ee toi tauta theohn en gounasi keitai,
os tis en amfialoh Ithakee basileusei Akhaiohn:
kteemata d᾽ autos ekhois kai dohmasin oisin anassois.
mee gar o g᾽ elthoi aneer os tis s᾽ aekonta bieefin
kteemat᾽ aporraisei, Ithakees eti naietoohsees.
all᾽ etheloh se, feriste, peri xeinoio eresthai,
oppothen outos aneer, poiees d᾽ ex eukhetai einai
gaiees, pou de nu oi geneee kai patris aroura.
eee tin᾽ aggelieen patros ferei erkhomenoio,
ee eon autou khreios eeldomenos tod᾽ ikanei;
oion anaixas afar oikhetai, oud᾽ upemeine
gnohmenai: ou men gar ti kakoh eis ohpa eohkei.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Eurumakh᾽, ee toi nostos apohleto patros emoio:
out᾽ oun aggeliee eti peithomai, ei pothen elthoi,
oute theopropiees empazomai, een tina meeteer
es megaron kalesasa theopropon exereeetai.
xeinos d᾽ outos emos patrohios ek Tafou estin,
Mentees d᾽ Agkhialoio daifronos eukhetai einai
uios, atar Tafioisi fileeretmoisin anassei.
"

ohs fato Teelemakhos, fresi d᾽ athanateen theon egnoh.
oi d᾽ eis orkheestun te kai imeroessan aoideen
trepsamenoi terponto, menon d᾽ epi esperon elthein.
toisi de terpomenoisi melas epi esperos eelthe:
dee tote kakkeiontes eban oikonde ekastos.
Teelemakhos d᾽, othi oi thalamos perikalleos aulees
upseelos dedmeeto periskeptoh eni khohroh,
enth᾽ ebee eis euneen polla fresi mermeerizohn.
toh d᾽ ar᾽ am᾽ aithomenas daidas fere kedna iduia
Euruklei᾽, Ohpos thugateer Peiseenoridao,
teen pote Laertees priato kteatessin eoisin
prohtheebeen et᾽ eousan, eeikosaboia d᾽ edohken,
isa de min kednee alokhoh tien en megaroisin,
eunee d᾽ ou pot᾽ emikto, kholon d᾽ aleeine gunaikos:
ee oi am᾽ aithomenas daidas fere, kai e malista
dmohaohn fileeske, kai etrefe tutthon eonta.
ohixen de thuras thalamou puka poieetoio,
ezeto d᾽ en lektroh, malakon d᾽ ekdune khitohna:
kai ton men graiees pukimeedeos embale khersin.
ee men ton ptuxasa kai askeesasa khitohna,
passaloh agkremasasa para treetoisi lekhessi
bee r᾽ imen ek thalamoio, thureen d᾽ eperusse korohnee
argureee, epi de kleeid᾽ etanussen imanti.
enth᾽ o ge pannukhios, kekalummenos oios aohtoh,
bouleue fresin eesin odon teen pefrad᾽ Atheenee.


Book 2
------

eemos d᾽ eerigeneia fanee rododaktulos Eeohs,
ohrnut᾽ ar᾽ ex euneefin Odusseeos filos uios
eimata essamenos, peri de xifos oxu thet᾽ ohmoh,
possi d᾽ upo liparoisin edeesato kala pedila,
bee d᾽ imen ek thalamoio theoh enaligkios anteen.
aipsa de keerukessi ligufthoggoisi keleuse
keerussein agoreende karee komoohntas Akhaious.
oi men ekeerusson, toi d᾽ eegeironto mal᾽ ohka.
autar epei r᾽ eegerthen omeegerees t᾽ egenonto,
bee r᾽ imen eis agoreen, palamee d᾽ ekhe khalkeon egkhos,
ouk oios, ama toh ge duoh kunes argoi eponto.
thespesieen d᾽ ara toh ge kharin katekheuen Atheenee.
ton d᾽ ara pantes laoi eperkhomenon theeeunto:
ezeto d᾽ en patros thohkoh, eixan de gerontes.
toisi d᾽ epeith᾽ eerohs Aiguptios eerkh᾽ agoreuein,
os dee geerai kufos eeen kai muria eedee.
kai gar tou filos uios am᾽ antitheoh Oduseei
Ilion eis eupohlon ebee koilees eni neeusin,
Antifos aikhmeetees: ton d᾽ agrios ektane Kuklohps
en speei glafuroh, pumaton d᾽ ohplissato dorpon.
treis de oi alloi esan, kai o men mneesteersin omilei,
Eurunomos, duo d᾽ aien ekhon patrohia erga.
all᾽ oud᾽ ohs tou leethet᾽ oduromenos kai akheuohn.
tou o ge dakru kheohn agoreesato kai meteeipe:
"
keklute dee nun meu, Ithakeesioi, otti ken eipoh:
oute poth᾽ eemeteree agoree genet᾽ oute thoohkos
ex ou Odusseus dios ebee koilees eni neeusi.
nun de tis ohd᾽ eegeire; tina khreioh toson ikei
eee neohn androhn ee oi progenesteroi eisin;
eee tin᾽ aggelieen stratou ekluen erkhomenoio,
een kh᾽ eemin safa eipoi, ote proteros ge puthoito;
eee ti deemion allo pifausketai eed᾽ agoreuei;
esthlos moi dokei einai, oneemenos. eithe oi autoh
Zeus agathon teleseien, oti fresin eesi menoina.
"

ohs fato, khaire de feemee Odusseeos filos uios,
oud᾽ ar᾽ eti deen eesto, menoineesen d᾽ agoreuein,
stee de mesee agoree: skeeptron de oi embale kheiri
keerux Peiseenohr pepnumena meedea eidohs.
prohton epeita geronta kathaptomenos proseeipen:
"

oh geron, oukh ekas outos aneer, takha d᾽ eiseai autos,
os laon eegeira: malista de m᾽ algos ikanei.
oute tin᾽ aggelieen stratou ekluon erkhomenoio,
een kh᾽ umin safa eipoh, ote proteros ge puthoimeen,
oute ti deemion allo pifauskomai oud᾽ agoreuoh,
all᾽ emon autou khreios, o moi kaka empesen oikoh
doia: to men pater᾽ esthlon apohlesa, os pot᾽ en umin
toisdessin basileue, pateer d᾽ ohs eepios eeen:
nun d᾽ au kai polu meizon, o dee takha oikon apanta
pagkhu diarraisei, bioton d᾽ apo pampan olessei.
meeteri moi mneesteeres epekhraon ouk ethelousee,
tohn androhn filoi uies, oi enthade g᾽ eisin aristoi,
oi patros men es oikon aperrigasi neesthai
Ikariou, ohs k᾽ autos eednohsaito thugatra,
doiee d᾽ oh k᾽ etheloi kai oi kekharismenos elthoi:
oi d᾽ eis eemeteron pohleumenoi eemata panta,
bous iereuontes kai ois kai pionas aigas
eilapinazousin pinousi te aithopa oinon
mapsidiohs: ta de polla katanetai. ou gar ep᾽ aneer,
oios Odusseus esken, areen apo oikou amunai.
eemeis d᾽ ou nu ti toioi amunemen: ee kai epeita
leugaleoi t᾽ esomestha kai ou dedaeekotes alkeen.
ee t᾽ an amunaimeen, ei moi dunamis ge pareiee.
ou gar et᾽ anskheta erga teteukhatai, oud᾽ eti kalohs
oikos emos diolohle. nemesseetheete kai autoi,
allous t᾽ aidestheete periktionas anthrohpous,
oi perinaietaousi: theohn d᾽ upodeisate meenin,
mee ti metastrepsohsin agassamenoi kaka erga.
lissomai eemen Zeenos Olumpiou eede Themistos,
ee t᾽ androhn agoras eemen luei eede kathizei:
skhesthe, filoi, kai m᾽ oion easate penthei lugroh
teiresth᾽, ei mee pou ti pateer emos esthlos Odusseus
dusmeneohn kak᾽ erexen eukneemidas Akhaious,
tohn m᾽ apotinumenoi kaka rezete dusmeneontes,
toutous otrunontes. emoi de ke kerdion eiee
umeas esthemenai keimeelia te probasin te.
ei kh᾽ umeis ge fagoite, takh᾽ an pote kai tisis eiee:
tofra gar an kata astu potiptussoimetha muthoh
khreemat᾽ apaitizontes, eohs k᾽ apo panta dotheiee:
nun de moi apreektous odunas emballete thumoh.
"

ohs fato khohomenos, poti de skeeptron bale gaiee
dakru᾽ anapreesas: oiktos d᾽ ele laon apanta.
enth᾽ alloi men pantes akeen esan, oude tis etlee
Teelemakhon muthoisin ameipsasthai khalepoisin:
Antinoos de min oios ameibomenos proseeipe:
"

Teelemakh᾽ upsagoree, menos askhete, poion eeipes
eemeas aiskhunohn: ethelois de ke mohmon anapsai.
soi d᾽ ou ti mneesteeres Akhaiohn aitioi eisin,
alla filee meeteer, ee toi peri kerdea oiden.
eedee gar triton estin etos, takha d᾽ eisi tetarton,
ex ou atembei thumon eni steethessin Akhaiohn.
pantas men r᾽ elpei kai upiskhetai andri ekastoh
aggelias proieisa, noos de oi alla menoina.
ee de dolon tond᾽ allon eni fresi mermeerixe:
steesamenee megan iston eni megaroisin ufaine,
lepton kai perimetron: afar d᾽ eemin meteeipe:
"

kouroi emoi mneesteeres, epei thane dios Odusseus,
mimnet᾽ epeigomenoi ton emon gamon, eis o ke faros
ektelesoh, mee moi metamohnia neemat᾽ oleetai,
Laertee eerohi tafeeion, eis ote ken min
moir᾽ oloee katheleesi taneelegeos thanatoio,
mee tis moi kata deemon Akhaiiadohn nemeseesee.
ai ken ater speirou keitai polla kteatissas.
"

ohs efath᾽, eemin d᾽ aut᾽ epepeitheto thumos ageenohr.
entha kai eematiee men ufainesken megan iston,
nuktas d᾽ alluesken, epei daidas paratheito.
ohs trietes men eleethe doloh kai epeithen Akhaious:
all᾽ ote tetraton eelthen etos kai epeeluthon ohrai,
kai tote dee tis eeipe gunaikohn, ee safa eedee,
kai teen g᾽ alluousan efeuromen aglaon iston.
ohs to men exetelesse kai ouk ethelous᾽ up᾽ anagkees:
soi d᾽ ohde mneesteeres upokrinontai, in᾽ eidees
autos soh thumoh, eidohsi de pantes Akhaioi:
meetera seen apopempson, anohkhthi de min gameesthai
toh oteoh te pateer keletai kai andanei autee.
ei d᾽ et᾽ anieesei ge polun khronon uias Akhaiohn,
ta froneous᾽ ana thumon, o oi peri dohken Atheenee
erga t᾽ epistasthai perikallea kai frenas esthlas
kerdea th᾽, oi᾽ ou poh tin᾽ akouomen oude palaiohn,
taohn ai paros eesan euplokamides Akhaiai,
Turoh t᾽ Alkmeenee te eustefanos te Mukeenee:
taohn ou tis omoia noeemata Peenelopeiee
eedee: atar men touto g᾽ enaisimon ouk enoeese.
tofra gar oun bioton te teon kai kteemat᾽ edontai,
ofra ke keinee touton ekhee noon, on tina oi nun
en steethessi titheisi theoi. mega men kleos autee
poieit᾽, autar soi ge potheen poleos biotoio.
eemeis d᾽ out᾽ epi erga paros g᾽ imen oute pee allee,
prin g᾽ auteen geemasthai Akhaiohn oh k᾽ etheleesi.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Antino᾽, ou pohs esti domohn aekousan apohsai
ee m᾽ etekh᾽, ee m᾽ ethrepse: pateer d᾽ emos allothi gaiees,
zohei o g᾽ ee tethneeke: kakon de me poll᾽ apotinein
Ikarioh, ai k᾽ autos ekohn apo meetera pempsoh.
ek gar tou patros kaka peisomai, alla de daimohn
dohsei, epei meeteer stugeras areeset᾽ erinus
oikou aperkhomenee: nemesis de moi ex anthrohpohn
essetai: ohs ou touton egoh pote muthon enipsoh.
umeteros d᾽ ei men thumos nemesizetai autohn,
exite moi megarohn, allas d᾽ alegunete daitas
uma kteemat᾽ edontes ameibomenoi kata oikous.
ei d᾽ umin dokeei tode lohiteron kai ameinon
emmenai, andros enos bioton neepoinon olesthai,
keiret᾽: egoh de theous epibohsomai aien eontas,
ai ke pothi Zeus dohsi palintita erga genesthai.
neepoinoi ken epeita domohn entosthen oloisthe.
"

ohs fato Teelemakhos, toh d᾽ aietoh euruopa Zeus
upsothen ek korufees oreos proeeeke petesthai.
toh d᾽ eohs men r᾽ epetonto meta pnoiees anemoio
pleesioh alleeloisi titainomenoh pterugessin:
all᾽ ote dee messeen agoreen polufeemon ikestheen,
enth᾽ epidineethente tinaxastheen ptera pukna,
es d᾽ ideteen pantohn kefalas, ossonto d᾽ olethron:
drupsamenoh d᾽ onukhessi pareias amfi te deiras
dexioh eeixan dia t᾽ oikia kai polin autohn.
thambeesan d᾽ ornithas, epei idon ofthalmoisin:
ohrmeenan d᾽ ana thumon a per teleesthai emellon.
toisi de kai meteeipe gerohn eerohs Alithersees
Mastoridees: o gar oios omeelikieen ekekasto
ornithas gnohnai kai enaisima mutheesasthai:
o sfin eu froneohn agoreesato kai meteeipe:
"

keklute dee nun meu, Ithakeesioi, otti ken eipoh:
mneesteersin de malista pifauskomenos tade eiroh:
toisin gar mega peema kulindetai: ou gar Odusseus
deen apaneuthe filohn ohn essetai, alla pou eedee
eggus eohn toisdessi fonon kai keera futeuei
pantessin: polesin de kai alloisin kakon estai,
oi nemomesth᾽ Ithakeen eudeielon. alla polu prin
frazohmesth᾽, ohs ken katapausomen: oi de kai autoi
pauesthohn: kai gar sfin afar tode lohion estin.
ou gar apeireetos manteuomai, all᾽ eu eidohs:
kai gar keinoh feemi teleuteetheenai apanta,
ohs oi emutheomeen, ote Ilion eisanebainon
Argeioi, meta de sfin ebee polumeetis Odusseus.
feen kaka polla pathont᾽, olesant᾽ apo pantas etairous,
agnohston pantessin eeikostoh eniautoh
oikad᾽ eleusesthai: ta de dee nun panta teleitai.
"

ton d᾽ aut᾽ Eurumakhos Polubou pais antion eeuda:
"oh geron, ei d᾽ age nun manteueo soisi tekessin
oikad᾽ iohn, mee pou ti kakon paskhohsin opissoh:
tauta d᾽ egoh seo pollon ameinohn manteuesthai.
ornithes de te polloi up᾽ augas eeelioio
foitohs᾽, oude te pantes enaisimoi: autar Odusseus
ohleto teel᾽, ohs kai su katafthisthai sun ekeinoh
ohfeles. ouk an tossa theopropeohn agoreues,
oude ke Teelemakhon kekholohmenon ohd᾽ anieiees,
soh oikoh dohron potidegmenos, ai ke poreesin.
all᾽ ek toi ereoh, to de kai tetelesmenon estai:
ai ke neohteron andra palaia te polla te eidohs
parfamenos epeessin epotrunees khalepainein,
autoh men oi prohton anieeresteron estai,
preexai d᾽ empees ou ti duneesetai eineka tohnde:
soi de, geron, thoheen epitheesomen, een k᾽ eni thumoh
tinohn askhallees: khalepon de toi essetai algos.
Teelemakhoh d᾽ en pasin egohn upotheesomai autos:
meetera een es patros anohgetoh aponeesthai:
oi de gamon teuxousi kai artuneousin eedna
polla mal᾽, ossa eoike filees epi paidos epesthai.
ou gar prin pausesthai oiomai uias Akhaiohn
mneestuos argaleees, epei ou tina deidimen empees,
out᾽ oun Teelemakhon mala per polumuthon eonta,
oute theopropiees empazometh᾽, een su, geraie,
mutheai akraanton, apekhthaneai d᾽ eti mallon.
khreemata d᾽ aute kakohs bebrohsetai, oude pot᾽ isa
essetai, ofra ken ee ge diatribeesin Akhaious
on gamon: eemeis d᾽ au potidegmenoi eemata panta
eineka tees aretees eridainomen, oude met᾽ allas
erkhometh᾽, as epieikes opuiemen estin ekastoh.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Eurumakh᾽ eede kai alloi, osoi mneesteeres agauoi,
tauta men oukh umeas eti lissomai oud᾽ agoreuoh:
eedee gar ta isasi theoi kai pantes Akhaioi.
all᾽ age moi dote neea thoeen kai eikos᾽ etairous,
oi ke moi entha kai entha diapreessohsi keleuthon.
eimi gar es Sparteen te kai es Pulon eemathoenta
noston peusomenos patros deen oikhomenoio,
een tis moi eipeesi brotohn ee ossan akousoh
ek Dios, ee te malista ferei kleos anthrohpoisin:
ei men ken patros bioton kai noston akousoh,
ee t᾽ an, trukhomenos per, eti tlaieen eniauton:
ei de ke tethneeohtos akousoh meed᾽ et᾽ eontos,
nosteesas dee epeita fileen es patrida gaian
seema te oi kheuoh kai epi kterea ktereixoh
polla mal᾽, ossa eoike, kai aneri meetera dohsoh.
"

ee toi o g᾽ ohs eipohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezeto, toisi d᾽ anestee
Mentohr, os r᾽ Oduseeos amumonos eeen etairos,
kai oi iohn en neeusin epetrepen oikon apanta,
peithesthai te geronti kai empeda panta fulassein:
o sfin eu froneohn agoreesato kai meteeipen:
"

keklute dee nun meu, Ithakeesioi, otti ken eipoh:
mee tis eti profrohn aganos kai eepios estoh
skeeptoukhos basileus, meede fresin aisima eidohs,
all᾽ aiei khalepos t᾽ eiee kai aisula rezoi:
ohs ou tis memneetai Odusseeos theioio
laohn oisin anasse, pateer d᾽ ohs eepios eeen.
all᾽ ee toi mneesteeras ageenoras ou ti megairoh
erdein erga biaia kakorrafieesi nooio:
sfas gar parthemenoi kefalas katedousi biaiohs
oikon Odusseeos, ton d᾽ ouketi fasi neesthai.
nun d᾽ alloh deemoh nemesizomai, oion apantes
eesth᾽ aneoh, atar ou ti kathaptomenoi epeessi
paurous mneesteeras katapauete polloi eontes.
"

ton d᾽ Eueenoridees Leiohkritos antion eeuda:
"Mentor atarteere, frenas eelee, poion eeipes
eemeas otrunohn katapauemen. argaleon de
andrasi kai pleonessi makheesasthai peri daiti.
ei per gar k᾽ Oduseus Ithakeesios autos epelthohn
dainumenous kata dohma eon mneesteeras agauous
exelasai megaroio menoineesei᾽ eni thumoh,
ou ken oi kekharoito gunee, mala per khateousa,
elthont᾽, alla ken autou aeikea potmon epispoi,
ei pleonessi makhoito: su d᾽ ou kata moiran eeipes.
all᾽ age, laoi men skidnasth᾽ epi erga ekastos,
toutoh d᾽ otruneei Mentohr odon eed᾽ Alithersees,
oi te oi ex arkhees patrohioi eisin etairoi.
all᾽ oioh, kai deetha katheemenos aggeliaohn
peusetai ein Ithakee, teleei d᾽ odon ou pote tauteen.
"

ohs ar᾽ efohneesen, lusen d᾽ agoreen aipseereen.
oi men ar᾽ eskidnanto ea pros dohmath᾽ ekastos,
mneesteeres d᾽ es dohmat᾽ isan theiou Oduseeos.

Teelemakhos d᾽ apaneuthe kiohn epi thina thalassees,
kheiras nipsamenos poliees alos eukhet᾽ Atheenee:
"kluthi meu, o khthizos theos eeluthes eemeteron doh
kai m᾽ en neei keleusas ep᾽ eeeroeidea ponton
noston peusomenon patros deen oikhomenoio
erkhesthai: ta de panta diatribousin Akhaioi,
mneesteeres de malista kakohs upereenoreontes.
"

ohs efat᾽ eukhomenos, skhedothen de oi eelthen Atheenee,
Mentori eidomenee eemen demas eede kai audeen,
kai min fohneesas᾽ epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

Teelemakh᾽, oud᾽ opithen kakos esseai oud᾽ anoeemohn,
ei dee toi sou patros enestaktai menos eeu,
oios keinos eeen telesai ergon te epos te:
ou toi epeith᾽ aliee odos essetai oud᾽ atelestos.
ei d᾽ ou keinou g᾽ essi gonos kai Peenelopeiees,
ou se g᾽ epeita eolpa teleuteesein, a menoinas.
pauroi gar toi paides omoioi patri pelontai,
oi pleones kakious, pauroi de te patros areious.
all᾽ epei oud᾽ opithen kakos esseai oud᾽ anoeemohn,
oude se pagkhu ge meetis Odusseeos proleloipen,
elpohree toi epeita teleuteesai tade erga.
toh nun mneesteerohn men ea bouleen te noon te
afradeohn, epei ou ti noeemones oude dikaioi:
oude ti isasin thanaton kai keera melainan,
os dee sfi skhedon estin, ep᾽ eemati pantas olesthai.
soi d᾽ odos ouketi deeron apessetai een su menoinas:
toios gar toi etairos egoh patrohios eimi,
os toi neea thoeen steleoh kai am᾽ epsomai autos.
alla su men pros dohmat᾽ iohn mneesteersin omilei,
oplisson t᾽ eeia kai aggesin arson apanta,
oinon en amfiforeusi, kai alfita, muelon androhn,
dermasin en pukinoisin: egoh d᾽ ana deemon etairous
aips᾽ ethelonteeras sullexomai. eisi de neees
pollai en amfialoh Ithakee, neai eede palaiai:
taohn men toi egohn epiopsomai ee tis aristee,
ohka d᾽ efoplissantes eneesomen eurei pontoh.
"

ohs fat᾽ Atheenaiee kouree Dios: oud᾽ ar᾽ eti deen
Teelemakhos paremimnen, epei theou ekluen audeen.
bee d᾽ ienai pros dohma, filon tetieemenos eetor,
eure d᾽ ara mneesteeras ageenoras en megaroisin,
aigas aniemenous sialous th᾽ euontas en aulee.
Antinoos d᾽ ithus gelasas kie Teelemakhoio,
en t᾽ ara oi fu kheiri, epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomaze:
"

Teelemakh᾽ upsagoree, menos askhete, mee ti toi allo
en steethessi kakon meletoh ergon te epos te,
alla moi esthiemen kai pinemen, ohs to paros per.
tauta de toi mala panta teleuteesousin Akhaioi,
neea kai exaitous eretas, ina thasson ikeeai
es Pulon eegatheeen met᾽ agauou patros akoueen.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Antino᾽, ou pohs estin uperfialoisi meth᾽ umin
dainusthai t᾽ akeonta kai eufrainesthai ekeelon.
ee oukh alis ohs to paroithen ekeirete polla kai esthla
kteemat᾽ ema, mneesteeres, egoh d᾽ eti neepios eea;
nun d᾽ ote dee megas eimi kai allohn muthon akouohn
punthanomai, kai dee moi aexetai endothi thumos,
peireesoh, ohs k᾽ ummi kakas epi keeras ieeloh,
eee Pulond᾽ elthohn, ee autou tohd᾽ eni deemoh.
eimi men, oud᾽ aliee odos essetai een agoreuoh,
emporos: ou gar neeos epeebolos oud᾽ eretaohn
gignomai: ohs nu pou ummin eeisato kerdion einai.
"

ee ra, kai ek kheiros kheira spasat᾽ Antinooio
reia: mneesteeres de domon kata daita penonto.
oi d᾽ epelohbeuon kai ekertomeon epeessin.
ohde de tis eipeske neohn upereenoreontohn:
"

ee mala Teelemakhos fonon eemin mermeerizei.
ee tinas ek Pulou axei amuntoras eemathoentos
ee o ge kai Sparteethen, epei nu per ietai ainohs:
eee kai eis Efureen ethelei, pieiran arouran,
elthein, ofr᾽ enthen thumofthora farmak᾽ eneikee,
en de balee kreeteeri kai eemeas pantas olessee.
"

allos d᾽ aut᾽ eipeske neohn upereenoreontohn:
"tis d᾽ oid᾽, ei ke kai autos iohn koilees epi neeos
teele filohn apoleetai alohmenos ohs per Odusseus;
outoh ken kai mallon ofelleien ponon ammin:
kteemata gar ken panta dasaimetha, oikia d᾽ aute
toutou meeteri doimen ekhein eed᾽ os tis opuioi.
"

ohs fan, o d᾽ upsorofon thalamon katebeeseto patros
eurun, othi neetos khrusos kai khalkos ekeito
esthees t᾽ en kheeloisin alis t᾽ euohdes elaion:
en de pithoi oinoio palaiou eedupotoio
estasan, akreeton theion poton entos ekhontes,
exeiees poti toikhon areerotes, ei pot᾽ Odusseus
oikade nosteeseie kai algea polla mogeesas.
kleeistai d᾽ epesan sanides pukinohs araruiai,
diklides: en de gunee tamiee nuktas te kai eemar
eskh᾽, ee pant᾽ efulasse noou poluidreieesin,
Euruklei᾽, Ohpos thugateer Peiseenoridao.
teen tote Teelemakhos prosefee thalamonde kalessas:
"

mai᾽, age dee moi oinon en amfiforeusin afusson
eedun, otis meta ton larohtatos on su fulasseis
keinon oiomenee ton kammoron, ei pothen elthoi
diogenees Oduseus thanaton kai keeras aluxas.
dohdeka d᾽ empleeson kai pohmasin arson apantas.
en de moi alfita kheuon eurrafeessi doroisin:
eikosi d᾽ estoh metra muleefatou alfitou aktees.
autee d᾽ oiee isthi: ta d᾽ athroa panta tetukhthoh:
esperios gar egohn aireesomai, oppote ken dee
meeteer eis uperoh᾽ anabee koitou te medeetai.
eimi gar es Sparteen te kai es Pulon eemathoenta
noston peusomenos patros filou, een pou akousoh.
"

ohs fato, kohkusen de filee trofos Eurukleia,
kai r᾽ olofuromenee epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"tipte de toi, file teknon, eni fresi touto noeema
epleto; pee d᾽ etheleis ienai polleen epi gaian
mounos eohn agapeetos; o d᾽ ohleto teelothi patrees
diogenees Oduseus allognohtoh eni deemoh.
oi de toi autik᾽ ionti kaka frassontai opissoh,
ohs ke doloh fthiees, tade d᾽ autoi panta dasontai.
alla men᾽ auth᾽ epi soisi katheemenos: oude ti se khree
ponton ep᾽ atrugeton kaka paskhein oud᾽ alaleesthai.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"tharsei, mai᾽, epei ou toi aneu theou eede ge boulee.
all᾽ omoson mee meetri filee tade mutheesasthai,
prin g᾽ ot᾽ an endekatee te duohdekatee te geneetai,
ee auteen pothesai kai aformeethentos akousai,
ohs an mee klaiousa kata khroa kalon iaptee.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, greeus de theohn megan orkon apohmnu.
autar epei r᾽ omosen te teleuteesen te ton orkon,
autik᾽ epeita oi oinon en amfiforeusin afussen,
en de oi alfita kheuen eurrafeessi doroisi.
Teelemakhos d᾽ es dohmat᾽ iohn mneesteersin omilei.

enth᾽ aut᾽ all᾽ enoeese thea, glaukohpis Atheenee.
Teelemakhoh eikuia kata ptolin ohkheto pantee,
kai ra ekastoh fohti paristamenee fato muthon,
esperious d᾽ epi neea thoeen ageresthai anohgei.
ee d᾽ aute Fronioio Noeemona faidimon uion
eetee neea thoeen: o de oi profrohn upedekto.

duseto t᾽ eeelios skioohnto te pasai aguiai,
kai tote neea thoeen alad᾽ eiruse, panta d᾽ en autee
opl᾽ etithei, ta te neees eusselmoi foreousi.
steese d᾽ ep᾽ eskhatiee limenos, peri d᾽ esthloi etairoi
athrooi eegerethonto: thea d᾽ ohtrunen ekaston.

enth᾽ aut᾽ all᾽ enoeese thea, glaukohpis Atheenee.
bee r᾽ ienai pros dohmat᾽ Odusseeos theioio:
entha mneesteeressin epi glukun upnon ekheue,
plaze de pinontas, kheirohn d᾽ ekballe kupella.
oi d᾽ eudein ohrnunto kata ptolin, oud᾽ ar᾽ eti deen
eeat᾽, epei sfisin upnos epi blefaroisin epipten.
autar Teelemakhon prosefee glaukohpis Atheenee
ekprokalessamenee megarohn eu naietaontohn,
Mentori eidomenee eemen demas eede kai audeen:
"

Teelemakh᾽, eedee men toi eukneemides etairoi
eeat᾽ epeeretmoi teen seen potidegmenoi ormeen:
all᾽ iomen, mee deetha diatribohmen odoio.
"

ohs ara fohneesas᾽ eegeesato Pallas Atheenee
karpalimohs: o d᾽ epeita met᾽ ikhnia baine theoio.
autar epei r᾽ epi neea kateeluthon eede thalassan,
euron epeit᾽ epi thini karee komoohntas etairous.
toisi de kai meteeif᾽ ieree is Teelemakhoio:
"

deute, filoi, eeia ferohmetha: panta gar eedee
athro᾽ eni megaroh. meeteer d᾽ emee ou ti pepustai,
oud᾽ allai dmohai, mia d᾽ oiee muthon akousen.
"

ohs ara fohneesas eegeesato, toi d᾽ am᾽ eponto.
oi d᾽ ara panta ferontes eusselmoh epi neei
katthesan, ohs ekeleusen Odusseeos filos uios.
an d᾽ ara Teelemakhos neeos bain᾽, eerkhe d᾽ Atheenee,
neei d᾽ eni prumnee kat᾽ ar᾽ ezeto: agkhi d᾽ ar᾽ autees
ezeto Teelemakhos. toi de prumneesi᾽ elusan,
an de kai autoi bantes epi kleeisi kathizon.
toisin d᾽ ikmenon ouron iei glaukohpis Atheenee,
akraee Zefuron, keladont᾽ epi oinopa ponton.
Teelemakhos d᾽ etaroisin epotrunas ekeleusen
oplohn aptesthai: toi d᾽ otrunontos akousan.
iston d᾽ eilatinon koilees entosthe mesodmees
steesan aeirantes, kata de protonoisin edeesan,
elkon d᾽ istia leuka eustreptoisi boeusin.
epreesen d᾽ anemos meson istion, amfi de kuma
steiree porfureon megal᾽ iakhe neeos iousees:
ee d᾽ etheen kata kuma diapreessousa keleuthon.
deesamenoi d᾽ ara opla thoeen ana neea melainan
steesanto kreeteeras epistefeas oinoio,
leibon d᾽ athanatoisi theois aieigeneteesin,
ek pantohn de malista Dios glaukohpidi kouree.
pannukhiee men r᾽ ee ge kai eeoh peire keleuthon.


Book 3
------

Eeelios d᾽ anorouse, lipohn perikallea limneen,
ouranon es polukhalkon, in᾽ athanatoisi faeinoi
kai thneetoisi brotoisin epi zeidohron arouran:
oi de Pulon, Neeleeos euktimenon ptoliethron,
ixon: toi d᾽ epi thini thalassees iera rezon,
taurous pammelanas, enosikhthoni kuanokhaitee.
ennea d᾽ edrai esan, pentakosioi d᾽ en ekastee
eeato kai proukhonto ekastothi ennea taurous.
euth᾽ oi splagkhna pasanto, theoh d᾽ epi meeri᾽ ekaion,
oi d᾽ ithus katagonto id᾽ istia neeos eisees
steilan aeirantes, teen d᾽ ohrmisan, ek d᾽ eban autoi:
ek d᾽ ara Teelemakhos neeos bain᾽, eerkhe d᾽ Atheenee.
ton proteree proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"

Teelemakh᾽, ou men se khree et᾽ aidous, oud᾽ eebaion:
touneka gar kai ponton epeplohs, ofra putheeai
patros, opou kuthe gaia kai on tina potmon epespen.
all᾽ age nun ithus kie Nestoros ippodamoio:
eidomen een tina meetin eni steethessi kekeuthe.
lissesthai de min autos, opohs neemertea eipee:
pseudos d᾽ ouk ereei: mala gar pepnumenos esti.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Mentor, pohs t᾽ ar᾽ ioh; pohs t᾽ ar prosptuxomai auton;
oude ti poh muthoisi pepeireemai pukinoisin:
aidohs d᾽ au neon andra geraiteron exereesthai.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"Teelemakh᾽, alla men autos eni fresi seesi noeeseis,
alla de kai daimohn upotheesetai: ou gar oioh
ou se theohn aekeeti genesthai te trafemen te.
"

ohs ara fohneesas᾽ eegeesato Pallas Atheenee
karpalimohs: o d᾽ epeita met᾽ ikhnia baine theoio.
ixon d᾽ es Puliohn androhn agurin te kai edras,
enth᾽ ara Nestohr eesto sun uiasin, amfi d᾽ etairoi
dait᾽ entunomenoi krea t᾽ ohptohn alla t᾽ epeiron.
oi d᾽ ohs oun xeinous idon, athrooi eelthon apantes,
khersin t᾽ eespazonto kai edriaasthai anohgon.
prohtos Nestoridees Peisistratos egguthen elthohn
amfoterohn ele kheira kai idrusen para daiti
kohesin en malakoisin epi psamathois alieesin
par te kasigneetoh Thrasumeedei kai pateri oh:
dohke d᾽ ara splagkhnohn moiras, en d᾽ oinon ekheuen
khruseioh depai: deidiskomenos de proseeuda
Pallad᾽ Atheenaieen koureen Dios aigiokhoio:
"

eukheo nun, oh xeine, Poseidaohni anakti:
tou gar kai daitees eenteesate deuro molontes.
autar epeen speisees te kai euxeai, ee themis esti,
dos kai toutoh epeita depas melieedeos oinou
speisai, epei kai touton oiomai athanatoisin
eukhesthai: pantes de theohn khateous᾽ anthrohpoi.
alla neohteros estin, omeelikiee d᾽ emoi autoh:
touneka soi proteroh dohsoh khruseion aleison.
"

ohs eipohn en kheiri tithei depas eedeos oinou:
khaire d᾽ Atheenaiee pepnumenoh andri dikaioh,
ouneka oi proteree dohke khruseion aleison:
autika d᾽ eukheto polla Poseidaohni anakti:
"

kluthi, Poseidaon gaieeokhe, meede megeerees
eemin eukhomenoisi teleuteesai tade erga.
Nestori men prohtista kai uiasi kudos opaze,
autar epeit᾽ alloisi didou khariessan amoibeen
sumpasin Pulioisin agakleitees ekatombees.
dos d᾽ eti Teelemakhon kai eme preexanta neesthai,
ouneka deur᾽ ikomestha thoee sun neei melainee.
"

ohs ar᾽ epeit᾽ eerato kai autee panta teleuta.
dohke de Teelemakhoh kalon depas amfikupellon:
ohs d᾽ autohs eerato Odusseeos filos uios.
oi d᾽ epei ohpteesan kre᾽ upertera kai erusanto,
moiras dassamenoi dainunt᾽ erikudea daita.
autar epei posios kai edeetuos ex eron ento,
tois ara muthohn eerkhe Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"

nun dee kallion esti metalleesai kai eresthai
xeinous, oi tines eisin, epei tarpeesan edohdees.
oh xeinoi, tines este; pothen pleith᾽ ugra keleutha;
ee ti kata preexin ee mapsidiohs alaleesthe
oia te leeisteeres upeir ala, toi t᾽ aloohntai
psukhas parthemenoi kakon allodapoisi perontes;
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda
tharseesas: autee gar eni fresi tharsos Atheenee
theekh᾽, ina min peri patros apoikhomenoio eroito
eed᾽ ina min kleos esthlon en anthrohpoisin ekheesin:
"

oh Nestor Neeleeiadee, mega kudos Akhaiohn,
eireai oppothen eimen: egoh de ke toi katalexoh.
eemeis ex Ithakees uponeeiou eileelouthmen:
preexis d᾽ eed᾽ idiee, ou deemios, een agoreuoh.
patros emou kleos euru meterkhomai, een pou akousoh,
diou Odusseeos talasifronos, on pote fasi
sun soi marnamenon Trohohn polin exalapaxai.
allous men gar pantas, osoi Trohsin polemixon,
peuthometh᾽, eekhi ekastos apohleto lugroh olethroh,
keinou d᾽ au kai olethron apeuthea theeke Kroniohn.
ou gar tis dunatai safa eipemen oppoth᾽ olohlen,
eith᾽ o g᾽ ep᾽ eepeirou damee andrasi dusmeneessin,
eite kai en pelagei meta kumasin Amfitritees.
touneka nun ta sa gounath᾽ ikanomai, ai k᾽ etheleestha
keinou lugron olethron enispein, ei pou opohpas
ofthalmoisi teoisin ee allou muthon akousas
plazomenou: peri gar min oizuron teke meeteer.
meede ti m᾽ aidomenos meilisseo meed᾽ eleairohn,
all᾽ eu moi katalexon opohs eenteesas opohpees.
lissomai, ei pote toi ti pateer emos, esthlos Odusseus,
ee epos eee ti ergon upostas exetelesse
deemoh eni Trohohn, othi paskhete peemat᾽ Akhaioi,
tohn nun moi mneesai, kai moi neemertes enispes.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"oh fil᾽, epei m᾽ emneesas oizuos, een en ekeinoh
deemoh anetleemen menos askhetoi uies Akhaiohn,
eemen osa xun neeusin ep᾽ eeeroeidea ponton
plazomenoi kata leeid᾽, opee arxeien Akhilleus,
eed᾽ osa kai peri astu mega Priamoio anaktos
marnameth᾽: entha d᾽ epeita katektathen ossoi aristoi.
entha men Aias keitai areeios, entha d᾽ Akhilleus,
entha de Patroklos, theofin meestohr atalantos,
entha d᾽ emos filos uios, ama krateros kai amumohn,
Antilokhos, peri men theiein takhus eede makheetees:
alla te poll᾽ epi tois pathomen kaka: tis ken ekeina
panta ge mutheesaito katathneetohn anthrohpohn;
oud᾽ ei pentaetes ge kai exaetes paramimnohn
exereois osa keithi pathon kaka dioi Akhaioi:
prin ken anieetheis seen patrida gaian ikoio.
einaetes gar sfin kaka raptomen amfiepontes
pantoioisi doloisi, mogis d᾽ etelesse Kroniohn.
enth᾽ ou tis pote meetin omoiohtheemenai anteen
eethel᾽, epei mala pollon enika dios Odusseus
pantoioisi doloisi, pateer teos, ei eteon ge
keinou ekgonos essi: sebas m᾽ ekhei eisoroohnta.
ee toi gar muthoi ge eoikotes, oude ke faiees
andra neohteron ohde eoikota mutheesasthai.
enth᾽ ee toi eeos men egoh kai dios Odusseus
oute pot᾽ ein agoree dikh᾽ ebazomen out᾽ eni boulee,
all᾽ ena thumon ekhonte nooh kai epifroni boulee
frazometh᾽ Argeioisin opohs okh᾽ arista genoito.
autar epei Priamoio polin diepersamen aipeen,
beemen d᾽ en neeessi, theos d᾽ eskedassen Akhaious,
kai tote dee Zeus lugron eni fresi meedeto noston
Argeiois, epei ou ti noeemones oude dikaioi
pantes esan: toh sfeohn polees kakon oiton epespon
meenios ex oloees glaukohpidos obrimopatrees.
ee t᾽ erin Atreideesi met᾽ amfoteroisin etheeke.
toh de kalessamenoh agoreen es pantas Akhaious,
maps, atar ou kata kosmon, es eeelion katadunta,
oi eelthon oinoh bebareeotes uies Akhaiohn,
muthon mutheistheen, tou eineka laon ageiran.
enth᾽ ee toi Menelaos anohgei pantas Akhaious
nostou mimneeskesthai ep᾽ eurea nohta thalassees,
oud᾽ Agamemnoni pampan eeendane: bouleto gar ra
laon erukakeein rexai th᾽ ieras ekatombas,
ohs ton Atheenaiees deinon kholon exakesaito,
neepios, oude to eedee, o ou peisesthai emellen:
ou gar t᾽ aipsa theohn trepetai noos aien eontohn.
ohs toh men khalepoisin ameibomenoh epeessin
estasan: oi d᾽ anorousan eukneemides Akhaioi
eekhee thespesiee, dikha de sfisin eendane boulee.
nukta men aesamen khalepa fresin ormainontes
alleelois: epi gar Zeus eertue peema kakoio:
eeohthen d᾽ oi men neas elkomen eis ala dian
kteemata t᾽ entithemestha bathuzohnous te gunaikas.
eemisees d᾽ ara laoi ereetuonto menontes
authi par᾽ Atreidee Agamemnoni, poimeni laohn:
eemisees d᾽ anabantes elaunomen: ai de mal᾽ ohka
epleon, estoresen de theos megakeetea ponton.
es Tenedon d᾽ elthontes erexamen ira theois῀n,
oikade iemenoi: Zeus d᾽ ou poh meedeto noston,
skhetlios, os r᾽ erin ohrse kakeen epi deuteron autis.
oi men apostrepsantes eban neas amfielissas
amf᾽ Oduseea anakta daifrona, poikilomeeteen,
autis ep᾽ Atreidee Agamemnoni eera ferontes:
autar egoh sun neeusin aollesin, ai moi eponto,
feugon, epei gignohskon, odee kaka meedeto daimohn.
feuge de Tudeos uios areeios, ohrse d᾽ etairous.
opse de dee meta nohi kie xanthos Menelaos,
en Lesboh d᾽ ekikhen dolikhon ploon ormainontas,
ee kathuperthe Khioio neoimetha paipaloessees,
neesou epi Psuriees, auteen ep᾽ arister᾽ ekhontes,
ee upenerthe Khioio, par᾽ eenemoenta Mimanta.
eeteomen de theon feenai teras: autar o g᾽ eemin
deixe, kai eenohgei pelagos meson eis Euboian
temnein, ofra takhista upek kakoteeta fugoimen.
ohrto d᾽ epi ligus ouros aeemenai: ai de mal᾽ ohka
ikhthuoenta keleutha diedramon, es de Geraiston
ennukhiai katagonto: Poseidaohni de taurohn
poll᾽ epi meer᾽ ethemen, pelagos mega metreesantes.
tetraton eemar eeen, ot᾽ en Argei neeas eisas
Tudeideoh etaroi Diomeedeos ippodamoio
istasan: autar egoh ge Pulond᾽ ekhon, oude pot᾽ esbee
ouros, epei dee prohta theos proeeeken aeenai.

ohs eelthon, file teknon, apeuthees, oude ti oida
keinohn, oi t᾽ esaohthen Akhaiohn oi t᾽ apolonto.
ossa d᾽ eni megaroisi katheemenos eemeteroisi
peuthomai, ee themis esti, daeeseai, koude se deusoh.
eu men Murmidonas fas᾽ elthemen egkhesimohrous,
ous ag᾽ Akhilleeos megathumou faidimos uios,
eu de Filokteeteen, Poiantion aglaon uion.
pantas d᾽ Idomeneus Kreeteen eiseegag᾽ etairous,
oi fugon ek polemou, pontos de oi ou tin᾽ apeeura.
Atreideen de kai autoi akouete, nosfin eontes,
ohs t᾽ eelth᾽, ohs t᾽ Aigisthos emeesato lugron olethron.
all᾽ ee toi keinos men epismugerohs apetisen:
ohs agathon kai paida katafthimenoio lipesthai
andros, epei kai keinos etisato patrofoneea,
Aigisthon dolomeetin, o oi patera kluton ekta.
kai su filos, mala gar s᾽ orooh kalon te megan te,
alkimos ess᾽, ina tis se kai opsigonohn eu eipee.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"oh Nestor Neeleeiadee, mega kudos Akhaiohn,
kai lieen keinos men etisato, kai oi Akhaioi
oisousi kleos euru kai essomenoisi puthesthai:
ai gar emoi tosseende theoi dunamin peritheien,
tisasthai mneesteeras uperbasiees alegeinees,
oi te moi ubrizontes atasthala meekhanoohntai.
all᾽ ou moi toiouton epeklohsan theoi olbon,
patri t᾽ emoh kai emoi: nun de khree tetlamen empees.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"oh fil᾽, epei dee tauta m᾽ anemneesas kai eeipes,
fasi mneesteeras sees meeteros eineka pollous
en megarois aekeeti sethen kaka meekhanaasthai:
eipe moi, eee ekohn upodamnasai, ee se ge laoi
ekhthairous᾽ ana deemon, epispomenoi theou omfee.
tis d᾽ oid᾽ ei ke pote sfi bias apotisetai elthohn,
ee o ge mounos eohn ee kai sumpantes Akhaioi;
ei gar s᾽ ohs etheloi fileein glaukohpis Atheenee,
ohs tot᾽ Odusseeos perikeedeto kudalimoio
deemoh eni Trohohn, othi paskhomen alge᾽ Akhaioi--
ou gar poh idon ohde theous anafanda fileuntas,
ohs keinoh anafanda paristato Pallas Atheenee--
ei s᾽ outohs etheloi fileein keedoito te thumoh,
toh ken tis keinohn ge kai eklelathoito gamoio.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"oh geron, ou poh touto epos teleesthai oioh:
lieen gar mega eipes: agee m᾽ ekhei. ouk an emoi ge
elpomenoh ta genoit᾽, oud᾽ ei theoi ohs etheloien.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"Teelemakhe, poion se epos fugen erkos odontohn.
reia theos g᾽ ethelohn kai teelothen andra saohsai.
bouloimeen d᾽ an egoh ge kai algea polla mogeesas
oikade t᾽ elthemenai kai nostimon eemar idesthai,
ee elthohn apolesthai efestios, ohs Agamemnohn
ohleth᾽ up᾽ Aigisthoio doloh kai ees alokhoio.
all᾽ ee toi thanaton men omoiion oude theoi per
kai filoh andri dunantai alalkemen, oppote ken dee
moir᾽ oloee katheleesi taneelegeos thanatoio.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Mentor, meeketi tauta legohmetha keedomenoi per:
keinoh d᾽ ouketi nostos eteetumos, alla oi eedee
frassant᾽ athanatoi thanaton kai keera melainan.
nun d᾽ etheloh epos allo metalleesai kai eresthai
Nestor᾽, epei peri oide dikas eede fronin allohn:
tris gar dee min fasin anaxasthai gene᾽ androhn:
ohs te moi athanatos indalletai eisoraasthai.
oh Nestor Neeleeiadee, su d᾽ aleethes enispes:
pohs ethan᾽ Atreidees euru kreiohn Agamemnohn;
pou Menelaos eeen; tina d᾽ autoh meesat᾽ olethron
Aigisthos dolomeetis, epei ktane pollon areioh;
ee ouk Argeos eeen Akhaiikou, alla pee allee
plazet᾽ ep᾽ anthrohpous, o de tharseesas katepefne;
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"toigar egoh toi, teknon, aleethea pant᾽ agoreusoh.
ee toi men tade kautos oieai, ohs ken etukhthee,
ei zohon g᾽ Aigisthon eni megaroisin etetmen
Atreidees Troieethen iohn, xanthos Menelaos:
toh ke oi oude thanonti khuteen epi gaian ekheuan,
all᾽ ara ton ge kunes te kai oiohnoi katedapsan
keimenon en pedioh ekas asteos, oude ke tis min
klausen Akhaiiadohn: mala gar mega meesato ergon.
eemeis men gar keithi poleas teleontes aethlous
eemeth᾽: o d᾽ eukeelos mukhoh Argeos ippobotoio
poll᾽ Agamemnoneeen alokhon thelgesk᾽ epeessin.
ee d᾽ ee toi to prin men anaineto ergon aeikes
dia Klutaimneestree: fresi gar kekhreet᾽ agatheesi:
par d᾽ ar᾽ eeen kai aoidos aneer, oh poll᾽ epetellen
Atreidees Troieende kiohn erusasthai akoitin.
all᾽ ote dee min moira theohn epedeese dameenai,
dee tote ton men aoidon agohn es neeson ereemeen
kallipen oiohnoisin elohr kai kurma genesthai,
teen d᾽ ethelohn ethelousan aneegagen onde domonde.
polla de meeri᾽ ekeee theohn ierois epi bohmois,
polla d᾽ agalmat᾽ aneepsen, ufasmata te khruson te,
ektelesas mega ergon, o ou pote elpeto thumoh.

eemeis men gar ama pleomen Troieethen iontes,
Atreidees kai egoh, fila eidotes alleeloisin:
all᾽ ote Sounion iron afikometh᾽, akron Atheeneohn,
entha kuberneeteen Menelaou Foibos Apollohn
ois aganois beleessin epoikhomenos katepefne,
peedalion meta khersi theousees neeos ekhonta,
Frontin Oneetorideen, os ekainuto ful᾽ anthrohpohn
neea kuberneesai, opote sperkhoien aellai.
ohs o men entha kateskhet᾽, epeigomenos per odoio,
ofr᾽ etaron thaptoi kai epi kterea kteriseien.
all᾽ ote dee kai keinos iohn epi oinopa ponton
en neeusi glafureesi Maleiaohn oros aipu
ixe theohn, tote dee stugereen odon euruopa Zeus
efrasato, ligeohn d᾽ anemohn ep᾽ autmena kheue,
kumata te trofeonto pelohria, isa oressin.
entha diatmeexas tas men Kreetee epelassen,
eekhi Kudohnes enaion Iardanou amfi reethra.
esti de tis lissee aipeia te eis ala petree
eskhatiee Gortunos en eeeroeidei pontoh:
entha Notos mega kuma poti skaion rion ohthei,
es Faiston, mikros de lithos mega kum᾽ apoergei.
ai men ar᾽ enth᾽ eelthon, spoudee d᾽ eeluxan olethron
andres, atar neeas ge poti spiladessin eaxan
kumat᾽: atar tas pente neas kuanoprohreious
Aiguptoh epelasse ferohn anemos te kai udohr.
ohs o men entha polun bioton kai khruson ageirohn
eelato xun neeusi kat᾽ allothroous anthrohpous:
tofra de taut᾽ Aigisthos emeesato oikothi lugra.
eptaetes d᾽ eenasse polukhrusoio Mukeenees,
kteinas Atreideen, dedmeeto de laos up᾽ autoh.
toh de oi ogdoatoh kakon eeluthe dios Orestees
aps ap᾽ Atheenaohn, kata d᾽ ektane patrofoneea,
Aigisthon dolomeetin, o oi patera kluton ekta.
ee toi o ton kteinas dainu tafon Argeioisin
meetros te stugerees kai analkidos Aigisthoio:
auteemar de oi eelthe boeen agathos Menelaos
polla kteemat᾽ agohn, osa oi nees akhthos aeiran.

kai su, filos, mee deetha domohn apo teel᾽ alaleeso,
kteemata te prolipohn andras t᾽ en soisi domoisin
outoh uperfialous, mee toi kata panta fagohsin
kteemata dassamenoi, su de teeusieen odon elthees.
all᾽ es men Menelaon egoh kelomai kai anohga
elthein: keinos gar neon allothen eileelouthen,
ek tohn anthrohpohn, othen ouk elpoito ge thumoh
elthemen, on tina prohton aposfeelohsin aellai
es pelagos mega toion, othen te per oud᾽ oiohnoi
autoetes oikhneusin, epei mega te deinon te.
all᾽ ithi nun sun neei te see kai sois etaroisin:
ei d᾽ etheleis pezos, para toi difros te kai ippoi,
par de toi uies emoi, oi toi pompeees esontai
es Lakedaimona dian, othi xanthos Menelaos.
lissesthai de min autos, ina neemertes enispee:
pseudos d᾽ ouk ereei: mala gar pepnumenos estin.
"

ohs efat᾽, eeelios d᾽ ar᾽ edu kai epi knefas eelthe.
toisi de kai meteeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"oh geron, ee toi tauta kata moiran katelexas:
all᾽ age tamnete men glohssas, keraasthe de oinon,
ofra Poseidaohni kai allois athanatoisin
speisantes koitoio medohmetha: toio gar ohree.
eedee gar faos oikheth᾽ upo zofon, oude eoiken:
deetha theohn en daiti thaassemen, alla neesthai.
"

ee ra Dios thugateer, oi d᾽ ekluon audeesasees.
toisi de keerukes men udohr epi kheiras ekheuan,
kouroi de kreeteeras epestepsanto potoio,
nohmeesan d᾽ ara pasin eparxamenoi depaessi:
glohssas d᾽ en puri ballon, anistamenoi d᾽ epeleibon.
autar epei speisan t᾽ epion th᾽, oson eethele thumos,
dee tot᾽ Atheenaiee kai Teelemakhos theoeidees
amfoh iestheen koileen epi neea neesthai.
Nestohr d᾽ au kateruke kathaptomenos epeessin:
"

Zeus to g᾽ alexeeseie kai athanatoi theoi alloi,
ohs umeis par᾽ emeio thoeen epi neea kioite
ohs te teu ee para pampan aneimonos eede penikhrou,
oh ou ti khlainai kai reegea poll᾽ eni oikoh,
out᾽ autoh malakohs oute xeinoisin eneudein.
autar emoi para men khlainai kai reegea kala.
ou theen dee toud᾽ andros Odusseeos filos uios
neeos ep᾽ ikriofin katalexetai, ofr᾽ an egoh ge
zohoh, epeita de paides eni megaroisi lipohntai,
xeinous xeinizein, os tis k᾽ ema dohmath᾽ ikeetai.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea, glaukohpis Atheenee:
"eu dee tauta g᾽ efeestha, geron file: soi de eoiken
Teelemakhon peithesthai, epei polu kallion outohs.
all᾽ outos men nun soi am᾽ epsetai, ofra ken eudee
soisin eni megaroisin: egoh d᾽ epi neea melainan
eim᾽, ina tharsunoh th᾽ etarous eipoh te ekasta.
oios gar meta toisi geraiteros eukhomai einai:
oi d᾽ alloi filoteeti neohteroi andres epontai,
pantes omeelikiee megathumou Teelemakhoio.
entha ke lexaimeen koilee para neei melainee
nun: atar eeohthen meta Kaukohnas megathumous
eim᾽ entha khreios moi ofelletai, ou ti neon ge
oud᾽ oligon. su de touton, epei teon iketo dohma,
pempson sun difroh te kai uiei: dos de oi ippous,
oi toi elafrotatoi theiein kai kartos aristoi.
"

ohs ara fohneesas᾽ apebee glaukohpis Atheenee
feenee eidomenee: thambos d᾽ ele pantas idontas.
thaumazen d᾽ o geraios, opohs iden ofthalmois:
Teelemakhou d᾽ ele kheira, epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomazen:
"

oh filos, ou se eolpa kakon kai analkin esesthai,
ei dee toi neoh ohde theoi pompeees epontai.
ou men gar tis od᾽ allos Olumpia dohmat᾽ ekhontohn,
alla Dios thugateer, kudistee Tritogeneia,
ee toi kai pater᾽ esthlon en Argeioisin etima.
alla anass᾽ ileethi, didohthi de moi kleos esthlon,
autoh kai paidessi kai aidoiee parakoiti:
soi d᾽ au egoh rexoh boun eenin eurumetohpon
admeeteen, een ou poh upo zugon eegagen aneer:
teen toi egoh rexoh khruson kerasin perikheuas.
"

ohs efat᾽ eukhomenos, tou d᾽ eklue Pallas Atheenee.
toisin d᾽ eegemoneue Gereenios ippota Nestohr,
uiasi kai gambroisin, ea pros dohmata kala.
all᾽ ote dohmath᾽ ikonto agakluta toio anaktos,
exeiees ezonto kata klismous te thronous te:
tois d᾽ o gerohn elthousin ana kreeteera kerassen
oinou eedupotoio, ton endekatoh eniautoh
ohixen tamiee kai apo kreedemnon eluse:
tou o gerohn kreeteera kerassato, polla d᾽ Atheenee
eukhet᾽ apospendohn, kouree Dios aigiokhoio.

autar epei speisan t᾽ epion th᾽, oson eethele thumos,
oi men kakkeiontes eban oikonde ekastos,
ton d᾽ autou koimeese Gereenios ippota Nestohr,
Teelemakhon, filon uion Odusseeos theioio,
treetois en lekheessin up᾽ aithousee eridoupoh,
par᾽ d᾽ ar᾽ eummelieen Peisistraton, orkhamon androhn,
os oi et᾽ eeitheos paidohn een en megaroisin:
autos d᾽ aute katheude mukhoh domou upseeloio,
toh d᾽ alokhos despoina lekhos porsune kai euneen.

eemos d᾽ eerigeneia fanee rododaktulos Eeohs,
ohrnut᾽ ar᾽ ex euneefi Gereenios ippota Nestohr,
ek d᾽ elthohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezet᾽ epi xestoisi lithoisin,
oi oi esan proparoithe thuraohn upseelaohn,
leukoi, apostilbontes aleifatos: ois epi men prin
Neeleus izesken, theofin meestohr atalantos:
all᾽ o men eedee keeri dameis Aidosde bebeekei,
Nestohr au tot᾽ efize Gereenios, ouros Akhaiohn,
skeeptron ekhohn. peri d᾽ uies aollees eegerethonto
ek thalamohn elthontes, Ekhefrohn te Stratios te
Perseus t᾽ Areetos te kai antitheos Thrasumeedees.
toisi d᾽ epeith᾽ ektos Peisistratos eeluthen eerohs,
par d᾽ ara Teelemakhon theoeikelon eisan agontes.
toisi de muthohn eerkhe Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"

karpalimohs moi, tekna fila, kreeeenat᾽ eeldohr,
ofr᾽ ee toi prohtista theohn ilassom᾽ Atheeneen,
ee moi enargees eelthe theou es daita thaleian.
all᾽ ag᾽ o men pediond᾽ epi boun, itoh, ofra takhista
eltheesin, elasee de boohn epiboukolos aneer:
eis d᾽ epi Teelemakhou megathumou neea melainan
pantas iohn etarous agetoh, lipetoh de du᾽ oious:
eis d᾽ au khrusokhoon Laerkea deuro kelesthoh
elthein, ofra boos khruson kerasin perikheuee.
oi d᾽ alloi menet᾽ autou aollees, eipate d᾽ eisoh
dmoheesin kata dohmat᾽ agakluta daita penesthai,
edras te xula t᾽ amfi kai aglaon oisemen udohr.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes epoipnuon. eelthe men ar bous
ek pediou, eelthon de thoees para neeos eisees
Teelemakhou etaroi megaleetoros, eelthe de khalkeus
opl᾽ en khersin ekhohn khalkeeia, peirata tekhnees,
akmona te sfuran t᾽ eupoieeton te puragreen,
oisin te khruson eirgaxeto: eelthe d᾽ Atheenee
irohn antioohsa. gerohn d᾽ ippeelata Nestohr
khruson edohkh᾽: o d᾽ epeita boos kerasin perikheuen
askeesas, in᾽ agalma thea kekharoito idousa.
boun d᾽ ageteen keraohn Stratios kai dios Ekhefrohn.
kherniba de sf᾽ Areetos en anthemoenti lebeeti
eeluthen ek thalamoio ferohn, eteree d᾽ ekhen oulas
en kaneoh pelekun de meneptolemos Thrasumeedees
oxun ekhohn en kheiri paristato boun epikopsohn.
Perseus d᾽ amnion eikhe: gerohn d᾽ ippeelata Nestohr
kherniba t᾽ oulokhutas te kateerkheto, polla d᾽ Atheenee
eukhet᾽ aparkhomenos, kefalees trikhas en puri ballohn.

autar epei r᾽ euxanto kai oulokhutas probalonto,
autika Nestoros uios uperthumos Thrasumeedees
eelasen agkhi stas: pelekus d᾽ apekopse tenontas
aukhenious, lusen de boos menos. ai d᾽ ololuxan
thugateres te nuoi te kai aidoiee parakoitis
Nestoros, Eurudikee, presba Klumenoio thugatrohn.
oi men epeit᾽ anelontes apo khthonos euruodeiees
eskhon: atar sfaxen Peisistratos, orkhamos androhn.
tees d᾽ epei ek melan aima ruee, lipe d᾽ ostea thumos,
aips᾽ ara min diekheuan, afar d᾽ ek meeria tamnon
panta kata moiran, kata te knisee ekalupsan
diptukha poieesantes, ep᾽ autohn d᾽ ohmotheteesan.
kaie d᾽ epi skhizees o gerohn, epi d᾽ aithopa oinon
leibe: neoi de par᾽ auton ekhon pempohbola khersin.
autar epei kata meer᾽ ekaee kai splagkhna pasanto,
mistullon t᾽ ara talla kai amf᾽ obeloisin epeiran,
ohptohn d᾽ akroporous obelous en khersin ekhontes.

tofra de Teelemakhon lousen kalee Polukastee,
Nestoros oplotatee thugateer Neeleeiadao.
autar epei lousen te kai ekhrisen lip᾽ elaioh,
amfi de min faros kalon balen eede khitohna,
ek r᾽ asaminthou bee demas athanatoisin omoios:
par d᾽ o ge Nestor᾽ iohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezeto, poimena laohn.

oi d᾽ epei ohpteesan kre᾽ upertera kai erusanto,
dainunth᾽ ezomenoi: epi d᾽ aneres esthloi oronto
oinon oinokhoeuntes eni khruseois depaessin.
autar epei posios kai edeetuos ex eron ento,
toisi de muthohn eerkhe Gereenios ippota Nestohr:
"

paides emoi, age Teelemakhoh kallitrikhas ippous
zeuxath᾽ uf᾽ armat᾽ agontes, ina preesseesin odoio.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara tou mala men kluon eed᾽ epithonto,
karpalimohs d᾽ ezeuxan uf᾽ armasin ohkeas ippous.
en de gunee tamiee siton kai oinon etheeken
opsa te, oia edousi diotrefees basileees.
an d᾽ ara Teelemakhos perikallea beeseto difron:
par d᾽ ara Nestoridees Peisistratos, orkhamos androhn,
es difron t᾽ anebaine kai eenia lazeto khersi,
mastixen d᾽ elaan, toh d᾽ ouk aekonte petestheen
es pedion, lipeteen de Pulou aipu ptoliethron.
oi de paneemerioi seion zugon amfis ekhontes.

duseto t᾽ eeelios skioohnto te pasai aguiai,
es Feeras d᾽ ikonto Diokleeos poti dohma,
uieos Ortilokhoio, ton Alfeios teke paida.
entha de nukt᾽ aesan, o de tois par xeinia theeken.

eemos d᾽ eerigeneia fanee rododaktulos Eeohs,
ippous te zeugnunt᾽ ana th᾽ armata poikil᾽ ebainon:
ek d᾽ elasan prothuroio kai aithousees eridoupou:
mastixen d᾽ elaan, toh d᾽ ouk aekonte petestheen.
ixon d᾽ es pedion pureeforon, entha d᾽ epeita
eenon odon: toion gar upekferon ohkees ippoi.
duseto t᾽ eeelios skioohnto te pasai aguiai.


Book 4
------

oi d᾽ ixon koileen Lakedaimona keetohessan,
pros d᾽ ara dohmat᾽ elohn Menelaou kudalimoio.
ton d᾽ euron dainunta gamon polloisin eteesin
uieos eede thugatros amumonos oh eni oikoh.
teen men Akhilleeos reexeenoros uiei pempen:
en Troiee gar prohton upeskheto kai kateneuse
dohsemenai, toisin de theoi gamon exeteleion.
teen ar᾽ o g᾽ enth᾽ ippoisi kai armasi pempe neesthai
Murmidonohn proti astu perikluton, oisin anassen.
uiei de Sparteethen Alektoros eegeto koureen,
os oi teelugetos geneto krateros Megapenthees
ek doulees: Elenee de theoi gonon ouket᾽ efainon,
epei dee to prohton egeinato paid᾽ erateineen,
Ermioneen, ee eidos ekhe khruseees Afroditees.
ohs oi men dainunto kath᾽ upserefes mega dohma
geitones eede etai Menelaou kudalimoio,
terpomenoi: meta de sfin emelpeto theios aoidos
formizohn, doioh de kubisteeteere kat᾽ autous,
molpees exarkhontos, edineuon kata messous.

toh d᾽ aut᾽ en prothuroisi domohn autoh te kai ippoh,
Teelemakhos th᾽ eerohs kai Nestoros aglaos uios,
steesan: o de promolohn ideto kreiohn Eteohneus,
otreeros therapohn Menelaou kudalimoio,
bee d᾽ imen aggeleohn dia dohmata poimeni laohn,
agkhou d᾽ istamenos epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

xeinoh dee tine tohde, diotrefes oh Menelae,
andre duoh, geneee de Dios megaloio eikton.
all᾽ eip᾽, ee sfohin katalusomen ohkeas ippous,
ee allon pempohmen ikanemen, os ke fileesee.
"

ton de meg᾽ okhtheesas prosefee xanthos Menelaos:
"ou men neepios eestha, Boeethoidee Eteohneu,
to prin: atar men nun ge pais ohs neepia bazeis.
ee men dee nohi xeineeia polla fagonte
allohn anthrohpohn deur᾽ ikometh᾽, ai ke pothi Zeus
exopisoh per pausee oizuos. alla lu᾽ ippous
xeinohn, es d᾽ autous proteroh age thoineetheenai.
"

ohs fath᾽, o de megaroio diessuto, kekleto d᾽ allous
otreerous therapontas ama spesthai eoi autoh.
oi d᾽ ippous men lusan upo zugou idrohontas,
kai tous men katedeesan ef᾽ ippeieesi kapeesi,
par d᾽ ebalon zeias, ana de kri leukon emixan,
armata d᾽ eklinan pros enohpia pamfanoohnta,
autous d᾽ eiseegon theion domon. oi de idontes
thaumazon kata dohma diotrefeos basileeos:
ohs te gar eeeliou aiglee pelen eee seleenees
dohma kath᾽ upserefes Menelaou kudalimoio.
autar epei tarpeesan orohmenoi ofthalmoisin,
es r᾽ asaminthous bantes euxestas lousanto.
tous d᾽ epei oun dmohai lousan kai khrisan elaioh,
amfi d᾽ ara khlainas oulas balon eede khitohnas,
es ra thronous ezonto par᾽ Atreideen Menelaon.
kherniba d᾽ amfipolos prokhooh epekheue ferousa
kalee khruseiee uper argureoio lebeetos,
nipsasthai: para de xesteen etanusse trapezan.
siton d᾽ aidoiee tamiee paretheeke ferousa,
eidata poll᾽ epitheisa, kharizomenee pareontohn.
daitros de kreiohn pinakas paretheeken aeiras
pantoiohn, para de sfi tithei khruseia kupella.
toh kai deiknumenos prosefee xanthos Menelaos:
"

sitou th᾽ aptesthon kai khaireton. autar epeita
deipnou passamenoh eireesometh᾽, oi tines eston
androhn: ou gar sfohn ge genos apolohle tokeeohn,
all᾽ androhn genos este diotrefeohn basileeohn
skeeptoukhohn, epei ou ke kakoi toiousde tekoien.
"

ohs fato, kai sfin nohta boos para piona theeken
opt᾽ en khersin elohn, ta ra oi gera parthesan autoh.
oi d᾽ ep᾽ oneiath᾽ etoima prokeimena kheiras iallon.
autar epei posios kai edeetuos ex eron ento,
dee tote Teelemakhos prosefohnee Nestoros uion,
agkhi skhohn kefaleen, ina mee peuthoiath᾽ oi alloi:
"

frazeo, Nestoridee, toh emoh kekharismene thumoh,
khalkou te steropeen kad dohmata eekheeenta
khrusou t᾽ eelektrou te kai argurou eed᾽ elefantos.
Zeenos pou toieede g᾽ Olumpiou endothen aulee,
ossa tad᾽ aspeta polla: sebas m᾽ ekhei eisoroohnta.
"

tou d᾽ agoreuontos xuneto xanthos Menelaos,
kai sfeas fohneesas epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

tekna fil᾽, ee toi Zeeni brotohn ouk an tis erizoi:
athanatoi gar tou ge domoi kai kteemat᾽ easin:
androhn d᾽ ee ken tis moi erissetai, eee kai ouki,
kteemasin. ee gar polla pathohn kai poll᾽ epaleetheis
eegagomeen en neeusi kai ogdoatoh etei eelthon,
Kupron Foinikeen te kai Aiguptious epaleetheis,
Aithiopas th᾽ ikomeen kai Sidonious kai Erembous
kai Libueen, ina t᾽ arnes afar keraoi telethousi.
tris gar tiktei meela telesforon eis eniauton.
entha men oute anax epideuees oute ti poimeen
turou kai kreiohn oude glukeroio galaktos,
all᾽ aiei parekhousin epeeetanon gala theesthai.
eeos egoh peri keina polun bioton sunageirohn
eelohmeen, teeos moi adelfeon allos epefnen
lathree, anohisti, doloh oulomenees alokhoio:
ohs ou toi khairohn toisde kteatessin anassoh.
kai paterohn tade mellet᾽ akouemen, oi tines umin
eisin, epei mala polla pathon, kai apohlesa oikon
eu mala naietaonta, kekhandota polla kai esthla.
ohn ofelon tritateen per ekhohn en dohmasi moiran
naiein, oi d᾽ andres sooi emmenai, oi tot᾽ olonto
Troiee en eureiee ekas Argeos ippobotoio.
all᾽ empees pantas men oduromenos kai akheuohn
pollakis en megaroisi katheemenos eemeteroisin
allote men te gooh frena terpomai, allote d᾽ aute
pauomai: aipseeros de koros krueroio gooio.
tohn pantohn ou tosson oduromai, akhnumenos per,
ohs enos, os te moi upnon apekhthairei kai edohdeen
mnohomenoh, epei ou tis Akhaiohn toss᾽ emogeesen,
oss᾽ Oduseus emogeese kai eerato. toh d᾽ ar᾽ emellen
autoh keede᾽ esesthai, emoi d᾽ akhos aien alaston
keinou, opohs dee deeron apoikhetai, oude ti idmen,
zohei o g᾽ ee tethneeken. odurontai nu pou auton
Laertees th᾽ o gerohn kai ekhefrohn Peenelopeia
Teelemakhos th᾽, on eleipe neon gegaoht᾽ eni oikoh.
"

ohs fato, toh d᾽ ara patros uf᾽ imeron ohrse gooio.
dakru d᾽ apo blefarohn khamadis bale patros akousas,
khlainan porfureeen ant᾽ ofthalmoiin anaskhohn
amfotereesin khersi. noeese de min Menelaos,
mermeerixe d᾽ epeita kata frena kai kata thumon,
eee min auton patros easeie mneestheenai
ee proht᾽ exereoito ekasta te peireesaito.

eeos o tauth᾽ ohrmaine kata frena kai kata thumon,
ek d᾽ Elenee thalamoio thuohdeos upsorofoio
eeluthen Artemidi khruseelakatoh eikuia.
tee d᾽ ar᾽ am᾽ Adreestee klisieen eutukton etheeken,
Alkippee de tapeeta feren malakou erioio,
Fuloh d᾽ argureon talaron fere, ton oi etheeken
Alkandree, Poluboio damar, os enai᾽ eni Theebees
Aiguptiees, othi pleista domois en kteemata keitai:
os Menelaoh dohke du᾽ argureas asaminthous,
doious de tripodas, deka de khrusoio talanta.
khohris d᾽ auth᾽ Elenee alokhos pore kallima dohra:
khruseeen t᾽ eelakateen talaron th᾽ upokuklon opassen
argureon, khrusoh d᾽ epi kheilea kekraanto.
ton ra oi amfipolos Fuloh paretheeke ferousa
neematos askeetoio bebusmenon: autar ep᾽ autoh
eelakatee tetanusto iodnefes eiros ekhousa.
ezeto d᾽ en klismoh, upo de threenus posin eeen.
autika d᾽ ee g᾽ epeessi posin ereeinen ekasta:
"

idmen dee, Menelae diotrefes, oi tines oide
androhn eukhetoohntai ikanemen eemeteron doh;
pseusomai ee etumon ereoh; keletai de me thumos.
ou gar poh tina feemi eoikota ohde idesthai
out᾽ andr᾽ oute gunaika, sebas m᾽ ekhei eisoroohsan,
ohs od᾽ Odusseeos megaleetoros uii eoike,
Teelemakhoh, ton eleipe neon gegaoht᾽ eni oikoh
keinos aneer, ot᾽ emeio kunohpidos einek᾽ Akhaioi
eeltheth᾽ upo Troieen polemon thrasun ormainontes.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee xanthos Menelaos:
"outoh nun kai egoh noeoh, gunai, ohs su eiskeis:
keinou gar toioide podes toiaide te kheires
ofthalmohn te bolai kefalee t᾽ efuperthe te khaitai.
kai nun ee toi egoh memneemenos amf᾽ Oduseei
mutheomeen, osa keinos oizusas emogeesen
amf᾽ emoi, autar o pikron up᾽ ofrusi dakruon eibe,
khlainan porfureeen ant᾽ ofthalmoiin anaskhohn.
"

ton d᾽ au Nestoridees Peisistratos antion eeuda:
"Atreidee Menelae diotrefes, orkhame laohn,
keinou men toi od᾽ uios eteetumon, ohs agoreueis:
alla saofrohn esti, nemessatai d᾽ eni thumoh
ohd᾽ elthohn to prohton epesbolias anafainein
anta sethen, tou nohi theou ohs terpometh᾽ audee.
autar eme proeeeke Gereenios ippota Nestohr
toh ama pompon epesthai: eeldeto gar se idesthai,
ofra oi ee ti epos upotheeseai eee ti ergon.
polla gar alge᾽ ekhei patros pais oikhomenoio
en megarois, oh mee alloi aosseeteeres eohsin,
ohs nun Teelemakhoh o men oikhetai, oude oi alloi
eis᾽ oi ken kata deemon alalkoien kakoteeta.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee xanthos Menelaos:
"oh popoi, ee mala dee filou aneros uios emon doh
iketh᾽, os einek᾽ emeio poleas emogeesen aethlous:
kai min efeen elthonta fileesemen exokhon allohn
Argeiohn, ei nohin upeir ala noston edohke
neeusi thoeesi genesthai Olumpios euruopa Zeus.
kai ke oi Argei nassa polin kai dohmat᾽ eteuxa,
ex Ithakees agagohn sun kteemasi kai tekei oh
kai pasin laoisi, mian polin exalapaxas,
ai perinaietaousin, anassontai d᾽ emoi autoh.
kai ke tham᾽ enthad᾽ eontes emisgometh᾽: oude ken eemeas
allo diekrinen fileonte te terpomenoh te,
prin g᾽ ote dee thanatoio melan nefos amfekalupsen.
alla ta men pou mellen agassesthai theos autos,
os keinon dusteenon anostimon oion etheeken.
"

ohs fato, toisi de pasin uf᾽ imeron ohrse gooio.
klaie men Argeiee Elenee, Dios ekgegauia,
klaie de Teelemakhos te kai Atreidees Menelaos,
oud᾽ ara Nestoros uios adakrutoh ekhen osse:
mneesato gar kata thumon amumonos Antilokhoio,
ton r᾽ Eeous ekteine faeinees aglaos uios:
tou o g᾽ epimneestheis epea pteroent᾽ agoreuen:
"

Atreidee, peri men se brotohn pepnumenon einai
Nestohr faskh᾽ o gerohn, ot᾽ epimneesaimetha seio
oisin eni megaroisi, kai alleelous ereoimen.
kai nun, ei ti pou esti, pithoio moi: ou gar egoh ge
terpom᾽ oduromenos metadorpios, alla kai eeohs
essetai eerigeneia: nemessohmai ge men ouden
klaiein os ke thaneesi brotohn kai potmon epispee.
touto nu kai geras oion oizuroisi brotoisin,
keirasthai te komeen baleein t᾽ apo dakru pareiohn.
kai gar emos tethneeken adelfeos, ou ti kakistos
Argeiohn: melleis de su idmenai: ou gar egoh ge
eentees᾽ oude idon: peri d᾽ allohn fasi genesthai
Antilokhon, peri men theiein takhun eede makheeteen.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee xanthos Menelaos:
"oh fil᾽, epei tosa eipes, os᾽ an pepnumenos aneer
eipoi kai rexeie, kai os progenesteros eiee:
toiou gar kai patros, o kai pepnumena bazeis,
reia d᾽ arignohtos gonos aneros oh te Kroniohn
olbon epiklohsee gameonti te geinomenoh te,
ohs nun Nestori dohke diamperes eemata panta
auton men liparohs geeraskemen en megaroisin,
uieas au pinutous te kai egkhesin einai aristous.
eemeis de klauthmon men easomen, os prin etukhthee,
dorpou d᾽ exautis mneesohmetha, khersi d᾽ ef᾽ udohr
kheuantohn. muthoi de kai eeohthen per esontai
Teelemakhoh kai emoi diaeipemen alleeloisin.
"

ohs efat᾽, Asfaliohn d᾽ ar udohr epi kheiras ekheuen,
otreeros therapohn Menelaou kudalimoio.
oi d᾽ ep᾽ oneiath᾽ etoima prokeimena kheiras iallon.

enth᾽ aut᾽ all᾽ enoees᾽ Elenee Dios ekgegauia:
autik᾽ ar᾽ eis oinon bale farmakon, enthen epinon,
neepenthes t᾽ akholon te, kakohn epileethon apantohn.
os to katabroxeien, epeen kreeteeri migeiee,
ou ken efeemerios ge baloi kata dakru pareiohn,
oud᾽ ei oi katatethnaiee meeteer te pateer te,
oud᾽ ei oi proparoithen adelfeon ee filon uion
khalkoh deeioohen, o d᾽ ofthalmoisin orohto.
toia Dios thugateer ekhe farmaka meetioenta,
esthla, ta oi Poludamna poren, Thohnos parakoitis
Aiguptiee, tee pleista ferei zeidohros aroura
farmaka, polla men esthla memigmena polla de lugra:
ieetros de ekastos epistamenos peri pantohn
anthrohpohn: ee gar Paieeonos eisi genethlees.
autar epei r᾽ eneeeke keleuse te oinokhoeesai,
exautis muthoisin ameibomenee proseeipen:
"

Atreidee Menelae diotrefes eede kai oide
androhn esthlohn paides: atar theos allote alloh
Zeus agathon te kakon te didoi: dunatai gar apanta:
ee toi nun dainusthe katheemenoi en megaroisi
kai muthois terpesthe: eoikota gar katalexoh.
panta men ouk an egoh mutheesomai oud᾽ onomeenoh,
ossoi Odusseeos talasifronos eisin aethloi:
all᾽ oion tod᾽ erexe kai etlee karteros aneer
deemoh eni Trohohn, othi paskhete peemat᾽ Akhaioi.
