xeinon agohn agoreende dia ptolin: oud᾽ ar᾽ eti deen
Teelemakhos xeinoio ekas trapet᾽, alla parestee.
ton kai Peiraios proteros pros muthon eeipe:
"

Teelemakh᾽, aips᾽ otrunon emon poti dohma gunaikas,
ohs toi dohr᾽ apopempsoh, a toi Menelaos edohke.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"Peirai᾽, ou gar t᾽ idmen opohs estai tade erga.
ei ken eme mneesteeres ageenores en megaroisi
lathree kteinantes patrohia panta dasohntai,
auton ekhonta se boulom᾽ epauremen, ee tina tohnde:
ei de k᾽ egoh toutoisi fonon kai keera futeusoh,
dee tote moi khaironti ferein pros dohmata khairohn.
"

ohs eipohn xeinon talapeirion eegen es oikon.
autar epei r᾽ ikonto domous eu naietaontas,
khlainas men katethento kata klismous te thronous te,
es d᾽ asaminthous bantes euxestas lousanto.
tous d᾽ epei oun dmohai lousan kai khrisan elaioh,
amfi d᾽ ara khlainas oulas balon eede khitohnas,
ek r᾽ asaminthohn bantes epi klismoisi kathizon.
kherniba d᾽ amfipolos prokhooh epekheue ferousa
kalee khruseiee, uper argureoio lebeetos,
nipsasthai: para de xesteen etanusse trapezan.
siton d᾽ aidoiee tamiee paretheeke ferousa,
eidata poll᾽ epitheisa, kharizomenee pareontohn.
meeteer d᾽ antion ize para stathmon megaroio
klismoh keklimenee, lept᾽ eelakata strohfohsa.
oi d᾽ ep᾽ oneiath᾽ etoima prokeimena kheiras iallon,
autar epei posios kai edeetuos ex eron ento,
toisi de muthohn eerkhe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"

Teelemakh᾽, ee toi egohn uperohion eisanabasa
lexomai eis euneen, ee moi stonoessa tetuktai,
aiei dakrus᾽ emoisi pefurmenee, ex ou Odusseus
ohkheth᾽ am᾽ Atreideesin es Ilion: oude moi etlees,
prin elthein mneesteeras ageenoras es tode dohma,
noston sou patros safa eipemen, ei pou akousas.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"toigar egoh toi, meeter, aleetheieen katalexoh.
ohkhometh᾽ es te Pulon kai Nestora, poimena laohn:
dexamenos de me keinos en upseeloisi domoisin
endukeohs efilei, ohs ei te pateer eon uion
elthonta khronion neon allothen: ohs eme keinos
endukeohs ekomize sun uiasi kudalimoisin.
autar Odusseeos talasifronos ou pot᾽ efasken,
zohou oude thanontos, epikhthoniohn teu akousai:
alla m᾽ es Atreideen, dourikleiton Menelaon,
ippoisi proupempse kai armasi kolleetoisin.
enth᾽ idon Argeieen Eleneen, ees eineka polla
Argeioi Trohes te theohn ioteeti mogeesan.
eireto d᾽ autik᾽ epeita boeen agathos Menelaos
otteu khreeizohn ikomeen Lakedaimona dian:
autar egoh toh pasan aleetheieen katelexa:
kai tote dee me epessin ameibomenos proseeipen:
"

oh popoi, ee mala dee kraterofronos andros en eunee
eethelon euneetheenai, analkides autoi eontes.
ohs d᾽ opot᾽ en xulokhoh elafos krateroio leontos
nebrous koimeesasa neeegeneas galatheenous
kneemous exereeesi kai agkea poieeenta
boskomenee, o d᾽ epeita eeen eiseeluthen euneen,
amfoteroisi de toisin aeikea potmon efeeken,
ohs Oduseus keinoisin aeikea potmon efeesei.
ai gar, Zeu te pater kai Atheenaiee kai Apollon,
toios eohn oios pot᾽ euktimenee eni Lesboh
ex eridos Filomeeleidee epalaisen anastas,
kad d᾽ ebale kraterohs, kekharonto de pantes Akhaioi,
toios eohn mneesteersin omileeseien Odusseus:
pantes k᾽ ohkumoroi te genoiato pikrogamoi te.
tauta d᾽ a m᾽ eirohtas kai lisseai, ouk an egoh ge
alla parex eipoimi paraklidon oud᾽ apateesoh,
alla ta men moi eeipe gerohn alios neemertees,
tohn ouden toi egoh krupsoh epos oud᾽ epikeusoh.
fee min o g᾽ en neesoh ideein krater᾽ alge᾽ ekhonta,
numfees en megaroisi Kalupsous, ee min anagkee
iskhei: o d᾽ ou dunatai een patrida gaian ikesthai.
ou gar oi para neees epeeretmoi kai etairoi,
oi ken min pempoien ep᾽ eurea nohta thalassees
"

ohs efat᾽ Atreidees, dourikleitos Menelaos.
tauta teleuteesas neomeen: edosan de moi ouron
athanatoi, toi m᾽ ohka fileen es patrid᾽ epempsan.
"

ohs fato, tee d᾽ ara thumon eni steethessin orine.
toisi de kai meteeipe Theoklumenos theoeidees:
"

oh gunai aidoiee Laertiadeoh Oduseeos,
ee toi o g᾽ ou safa oiden, emeio de suntheo muthon:
atrekeohs gar soi manteusomai oud᾽ epikeusoh:
istoh nun Zeus prohta theohn, xeniee te trapeza
istiee t᾽ Oduseeos amumonos, een afikanoh,
ohs ee toi Oduseus eedee en patridi gaiee,
eemenos ee erpohn, tade peuthomenos kaka erga,
estin, atar mneesteersi kakon pantessi futeuei:
toion egohn oiohnon eusselmou epi neeos
eemenos efrasameen kai Teelemakhoh egegohneun.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"ai gar touto, xeine, epos tetelesmenon eiee:
toh ke takha gnoiees filoteeta te polla te dohra
ex emeu, ohs an tis se sunantomenos makarizoi.
"

ohs oi men toiauta pros alleelous agoreuon,
mneesteeres de paroithen Odusseeos megaroio
diskoisin terponto kai aiganeeesin ientes,
en tuktoh dapedoh, othi per paros ubrin ekhontes.
all᾽ ote dee deipneestos eeen kai epeeluthe meela
pantothen ex agrohn, oi d᾽ eegagon oi to paros per,
kai tote dee sfin eeipe Medohn: os gar ra malista
eendane keerukohn, kai sfin paregigneto daiti:
"

kouroi, epei dee pantes eterftheete fren᾽ aethlois,
erkhesthe pros dohmath᾽, in᾽ entunohmetha daita:
ou men gar ti khereion en ohree deipnon elesthai.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ anstantes eban peithonto te muthoh.
autar epei r᾽ ikonto domous eu naietaontas,
khlainas men katethento kata klismous te thronous te,
oi d᾽ iereuon ois megalous kai pionas aigas,
ireuon de suas sialous kai boun agelaieen,
dait᾽ entunomenoi. toi d᾽ ex agroio polinde
ohtrunont᾽ Oduseus t᾽ ienai kai dios uforbos.
toisi de muthohn eerkhe subohtees, orkhamos androhn:
"

xein᾽, epei ar dee epeita polind᾽ ienai meneaineis
seemeron, ohs epetellen anax emos--ee s᾽ an egoh ge
autou bouloimeen stathmohn ruteera lipesthai:
alla ton aideomai kai deidia, mee moi opissoh
neikeiee: khalepai de t᾽ anaktohn eisin omoklai--
all᾽ age nun iomen: dee gar memblohke malista
eemar, atar takha toi poti espera rigion estai.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"gignohskoh, froneoh: ta ge dee noeonti keleueis.
all᾽ iomen, su d᾽ epeita diamperes eegemoneue.
dos de moi, ei pothi toi ropalon tetmeemenon estin,
skeeriptesth᾽, epei ee fat᾽ arisfale᾽ emmenai oudon.
"

ee ra kai amf᾽ ohmoisin aeikea balleto peereen,
pukna rohgaleeen: en de strofos eeen aorteer:
Eumaios d᾽ ara oi skeeptron thumares edohke.
toh beeteen, stathmon de kunes kai bohtores andres
ruat᾽ opisthe menontes: o d᾽ es polin eegen anakta
ptohkhoh leugaleoh enaligkion eede geronti,
skeeptomenon: ta de lugra peri khroi eimata esto.

all᾽ ote dee steikhontes odon kata paipaloessan
asteos eggus esan kai epi kreeneen afikonto
tukteen kalliroon, othen udreuonto politai,
teen poiees᾽ Ithakos kai Neeritos eede Poluktohr:
amfi d᾽ ar᾽ aigeirohn udatotrefeohn een alsos,
pantose kukloteres, kata de psukhron reen udohr
upsothen ek petrees: bohmos d᾽ efuperthe tetukto
numfaohn, othi pantes epirrezeskon oditai:
entha sfeas ekikhan᾽ uios Dolioio Melantheus
aigas agohn, ai pasi meteprepon aipolioisi,
deipnon mneesteeressi: duoh d᾽ am᾽ eponto nomeees.
tous de idohn neikessen epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomazen,
ekpaglon kai aeikes: orine de keer Oduseeos:
"

nun men dee mala pagkhu kakos kakon eegeelazei,
ohs aiei ton omoion agei theos ohs ton omoin.
pee dee tonde molobron ageis, amegarte subohta,
ptohkhon anieeron daitohn apolumanteera;
os pollees flieesi parastas thlipsetai ohmous,
aitizohn akolous, ouk aoras oude lebeetas:
ton k᾽ ei moi doiees stathmohn ruteera genesthai
seekokoron t᾽ emenai thallon t᾽ erifoisi foreenai,
kai ken oron pinohn megaleen epigounida theito.
all᾽ epei oun dee erga kak᾽ emmathen, ouk etheleesei
ergon epoikhesthai, alla ptohssohn kata deemon
bouletai aitizohn boskein een gaster᾽ analton.
all᾽ ek toi ereoh, to de kai tetelesmenon estai:
ai k᾽ elthee pros dohmat᾽ Odusseeos theioio,
polla oi amfi karee sfela androhn ek palamaohn
pleurai apotripsousi domon kata ballomenoio.
"

ohs fato, kai pariohn lax enthoren afradieesin
iskhioh: oude min ektos atarpitou estufelixen,
all᾽ emen᾽ asfaleohs: o de mermeerixen Odusseus
eee metaixas ropaloh ek thumon eloito,
ee pros geen elaseie karee amfoudis aeiras.
all᾽ epetolmeese, fresi d᾽ eskheto: ton de subohtees
neikes᾽ esanta idohn, mega d᾽ euxato kheiras anaskhohn:
"

numfai kreenaiai, kourai Dios, ei pot᾽ Odusseus
umm᾽ epi meeri᾽ ekeee, kalupsas pioni deemoh,
arnohn eed᾽ erifohn, tode moi kreeeenat᾽ eeldohr,
ohs elthoi men keinos aneer, agagoi de e daimohn:
toh ke toi aglaias ge diaskedaseien apasas,
tas nun ubrizohn foreeis, alaleemenos aiei
astu kat᾽: autar meela kakoi ftheirousi nomeees.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe Melanthios, aipolos aigohn:
"oh popoi, oion eeipe kuohn olofohia eidohs,
ton pot᾽ egohn epi neeos eusselmoio melainees
axoh teel᾽ Ithakees, ina moi bioton polun alfoi.
ai gar Teelemakhon baloi argurotoxos Apollohn
seemeron en megarois, ee upo mneesteersi dameiee,
ohs Oduseei ge teelou apohleto nostimon eemar.
"

ohs eipohn tous men lipen autou eeka kiontas,
autar o bee, mala d᾽ ohka domous ikanen anaktos.
autika d᾽ eisoh ien, meta de mneesteersi kathizen,
antion Eurumakhou: ton gar fileeske malista.
toh para men kreiohn moiran thesan oi poneonto,
siton d᾽ aidoiee tamiee paretheeke ferousa
edmenai. agkhimolon d᾽ Oduseus kai dios uforbos
steeteen erkhomenoh, peri de sfeas eeluth᾽ iohee
formiggos glafurees: ana gar sfisi ballet᾽ aeidein
Feemios: autar o kheiros elohn proseeipe subohteen:
"

Eumai᾽, ee mala dee tade dohmata kal᾽ Oduseeos,
reia d᾽ arignoht᾽ esti kai en polloisin idesthai.
ex eterohn eter᾽ estin, epeeskeetai de oi aulee
toikhoh kai thrigkoisi, thurai d᾽ euerkees eisi
diklides: ouk an tis min aneer uperoplissaito.
gignohskoh d᾽ oti polloi en autoh daita tithentai
andres, epei knisee men aneenothen, en de te formigx
eepuei, een ara daiti theoi poieesan etaireen.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefees, Eumaie subohta:
"rei᾽ egnohs, epei oude ta t᾽ alla per ess᾽ anoeemohn.
all᾽ age dee frazohmeth᾽ opohs estai tade erga.
eee su prohtos eselthe domous eu naietaontas,
duseo de mneesteeras, egoh d᾽ upoleipsomai autou:
ei d᾽ etheleis, epimeinon, egoh d᾽ eimi proparoithe:
meede su deethunein, mee tis s᾽ ektosthe noeesas
ee balee ee elasee: ta de se frazesthai anohga.
" ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita polutlas dios Odusseus:
"

gignohskoh, froneoh: ta ge dee noeonti keleueis.
all᾽ erkheu proparoithen, egoh d᾽ upoleipsomai autou.
ou gar ti pleegeohn adaeemohn oude bolaohn:
tolmeeeis moi thumos, epei kaka polla pepontha
kumasi kai polemoh: meta kai tode toisi genesthoh:
gastera d᾽ ou pohs estin apokrupsai memauian,
oulomeneen, ee polla kak᾽ anthrohpoisi didohsi,
tees eneken kai neees euzugoi oplizontai
ponton ep᾽ atrugeton, kaka dusmeneessi ferousai.
" ohs oi men toiauta pros alleelous agoreuon:
an de kuohn kefaleen te kai ouata keimenos eskhen,
Argos, Odusseeos talasifronos, on ra pot᾽ autos
threpse men, oud᾽ aponeeto, paros d᾽ eis Ilion ireen
ohkheto. ton de paroithen agineskon neoi andres
aigas ep᾽ agroteras eede prokas eede lagohous:
dee tote keit᾽ apothestos apoikhomenoio anaktos,
en pollee koproh, ee oi proparoithe thuraohn
eemionohn te boohn te alis kekhut᾽, ofr᾽ an agoien
dmohes Odusseeos temenos mega kopreesontes:
entha kuohn keit᾽ Argos, enipleios kunoraisteohn.
dee tote g᾽, ohs enoeesen Odussea eggus eonta,
ouree men r᾽ o g᾽ eseene kai ouata kabbalen amfoh,
asson d᾽ ouket᾽ epeita duneesato oio anaktos
elthemen: autar o nosfin idohn apomorxato dakru,
reia lathohn Eumaion, afar d᾽ ereeineto muthoh:
"

Eumai᾽, ee mala thauma, kuohn ode keit᾽ eni koproh.
kalos men demas estin, atar tode g᾽ ou safa oida,
ei dee kai takhus eske theein epi eidei tohde,
ee autohs oioi te trapezeees kunes androhn
gignont᾽: aglaiees d᾽ eneken komeousin anaktes.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefees, Eumaie subohta:
"kai lieen andros ge kuohn ode teele thanontos.
ei toiosd᾽ eiee eemen demas eede kai erga,
oion min Troieende kiohn kateleipen Odusseus,
aipsa ke theeeesaio idohn takhuteeta kai alkeen.
ou men gar ti fugeske batheiees benthesin ulees
knohdalon, otti dioito: kai ikhnesi gar perieedee:
nun d᾽ ekhetai kakoteeti, anax de oi allothi patrees
ohleto, ton de gunaikes akeedees ou komeousi.
dmohes d᾽, eut᾽ an meeket᾽ epikrateohsin anaktes,
ouket᾽ epeit᾽ ethelousin enaisima ergazesthai:
eemisu gar t᾽ aretees apoainutai euruopa Zeus
aneros, eut᾽ an min kata doulion eemar eleesin.
"

ohs eipohn eiseelthe domous eu naietaontas,
bee d᾽ ithus megaroio meta mneesteeras agauous.
Argon d᾽ au kata moir᾽ elaben melanos thanatoio,
autik᾽ idont᾽ Oduseea eeikostoh eniautoh.

ton de polu prohtos ide Teelemakhos theoeidees
erkhomenon kata dohma subohteen, ohka d᾽ epeita
neus᾽ epi oi kalesas: o de papteenas ele difron
keimenon, entha te daitros efizeske krea polla
daiomenos mneesteersi domon kata dainumenoisi:
ton katetheeke ferohn pros Teelemakhoio trapezan
antion, entha d᾽ ar᾽ autos efezeto: toh d᾽ ara keerux
moiran elohn etithei kaneou t᾽ ek siton aeiras.

agkhimolon de met᾽ auton eduseto dohmat᾽ Odusseus,
ptohkhoh leugaleoh enaligkios eede geronti,
skeeptomenos: ta de lugra peri khroi eimata esto.
ize d᾽ epi melinou oudou entosthe thuraohn,
klinamenos stathmoh kuparissinoh, on pote tektohn
xessen epistamenohs kai epi stathmeen ithunen.
Teelemakhos d᾽ epi oi kalesas proseeipe subohteen,
arton t᾽ oulon elohn perikalleos ek kaneoio
kai kreas, ohs oi kheires ekhandanon amfibalonti:
"dos toh xeinoh tauta ferohn auton te keleue
aitizein mala pantas epoikhomenon mneesteeras:
aidohs d᾽ ouk agathee kekhreemenoh andri pareinai.
"

ohs fato, bee de suforbos, epei ton muthon akousen,
agkhou d᾽ istamenos epea pteroent᾽ agoreue:
"

Teelemakhos toi, xeine, didoi tade, kai se keleuei
aitizein mala pantas epoikhomenon mneesteeras:
aidoh d᾽ ouk agatheen fees᾽ emmenai andri proiktee.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"Zeu ana, Teelemakhon moi en andrasin olbion einai,
kai oi panta genoith᾽ ossa fresin eesi menoina.
"

ee ra kai amfotereesin edexato kai katetheeken
authi podohn proparoithen, aeikeliees epi peerees,
eesthie d᾽ eeos aoidos eni megaroisin aeiden:
euth᾽ o dedeipneekein, o d᾽ epaueto theios aoidos.
mneesteeres d᾽ omadeesan ana megar᾽. autar Atheenee,
agkhi paristamenee Laertiadeen Oduseea
ohtrun᾽, ohs an purna kata mneesteeras ageiroi,
gnoiee th᾽ oi tines eisin enaisimoi oi t᾽ athemistoi:
all᾽ oud᾽ ohs tin᾽ emell᾽ apalexeesein kakoteetos.
bee d᾽ imen aiteesohn endexia fohta ekaston,
pantose kheir᾽ oregohn, ohs ei ptohkhos palai eiee.
oi d᾽ eleairontes didosan, kai ethambeon auton,
alleelous t᾽ eironto tis eiee kai pothen elthoi.

toisi de kai meteeipe Melanthios, aipolos aigohn:
"keklute meu, mneesteeres agakleitees basileiees,
toude peri xeinou: ee gar min prosthen opohpa.
ee toi men oi deuro subohtees eegemoneuen,
auton d᾽ ou safa oida, pothen genos eukhetai einai.
"

ohs efat᾽, Antinoos d᾽ epesin neikesse subohteen:
"oh arignohte subohta, tiee de su tonde polinde
eegages; ee oukh alis eemin aleemones eisi kai alloi,
ptohkhoi anieeroi, daitohn apolumanteeres;
ee onosai oti toi bioton katedousin anaktos
enthad᾽ ageiromenoi, su de kai proti tond᾽ ekalessas;
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefees, Eumaie subohta:
"Antino᾽, ou men kala kai esthlos eohn agoreueis:
tis gar dee xeinon kalei allothen autos epelthohn
allon g᾽, ei mee tohn oi deemioergoi easi,
mantin ee ieeteera kakohn ee tektona dourohn,
ee kai thespin aoidon, o ken terpeesin aeidohn;
outoi gar kleetoi ge brotohn ep᾽ apeirona gaian:
ptohkhon d᾽ ouk an tis kaleoi truxonta e auton.
all᾽ aiei khalepos peri pantohn eis mneesteerohn
dmohsin Odusseeos, peri d᾽ aut᾽ emoi: autar egoh ge
ouk alegoh, eeos moi ekhefrohn Peenelopeia
zohei eni megarois kai Teelemakhos theoeidees.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"siga, mee moi touton ameibeo polla epessin:
Antinoos d᾽ eiohthe kakohs erethizemen aiei
muthoisin khalepoisin, epotrunei de kai allous.
"

ee ra kai Antinoon epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"Antino᾽, ee meu kala pateer ohs keedeai uios,
os ton xeinon anohgas apo megaroio diesthai
muthoh anagkaioh: mee touto theos teleseie.
dos oi elohn: ou toi fthoneoh: kelomai gar egoh ge:
meet᾽ oun meeter᾽ emeen azeu to ge meete tin᾽ allon
dmohohn, oi kata dohmat᾽ Odusseeos theioio.
all᾽ ou toi toiouton eni steethessi noeema:
autos gar fagemen polu bouleai ee domen alloh.
" ton d᾽ aut᾽ Antinoos apameibomenos proseeipe:
"Teelemakh᾽ upsagoree, menos askhete, poion eeipes.
ei oi tosson apantes orexeian mneesteeres,
kai ken min treis meenas apoprothen oikos erukoi.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, kai threenun elohn upefeene trapezees
keimenon, oh r᾽ epekhen liparous podas eilapinazohn:
oi d᾽ alloi pantes didosan, pleesan d᾽ ara peereen
sitou kai kreiohn: takha dee kai emellen Odusseus
autis ep᾽ oudon iohn proikos geusesthai Akhaiohn:
stee de par᾽ Antinoon, kai min pros muthon eeipe:
"

dos, filos: ou men moi dokeeis o kakistos Akhaiohn
emmenai, all᾽ ohristos, epei basileei eoikas.
toh se khree domenai kai lohion eee per alloi
sitou: egoh de ke se kleioh kat᾽ apeirona gaian.
kai gar egoh pote oikon en anthrohpoisin enaion
olbios afneion kai pollaki doskon aleetee,
toioh opoios eoi kai oteu kekhreemenos elthoi:
eesan de dmohes mala murioi alla te polla
oisin t᾽ eu zohousi kai afneioi kaleontai.
alla Zeus alapaxe Kroniohn--eethele gar pou--
os m᾽ ama leeisteersi poluplagktoisin aneeken
Aiguptond᾽ ienai, dolikheen odon, ofr᾽ apoloimeen.
steesa d᾽ en Aiguptoh potamoh neas amfielissas.
enth᾽ ee toi men egoh kelomeen erieeras etairous
autou par neeessi menein kai neeas erusthai,
opteeras de kata skopias ohtruna neesthai.
oi d᾽ ubrei eixantes, epispomenoi menei sfoh,
aipsa mal᾽ Aiguptiohn androhn perikalleas agrous
portheon, ek de gunaikas agon kai neepia tekna,
autous t᾽ ekteinon: takha d᾽ es polin iket᾽ autee.
oi de boees aiontes am᾽ eeoi fainomeneefin
eelthon: pleeto de pan pedion pezohn te kai ippohn
khalkou te steropees: en de Zeus terpikeraunos
fuzan emois etaroisi kakeen balen, oude tis etlee
steenai enantibion: peri gar kaka pantothen estee.
enth᾽ eemeohn pollous men apektanon oxei khalkoh,
tous d᾽ anagon zohous, sfisin ergazesthai anagkee.
autar em᾽ es Kupron xeinoh dosan antiasanti,
Dmeetori Iasidee, os Kuprou ifi anassen:
enthen dee nun deuro tod᾽ ikoh peemata paskhohn.
" ton d᾽ aut᾽ Antinoos apameibeto fohneesen te:
"tis daimohn tode peema proseegage, daitos anieen;
steeth᾽ outohs es messon, emees apaneuthe trapezees,
mee takha pikreen Aigupton kai Kupron ikeeai:
ohs tis tharsaleos kai anaidees essi proiktees.
exeiees pantessi paristasai: oi de didousi
mapsidiohs, epei ou tis episkhesis oud᾽ eleeetus
allotriohn kharisasthai, epei para polla ekastoh.
"

ton d᾽ anakhohreesas prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh popoi, ouk ara soi g᾽ epi eidei kai frenes eesan:
ou su g᾽ an ex oikou soh epistatee oud᾽ ala doiees,
os nun allotrioisi pareemenos ou ti moi etlees
sitou apoproelohn domenai: ta de polla parestin.
"

ohs efat᾽, Antinoos d᾽ ekholohsato keerothi mallon,
kai min upodra idohn epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"nun dee s᾽ ouketi kala diek megaroio g᾽ oioh
aps anakhohreesein, ote dee kai oneidea bazeis.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, kai threenun elohn bale dexion ohmon,
prumnotaton kata nohton: o d᾽ estathee eeute petree
empedon, oud᾽ ara min sfeelen belos Antinooio,
all᾽ akeohn kineese karee, kaka bussodomeuohn.
aps d᾽ o g᾽ ep᾽ oudon iohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezeto, kad d᾽ ara peereen
theeken eupleieen, meta de mneesteersin eeipe:
"

keklute meu, mneesteeres agakleitees basileiees,
ofr᾽ eipoh ta me thumos eni steethessi keleuei.
ou man out᾽ akhos esti meta fresin oute ti penthos,
oppot᾽ aneer peri oisi makheiomenos kteatessi
bleeetai, ee peri bousin ee argennees oiessin:
autar em᾽ Antinoos bale gasteros eineka lugrees,
oulomenees, ee polla kak᾽ anthrohpoisi didohsin.
all᾽ ei pou ptohkhohn ge theoi kai Erinues eisin,
Antinoon pro gamoio telos thanatoio kikheiee.
"

ton d᾽ aut᾽ Antinoos prosefee, Eupeitheos uios:
"esthi᾽ ekeelos, xeine, katheemenos, ee apith᾽ allee,
mee se neoi dia dohmat᾽ erussohs᾽, oi᾽ agoreueis,
ee podos ee kai kheiros, apodrupsohsi de panta.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes uperfialohs nemeseesan:
ohde de tis eipeske neohn upereenoreontohn:
"

Antino᾽, ou men kal᾽ ebales dusteenon aleeteen,
oulomen᾽, ei dee pou tis epouranios theos estin.
kai te theoi xeinoisin eoikotes allodapoisi,
pantoioi telethontes, epistrohfohsi poleeas,
anthrohpohn ubrin te kai eunomieen eforohntes.
"

ohs ar᾽ efan mneesteeres, o d᾽ ouk empazeto muthohn.
Teelemakhos d᾽ en men kradiee mega penthos aexe
bleemenou, oud᾽ ara dakru khamai balen ek blefaroiin,
all᾽ akeohn kineese karee, kaka bussodomeuohn.

tou d᾽ ohs oun eekouse perifrohn Peenelopeia
bleemenou en megaroh, met᾽ ara dmoheesin eeipen:
"aith᾽ outohs auton se baloi klutotoxos Apollohn.
" teen d᾽ aut᾽ Eurunomee tamiee pros muthon eeipen:
"ei gar ep᾽ areesin telos eemetereesi genoito:
ouk an tis toutohn ge euthronon Eeoh ikoito.
"

teen d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"mai᾽, ekhthroi men pantes, epei kaka meekhanoohntai:
Antinoos de malista melainee keeri eoike.
xeinos tis dusteenos aleeteuei kata dohma
aneras aitizohn: akhreemosunee gar anohgei:
enth᾽ alloi men pantes enepleesan t᾽ edosan te,
outos de threenui prumnon bale dexion ohmon.
"

ee men ar᾽ ohs agoreue meta dmoheesi gunaixin,
eemenee en thalamoh: o d᾽ edeipnee dios Odusseus:
ee d᾽ epi oi kalesasa proseeuda dion uforbon:
"

erkheo, di᾽ Eumaie, kiohn ton xeinon anohkhthi
elthemen, ofra ti min prosptuxomai eed᾽ ereohmai
ei pou Odusseeos talasifronos eee pepustai
ee iden ofthalmoisi: poluplagktoh gar eoike.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefees, Eumaie subohta
"ei gar toi, basileia, siohpeeseian Akhaioi:
oi᾽ o ge mutheitai, thelgoito ke toi filon eetor.
treis gar dee min nuktas ekhon, tria d᾽ eemat᾽ eruxa
en klisiee: prohton gar em᾽ iketo neeos apodras:
all᾽ ou poh kakoteeta dieenusen een agoreuohn.
ohs d᾽ ot᾽ aoidon aneer potiderketai, os te theohn ex
aeidei dedaohs epe᾽ imeroenta brotoisi,
tou d᾽ amoton memaasin akouemen, oppot᾽ aeidee:
ohs eme keinos ethelge pareemenos en megaroisi.
feesi d᾽ Odusseeos xeinos patrohios einai,
Kreetee naietaohn, othi Minohos genos estin.
enthen dee nun deuro tod᾽ iketo peemata paskhohn,
proprokulindomenos: steutai d᾽ Oduseeos akousai,
agkhou, Thesprohtohn androhn en pioni deemoh,
zohou: polla d᾽ agei keimeelia onde domonde.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"erkheo, deuro kalesson, in᾽ antion autos enispee.
outoi d᾽ eee thureesi katheemenoi epsiaasthohn.
ee autou kata dohmat᾽, epei sfisi thumos eufrohn.
autohn men gar kteemat᾽ akeerata keit᾽ eni oikoh,
sitos kai methu eedu: ta men oikeees edousin,
oi d᾽ eis eemeteron pohleumenoi eemata panta,
bous iereuontes kai ois kai pionas aigas,
eilapinazousin pinousi te aithopa oinon,
mapsidiohs: ta de polla katanetai. ou gar ep᾽ aneer,
oios Odusseus esken, areen apo oikou amunai.
ei d᾽ Oduseus elthoi kai ikoit᾽ es patrida gaian,
aipsa ke sun oh paidi bias apotisetai androhn.
"

ohs fato, Teelemakhos de meg᾽ eptaren, amfi de dohma
smerdaleon konabeese: gelasse de Peenelopeia,
aipsa d᾽ ar᾽ Eumaion epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

erkheo moi, ton xeinon enantion ohde kalesson.
oukh oraas o moi uios epeptare pasin epessi;
toh ke kai ouk atelees thanatos mneesteersi genoito
pasi mal᾽, oude ke tis thanaton kai keeras aluxei.
allo de toi ereoh, su d᾽ eni fresi balleo seesin:
ai k᾽ auton gnohoh neemertea pant᾽ eneponta,
essoh min khlainan te khitohna te, eimata kala.
"

ohs fato, bee de suforbos, epei ton muthon akousen:
agkhou d᾽ istamenos epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

xeine pater, kaleei se perifrohn Peenelopeia,
meeteer Teelemakhoio: metalleesai ti e thumos
amfi posei keletai, kai keedea per pepathuiee.
ei de ke se gnohee neemertea pant᾽ eneponta,
essei se khlainan te khitohna te, tohn su malista
khreeizeis: siton de kai aitizohn kata deemon
gastera boskeeseis: dohsei de toi os k᾽ etheleesi.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe polutlas dios Odusseus:
"Eumai᾽, aipsa k᾽ egoh neemertea pant᾽ enepoimi
kouree Ikarioio, perifroni Peenelopeiee:
oida gar eu peri keinou, omeen d᾽ anedegmeth᾽ oizun.
alla mneesteerohn khalepohn upodeidi᾽ omilon,
tohn ubris te biee te sideereon ouranon ikei.
kai gar nun, ote m᾽ outos aneer kata dohma kionta
ou ti kakon rexanta balohn oduneesin edohken,
oute ti Teelemakhos to g᾽ epeerkesen oute tis allos.
toh nun Peenelopeian eni megaroisin anohkhthi
meinai, epeigomeneen per, es eeelion katadunta:
kai tote m᾽ eiresthoh posios peri nostimon eemar,
assoteroh kathisasa parai puri: eimata gar toi
lugr᾽ ekhoh: oistha kai autos, epei se prohth᾽ iketeusa.
"

ohs fato, bee de suforbos, epei ton muthon akouse.
ton d᾽ uper oudou banta proseeuda Peenelopeia:
"

ou su g᾽ ageis, Eumaie: ti tout᾽ enoeesen aleetees;
ee tina pou deisas exaision eee kai allohs
aideitai kata dohma; kakos d᾽ aidoios aleetees.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefees, Eumaie subohta:
"mutheitai kata moiran, a per k᾽ oioito kai allos,
ubrin aluskazohn androhn upereenoreontohn.
alla se meinai anohgen es eeelion katadunta.
kai de soi ohd᾽ autee polu kallion, oh basileia,
oieen pros xeinon fasthai epos eed᾽ epakousai.
" ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"ouk afrohn o xeinos: oietai, ohs per an eiee:
ou gar pou tines ohde katathneetohn anthrohpohn
aneres ubrizontes atasthala meekhanoohntai.
"

ee men ar᾽ ohs agoreuen, o d᾽ ohkheto dios uforbos
mneesteerohn es omilon, epei diepefrade panta.
aipsa de Teelemakhon epea pteroenta proseeuda,
agkhi skhohn kefaleen, ina mee peuthoiath᾽ oi alloi:
"

oh fil᾽, egoh men apeimi, suas kai keina fulaxohn,
son kai emon bioton: soi d᾽ enthade panta melontohn.
auton men se prohta saoh, kai frazeo thumoh
mee ti pathees: polloi de kaka froneousin Akhaiohn,
tous Zeus exoleseie prin eemin peema genesthai.
"

ton d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"essetai outohs, atta: su d᾽ erkheo deielieesas:
eeohthen d᾽ ienai kai agein iereeia kala:
autar emoi tade panta kai athanatoisi meleesei.
"

ohs fath᾽, o d᾽ autis ar᾽ ezet᾽ euxestou epi difrou,
pleesamenos d᾽ ara thumon edeetuos eede poteetos
bee r᾽ imenai meth᾽ uas, lipe d᾽ erkea te megaron te,
pleion daitumonohn: oi d᾽ orkheestui kai aoidee
terpont᾽: eedee gar kai epeeluthe deielon eemar.


Book 18
-------

eelthe d᾽ epi ptohkhos pandeemios, os kata astu
ptohkheuesk᾽ Ithakees, meta d᾽ eprepe gasteri margee
azeekhes fagemen kai piemen: oude oi een is
oude biee, eidos de mala megas een oraasthai.
Arnaios d᾽ onom᾽ eske: to gar theto potnia meeteer
ek genetees: Iron de neoi kikleeskon apantes,
ounek᾽ apaggelleske kiohn, ote pou tis anohgoi:
os r᾽ elthohn Oduseea diohketo oio domoio,
kai min neikeiohn epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"
eike, geron, prothurou, mee dee takha kai podos elkee.
ouk aieis oti dee moi epillizousin apantes,
elkemenai de kelontai; egoh d᾽ aiskhunomai empees.
all᾽ ana, mee takha nohin eris kai khersi geneetai.
"

ton d᾽ ar᾽ upodra idohn prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"daimoni᾽, oute ti se rezoh kakon out᾽ agoreuoh,
oute tina fthoneoh domenai kai poll᾽ anelonta.
oudos d᾽ amfoterous ode kheisetai, oude ti se khree
allotriohn fthoneein: dokeeis de moi einai aleetees
ohs per egohn, olbon de theoi mellousin opazein.
khersi de mee ti lieen prokalizeo, mee me kholohsees,
mee se gerohn per eohn steethos kai kheilea fursoh
aimatos: eesukhiee d᾽ an emoi kai mallon et᾽ eiee
aurion: ou men gar ti s᾽ upostrepsesthai oioh
deuteron es megaron Laertiadeoh Oduseeos.
" ton de kholohsamenos prosefohneen Iros aleetees:
"oh popoi, ohs o molobros epitrokhadeen agoreuei,
greei kaminoi isos: on an kaka meetisaimeen
koptohn amfotereesi, khamai de ke pantas odontas
gnathmohn exelasaimi suos ohs leeiboteirees.
zohsai nun, ina pantes epignohohsi kai oide
marnamenous: pohs d᾽ an su neohteroh andri makhoio;
"

ohs oi men proparoithe thuraohn upseelaohn
oudou epi xestou panthumadon okrioohnto.
toiin de xuneeekh᾽ ieron menos Antinooio,
eedu d᾽ ar᾽ ekgelasas metefohnei mneesteeressin:
"

oh filoi, ou men poh ti paros toiouton etukhthee,
oieen terpohleen theos eegagen es tode dohma.
o xeinos te kai Iros erizeton alleeloiin
khersi makhessasthai: alla xunelassomen ohka.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes aneeixan geloohntes,
amfi d᾽ ara ptohkhous kakoeimonas eegerethonto.
toisin d᾽ Antinoos metefee, Eupeitheos uios:
"

keklute meu, mneesteeres ageenores, ofra ti eipoh.
gasteres aid᾽ aigohn keat᾽ en puri, tas epi dorpoh
katthemetha knisees te kai aimatos empleesantes:
oppoteros de ke nikeesee kreissohn te geneetai,
taohn een k᾽ etheleesin anastas autos elesthoh:
aiei auth᾽ eemin metadaisetai, oude tin᾽ allon
ptohkhon esoh misgesthai easomen aiteesonta.
"

ohs efat᾽ Antinoos, toisin d᾽ epieendane muthos.
tois de dolofroneohn metefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"

oh filoi, ou pohs esti neohteroh andri makhesthai
andra geronta, duee areemenon: alla me gasteer
otrunei kakoergos, ina pleegeesi dameioh.
all᾽ age nun moi pantes omossate karteron orkon,
mee tis ep᾽ Iroh eera ferohn eme kheiri bareiee
pleexee atasthallohn, toutoh de me ifi damassee.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes apohmnuon ohs ekeleuen.
autar epei r᾽ omosan te teleuteesan te ton orkon,
tois d᾽ autis meteeif᾽ ieree is Teelemakhoio:
"

xein᾽, ei s᾽ otrunei kradiee kai thumos ageenohr
touton alexasthai, tohn d᾽ allohn mee tin᾽ Akhaiohn
deidith᾽, epei pleonessi makheesetai os ke se theinee:
xeinodokos men egohn, epi d᾽ aineiton basileees,
Antinoos te kai Eurumakhos, pepnumenoh amfoh.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes epeeneon: autar Odusseus
zohsato men rakesin peri meedea, faine de meerous
kalous te megalous te, fanen de oi eurees ohmoi
steethea te stibaroi te brakhiones: autar Atheenee
agkhi paristamenee mele᾽ eeldane poimeni laohn.
mneesteeres d᾽ ara pantes uperfialohs agasanto:
ohde de tis eipesken idohn es pleesion allon:
"

ee takha Iros Airos epispaston kakon exei,
oieen ek rakeohn o gerohn epigounida fainei.
"

ohs ar᾽ efan, Iroh de kakohs ohrineto thumos.
alla kai ohs dreesteeres agon zohsantes anagkee
deidiota: sarkes de peritromeonto melessin.
Antinoos d᾽ enenipen epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomazen:
"

nun men meet᾽ eiees, bougaie, meete genoio,
ei dee touton ge tromeeis kai deidias ainohs,
andra geronta, duee areemenon, ee min ikanei.
all᾽ ek toi ereoh, to de kai tetelesmenon estai:
ai ken s᾽ outos nikeesee kreissohn te geneetai,
pempsoh s᾽ eepeironde, balohn en neei melainee,
eis Ekheton basileea, brotohn deeleemona pantohn,
os k᾽ apo rina tameesi kai ouata neelei khalkoh,
meedea t᾽ exerusas dohee kusin ohma dasasthai.
"

ohs fato, toh d᾽ eti mallon upo tromos ellabe guia.
es messon d᾽ anagon: toh d᾽ amfoh kheiras aneskhon.
dee tote mermeerixe polutlas dios Odusseus
ee elasei᾽ ohs min psukhee lipoi authi pesonta,
eee min eek᾽ elaseie tanusseien t᾽ epi gaiee.
ohde de oi froneonti doassato kerdion einai,
eek᾽ elasai, ina mee min epifrassaiat᾽ Akhaioi.
dee tot᾽ anaskhomenoh o men eelase dexion ohmon
Iros, o d᾽ aukhen᾽ elassen up᾽ ouatos, ostea d᾽ eisoh
ethlasen: autika d᾽ eelthe kata stoma foinion aima,
kad d᾽ epes᾽ en konieesi makohn, sun d᾽ eelas᾽ odontas
laktizohn posi gaian: atar mneesteeres agauoi
kheiras anaskhomenoi geloh ekthanon. autar Odusseus
elke diek prothuroio labohn podos, ofr᾽ iket᾽ auleen,
aithousees te thuras: kai min poti erkion aulees
eisen anaklinas: skeeptron de oi embale kheiri,
kai min fohneesas epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

entauthoi nun eeso suas te kunas t᾽ aperukohn,
meede su ge xeinohn kai ptohkhohn koiranos einai
lugros eohn, mee pou ti kakon kai meizon epauree.
"

ee ra kai amf᾽ ohmoisin aeikea balleto peereen,
pukna rohgaleeen: en de strofos eeen aorteer.
aps d᾽ o g᾽ ep᾽ oudon iohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezeto: toi d᾽ isan eisoh
eedu gelohontes kai deikanoohnt᾽ epeessi:
"

Zeus toi doiee, xeine, kai athanatoi theoi alloi,
otti malist᾽ etheleis kai toi filon epleto thumoh,
os touton ton analton aleeteuein apepausas
en deemoh: takha gar min anaxomen eepeironde
eis Ekheton basileea, brotohn deeleemona pantohn.
"

ohs ar᾽ efan, khairen de kleeedoni dios Odusseus.
Antinoos d᾽ ara oi megaleen para gastera theeken,
empleieen knisees te kai aimatos: Amfinomos de
artous ek kaneoio duoh paretheeken aeiras
kai depai khruseoh deidisketo, fohneesen te:
"

khaire, pater oh xeine, genoito toi es per opissoh
olbos: atar men nun ge kakois ekheai poleessi.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"Amfinom᾽, ee mala moi dokeeis pepnumenos einai:
toiou gar kai patros, epei kleos esthlon akouon,
Nison Doulikhieea eun t᾽ emen afneion te:
tou s᾽ ek fasi genesthai, epeetee d᾽ andri eoikas.
touneka toi ereoh, su de suntheo kai meu akouson:
ouden akidnoteron gaia trefei anthrohpoio,
pantohn ossa te gaian epi pneiei te kai erpei.
ou men gar pote feesi kakon peisesthai opissoh,
ofr᾽ areteen parekhohsi theoi kai gounat᾽ orohree:
all᾽ ote dee kai lugra theoi makares telesohsi,
kai ta ferei aekazomenos tetleeoti thumoh:
toios gar noos estin epikhthoniohn anthrohpohn
oion ep᾽ eemar ageesi pateer androhn te theohn te.
kai gar egoh pot᾽ emellon en andrasin olbios einai,
polla d᾽ atasthal᾽ erexa biee kai kartei eikohn,
patri t᾽ emoh pisunos kai emoisi kasigneetoisi.
toh mee tis pote pampan aneer athemistios eiee,
all᾽ o ge sigee dohra theohn ekhoi, otti didoien.
oi᾽ orooh mneesteeras atasthala meekhanoohntas,
kteemata keirontas kai atimazontas akoitin
andros, on ouketi feemi filohn kai patridos aiees
deeron apessesthai: mala de skhedon. alla se daimohn
oikad᾽ upexagagoi, meed᾽ antiaseias ekeinoh,
oppote nosteeseie fileen es patrida gaian:
ou gar anaimohti ge diakrineesthai oioh
mneesteeras kai keinon, epei ke melathron upelthee.
"

ohs fato, kai speisas epien melieedea oinon,
aps d᾽ en khersin etheeke depas kosmeetori laohn.
autar o bee dia dohma filon tetieemenos eetor,
neustazohn kefalee: dee gar kakon osseto thumos.
all᾽ oud᾽ ohs fuge keera: pedeese de kai ton Atheenee
Teelemakhou upo khersi kai egkhei ifi dameenai.
aps d᾽ autis kat᾽ ar᾽ ezet᾽ epi thronou enthen anestee.

tee d᾽ ar᾽ epi fresi theeke thea glaukohpis Atheenee,
kouree Ikarioio, perifroni Peenelopeiee,
mneesteeressi faneenai, opohs petaseie malista
thumon mneesteerohn ide timeeessa genoito
mallon pros posios te kai uieos ee paros eeen.
akhreion d᾽ egelassen epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomazen:
"

Eurunomee, thumos moi eeldetai, ou ti paros ge,
mneesteeressi faneenai, apekhthomenoisi per empees:
paidi de ken eipoimi epos, to ke kerdion eiee,
mee panta mneesteersin uperfialoisin omilein,
oi t᾽ eu men bazousi, kakohs d᾽ opithen froneousi.
"

teen d᾽ aut᾽ Eurunomee tamiee pros muthon eeipen:
"nai dee tauta ge panta, tekos, kata moiran eeipes.
all᾽ ithi kai soh paidi epos fao meed᾽ epikeuthe,
khroht᾽ aponipsamenee kai epikhrisasa pareias:
meed᾽ outoh dakruoisi pefurmenee amfi prosohpa
erkheu, epei kakion pentheemenai akriton aiei.
eedee men gar toi pais teelikos, on su malista
eeroh athanatoisi geneieesanta idesthai.
"

teen d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"Eurunomee, mee tauta parauda, keedomenee per,
khroht᾽ aponiptesthai kai epikhriesthai aloifee:
aglaieen gar emoi ge theoi, toi Olumpon ekhousin,
ohlesan, ex ou keinos ebee koilees eni neeusin.
alla moi Autonoeen te kai Ippodameian anohkhthi
elthemen, ofra ke moi parsteeeton en megaroisin:
oiee d᾽ ouk eiseimi met᾽ aneras: aideomai gar.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, greeus de diek megaroio bebeekei
aggeleousa gunaixi kai otruneousa neesthai.

enth᾽ aut᾽ all᾽ enoeese thea glaukohpis Atheenee:
kouree Ikarioio kata glukun upnon ekheuen,
eude d᾽ anaklintheisa, luthen de oi apsea panta
autou eni klinteeri: teohs d᾽ ara dia theaohn
ambrota dohra didou, ina min theesaiat᾽ Akhaioi.
kallei men oi prohta prosohpata kala katheeren
ambrosioh, oioh per eustefanos Kuthereia
khrietai, eut᾽ an iee Kharitohn khoron imeroenta:
kai min makrotereen kai passona theeken idesthai,
leukotereen d᾽ ara min theeke pristou elefantos.
ee men ar᾽ ohs erxas᾽ apebeeseto dia theaohn,
eelthon d᾽ amfipoloi leukohlenoi ek megaroio
fthoggoh eperkhomenai: teen de glukus upnos aneeke,
kai r᾽ apomorxato khersi pareias fohneesen te:
"

ee me mal᾽ ainopathee malakon peri kohm᾽ ekalupsen.
aithe moi ohs malakon thanaton poroi Artemis agnee
autika nun, ina meeket᾽ oduromenee kata thumon
aiohna fthinuthoh, posios potheousa filoio
pantoieen areteen, epei exokhos eeen Akhaiohn.
"

ohs famenee katebain᾽ uperohia sigaloenta,
ouk oiee: ama tee ge kai amfipoloi du᾽ eponto.
ee d᾽ ote dee mneesteeras afiketo dia gunaikohn,
stee ra para stathmon tegeos puka poieetoio,
anta pareiaohn skhomenee lipara kreedemna:
amfipolos d᾽ ara oi kednee ekaterthe parestee.
tohn d᾽ autou luto gounat᾽, eroh d᾽ ara thumon ethelkhthen,
pantes d᾽ eereesanto parai lekheessi klitheenai.
ee d᾽ au Teelemakhon prosefohneen, on filon uion:
"

Teelemakh᾽, ouketi toi frenes empedoi oude noeema:
pais et᾽ eohn kai mallon eni fresi kerde᾽ enohmas:
nun d᾽, ote dee megas essi kai eebees metron ikaneis,
kai ken tis faiee gonon emmenai olbiou andros,
es megethos kai kallos orohmenos, allotrios fohs,
ouketi toi frenes eisin enaisimoi oude noeema.
oion dee tode ergon eni megaroisin etukhthee,
os ton xeinon easas aeikistheemenai outohs.
pohs nun, ei ti xeinos en eemeteroisi domoisin
eemenos ohde pathoi rustaktuos ex alegeinees;
soi k᾽ aiskhos lohbee te met᾽ anthrohpoisi peloito.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"meeter emee, to men ou se nemessohmai kekholohsthai:
autar egoh thumoh noeoh kai oida ekasta,
esthla te kai ta khereia: paros d᾽ eti neepios eea.
alla toi ou dunamai pepnumena panta noeesai:
ek gar me pleessousi pareemenoi allothen allos
oide kaka froneontes, emoi d᾽ ouk eisin arohgoi.
ou men toi xeinou ge kai Irou mohlos etukhthee
mneesteerohn ioteeti, biee d᾽ o ge ferteros eeen.
ai gar, Zeu te pater kai Atheenaiee kai Apollon,
outoh nun mneesteeres en eemeteroisi domoisi
neuoien kefalas dedmeemenoi, oi men en aulee,
oi d᾽ entosthe domoio, leluto de guia ekastou,
ohs nun Iros keinos ep᾽ auleieesi thureesin
eestai neustazohn kefalee, methuonti eoikohs,
oud᾽ orthos steenai dunatai posin oude neesthai
oikad᾽, opee oi nostos, epei fila guia leluntai.
"

ohs oi men toiauta pros alleelous agoreuon:
Eurumakhos d᾽ epeessi proseeuda Peenelopeian:
"

kouree Ikarioio, perifron Peenelopeia,
ei pantes se idoien an᾽ Iason Argos Akhaioi,
pleones ke mneesteeres en umeteroisi domoisin
eeohthen dainuat᾽, epei periessi gunaikohn
eidos te megethos te ide frenas endon eisas.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"Eurumakh᾽, ee toi emeen areteen eidos te demas te
ohlesan athanatoi, ote Ilion eisanebainon
Argeioi, meta toisi d᾽ emos posis eeen Odusseus.
ei keinos g᾽ elthohn ton emon bion amfipoleuoi,
meizon ke kleos eiee emon kai kallion outohs.
nun d᾽ akhomai: tosa gar moi epesseuen kaka daimohn.
ee men dee ote t᾽ eee lipohn kata patrida gaian,
dexitereen epi karpoh elohn eme kheira proseeuda:
"

oh gunai, ou gar oioh eukneemidas Akhaious
ek Troiees eu pantas apeemonas aponeesthai:
kai gar Trohas fasi makheetas emmenai andras,
eemen akontistas eede ruteeras oistohn
ippohn t᾽ ohkupodohn epibeetoras, oi ke takhista
ekrinan mega neikos omoiiou polemoio.
toh ouk oid᾽ ee ken m᾽ anesei theos, ee ken alohoh
autou eni Troiee: soi d᾽ enthade panta melontohn.
memneesthai patros kai meeteros en megaroisin
ohs nun, ee eti mallon emeu aponosfin eontos:
autar epeen dee paida geneieesanta ideeai,
geemasth᾽ oh k᾽ etheleestha, teon kata dohma lipousa.
"

keinos tohs agoreue: ta dee nun panta teleitai.
nux d᾽ estai ote dee stugeros gamos antiboleesei
oulomenees emethen, tees te Zeus olbon apeeura.
alla tod᾽ ainon akhos kradieen kai thumon ikanei:
mneesteerohn oukh eede dikee to paroithe tetukto:
oi t᾽ agatheen te gunaika kai afneioio thugatra
mneesteuein ethelohsi kai alleelois erisohsin,
autoi toi g᾽ apagousi boas kai ifia meela,
kourees daita filoisi, kai aglaa dohra didousin:
all᾽ ouk allotrion bioton neepoinon edousin.
"

ohs fato, geetheesen de polutlas dios Odusseus,
ouneka tohn men dohra parelketo, thelge de thumon
meilikhiois epeessi, noos de oi alla menoina.

teen d᾽ aut᾽ Antinoos prosefee, Eupeitheos uios,
"kouree Ikarioio, perifron Peenelopeia,
dohra men os k᾽ etheleesin Akhaiohn enthad᾽ eneikai,
dexasth᾽. ou gar kalon aneenasthai dosin estin:
eemeis d᾽ out᾽ epi erga paros g᾽ imen oute pee allee,
prin ge se toh geemasthai Akhaiohn os tis aristos.
"

ohs efat᾽ Antinoos, toisin d᾽ epieendane muthos:
dohra d᾽ ar᾽ oisemenai proesan keeruka ekastos.
Antinooh men eneike megan perikallea peplon,
poikilon: en d᾽ ar᾽ esan peronai duokaideka pasai
khruseiai, kleeisin eugnamptois araruiai.
ormon d᾽ Eurumakhoh poludaidalon autik᾽ eneike.
khruseon, eelektroisin eermenon eeelion ohs.
ermata d᾽ Eurudamanti duoh therapontes eneikan,
trigleena moroenta: kharis d᾽ apelampeto pollee.
ek d᾽ ara Peisandroio Poluktoridao anaktos
isthmion eeneiken therapohn, perikalles agalma.
allo d᾽ ar᾽ allos dohron Akhaiohn kalon eneiken.
ee men epeit᾽ anebain᾽ uperohia dia gunaikohn,
tee d᾽ ar᾽ am᾽ amfipoloi eferon perikallea dohra

oi d᾽ eis orkheestun te kai imeroessan aoideen
trepsamenoi terponto, menon d᾽ epi esperon elthein.
toisi de terpomenoisi melas epi esperos eelthen.
autika lampteeras treis istasan en megaroisin,
ofra faeinoien: peri de xula kagkana theekan,
aua palai, perikeela, neon kekeasmena khalkoh,
kai daidas metemisgon: amoibeedis d᾽ anefainon
dmohai Odusseeos talasifronos. autar o teesin
autos diogenees metefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"

dmohai Odusseeos, deen oikhomenoio anaktos,
erkhesthe pros dohmath᾽, in᾽ aidoiee basileia:
tee de par᾽ eelakata strofalizete, terpete d᾽ auteen
eemenai en megaroh, ee eiria peikete khersin:
autar egoh toutoisi faos pantessi parexoh.
een per gar k᾽ ethelohsin euthronon Eeoh mimnein,
ou ti me nikeesousi: polutleemohn de mal᾽ eimi.
"

ohs efath᾽, ai d᾽ egelassan, es alleelas de idonto.
ton d᾽ aiskhrohs enenipe Melanthoh kallipareeos,
teen Dolios men etikte, komisse de Peenelopeia,
paida de ohs atitalle, didou d᾽ ar᾽ athurmata thumoh:
all᾽ oud᾽ ohs ekhe penthos eni fresi Peenelopeiees,
all᾽ ee g᾽ Eurumakhoh misgesketo kai fileesken.
ee r᾽ Odusee᾽ enenipen oneideiois epeessin:
"

xeine talan, su ge tis frenas ekpepatagmenos essi,
oud᾽ etheleis eudein khalkeeion es domon elthohn,
eee pou es leskheen, all᾽ enthade poll᾽ agoreueis,
tharsaleohs polloisi met᾽ andrasin, oude ti thumoh
tarbeis: ee ra se oinos ekhei frenas, ee nu toi aiei
toioutos noos estin: o kai metamohnia bazeis.
ee alueis, oti Iron enikeesas ton aleeteen;
mee tis toi takha Irou ameinohn allos anastee,
os tis s᾽ amfi karee kekopohs khersi stibareesi
dohmatos ekpempseesi, foruxas aimati polloh.
"

teen d᾽ ar᾽ upodra idohn prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"ee takha Teelemakhoh ereoh, kuon, oi᾽ agoreueis,
keis᾽ elthohn, ina s᾽ authi dia meleisti tameesin.
"

ohs eipohn epeessi dieptoieese gunaikas.
ban d᾽ imenai dia dohma, luthen d᾽ upo guia ekastees
tarbosunee: fan gar min aleethea mutheesasthai.
autar o par lampteersi faeinohn aithomenoisin
esteekein es pantas orohmenos: alla de oi keer
ohrmaine fresin eesin, a r᾽ ouk atelesta genonto.

mneesteeras d᾽ ou pampan ageenoras eia Atheenee
lohbees iskhesthai thumalgeos, ofr᾽ eti mallon
duee akhos kradieen Laertiadeoh Oduseeos.
toisin d᾽ Eurumakhos, Polubou pais, eerkh᾽ agoreuein,
kertomeohn Oduseea: geloh d᾽ etaroisin eteukhe.
"

keklute meu, mneesteeres agakleitees basileiees,
ofr᾽ eipoh ta me thumos eni steethessi keleuei.
ouk atheei od᾽ aneer Oduseeion es domon ikei:
empees moi dokeei daidohn selas emmenai autou
kak kefalees, epei ou oi eni trikhes oud᾽ eebaiai.
"

ee r᾽, ama te proseeipen Odusseea ptoliporthon:
"xein᾽, ee ar k᾽ ethelois theeteuemen, ei s᾽ aneloimeen,
agrou ep᾽ eskhatiees--misthos de toi arkios estai--
aimasias te legohn kai dendrea makra futeuohn;
entha k᾽ egoh siton men epeeetanon parekhoimi,
eimata d᾽ amfiesaimi posin th᾽ upodeemata doieen.
all᾽ epei oun dee erga kak᾽ emmathes, ouk etheleeseis
ergon epoikhesthai, alla ptohssein kata deemon
bouleai, ofr᾽ an ekhees boskein seen gaster᾽ analton.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"Eurumakh᾽, ei gar nohin eris ergoio genoito
ohree en eiarinee, ote t᾽ eemata makra pelontai,
en poiee, drepanon men egohn eukampes ekhoimi,
kai de su toion ekhois, ina peireesaimetha ergou
neesties akhri mala knefaos, poiee de pareiee.
ei d᾽ au kai boes eien elaunemen, oi per aristoi,
aithohnes, megaloi, amfoh kekoreeote poiees,
eelikes, isoforoi, tohn te sthenos ouk alapadnon,
tetraguon d᾽ eiee, eikoi d᾽ upo bohlos arotroh:
toh ke m᾽ idois, ei ohlka dieenekea protamoimeen.
ei d᾽ au kai polemon pothen ormeeseie Kroniohn
seemeron, autar emoi sakos eiee kai duo doure
kai kuneee pagkhalkos, epi krotafois araruia,
toh ke m᾽ idois prohtoisin eni promakhoisi migenta,
oud᾽ an moi teen gaster᾽ oneidizohn agoreuois.
alla mal᾽ ubrixeis, kai toi noos estin apeenees:
kai pou tis dokeeis megas emmenai eede krataios,
ouneka par pauroisi kai ouk agathoisin omileis.
ei d᾽ Oduseus elthoi kai ikoit᾽ es patrida gaian,
aipsa ke toi ta thuretra, kai eurea per mal᾽ eonta,
feugonti steinoito diek prothuroio thuraze.
"

ohs efat᾽, Eurumakhos d᾽ ekholohsato keerothi mallon,
kai min upodra idohn epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

a deil᾽, ee takha toi teleoh kakon, oi᾽ agoreueis
tharsaleohs polloisi met᾽ andrasin, oude ti thumoh
tarbeis: ee ra se oinos ekhei frenas, ee nu toi aiei
toioutos noos estin: o kai metamohnia bazeis.
ee alueis, oti Iron enikeesas ton aleeteen;
"

ohs ara fohneesas sfelas ellaben: autar Odusseus
Amfinomou pros gouna kathezeto Doulikhieeos,
Eurumakhon deisas: o d᾽ ar᾽ oinokhoon bale kheira
dexitereen: prokhoos de khamai bombeese pesousa,
autar o g᾽ oimohxas pesen uptios en konieesi.
mneesteeres d᾽ omadeesan ana megara skioenta,
ohde de tis eipesken idohn es pleesion allon:
"

aith᾽ ohfell᾽ o xeinos alohmenos alloth᾽ olesthai
prin elthein: toh ou ti toson keladon metetheeke.
nun de peri ptohkhohn eridainomen, oude ti daitos
esthlees essetai eedos, epei ta khereiona nika.
" toisi de kai meteeif᾽ ieree is Teelemakhoio
"daimonioi, mainesthe kai ouketi keuthete thumoh
brohtun oude poteeta: theohn nu tis umm᾽ orothunei.
all᾽ eu daisamenoi katakeiete oikad᾽ iontes,
oppote thumos anohge: diohkoh d᾽ ou tin᾽ egoh ge.
"

ohs efath᾽, oi d᾽ ara pantes odax en kheilesi funtes
Teelemakhon thaumazon, o tharsaleohs agoreue.
toisin d᾽ Amfinomos agoreesato kai meteeipe
Nisou faidimos uios, Areetiadao anaktos:
"

oh filoi, ouk an dee tis epi reethenti dikaioh
antibiois epeessi kathaptomenos khalepainoi:
meete ti ton xeinon stufelizete meete tin᾽ allon
dmohohn, oi kata dohmat᾽ Odusseeos theioio.
all᾽ aget᾽, oinokhoos men eparxasthoh depaessin,
ofra speisantes katakeiomen oikad᾽ iontes:
ton xeinon de eohmen eni megarois Oduseeos
Teelemakhoh melemen: tou gar filon iketo dohma.
"

ohs fato, toisi de pasin eadota muthon eeipe.
toisin de kreeteera kerassato Moulios eerohs,
keerux Doulikhieus: therapohn d᾽ een Amfinomoio:
nohmeesen d᾽ ara pasin epistadon: oi de theoisi
speisantes makaressi pion melieedea oinon.
autar epei speisan t᾽ epion th᾽ oson eethele thumos,
ban r᾽ imenai keiontes ea pros dohmath᾽ ekastos.


Book 19
-------

autar o en megaroh upeleipeto dios Odusseus,
mneesteeressi fonon sun Atheenee mermeerizohn:
aipsa de Teelemakhon epea pteroenta proseeuda:
"

Teelemakhe, khree teukhe᾽ areeia katthemen eisoh
panta mal᾽: autar mneesteeras malakois epeessi
parfasthai, ote ken se metallohsin potheontes:
"ek kapnou katetheek᾽, epei ouketi toisin eohkei
oia pote Troieende kiohn kateleipen Odusseus,
alla kateekistai, osson puros iket᾽ autmee.
pros d᾽ eti kai tode meizon eni fresin ebale daimohn
mee pohs oinohthentes, erin steesantes en umin,
alleelous trohseete kataiskhuneete te daita
kai mneestun: autos gar efelketai andra sideeros.
""

ohs fato, Teelemakhos de filoh epepeitheto patri,
ek de kalessamenos prosefee trofon Eurukleian:
"

mai᾽, age dee moi eruxon eni megaroisi gunaikas,
ofra ken es thalamon katatheiomai entea patros
kala, ta moi kata oikon akeedea kapnos amerdei
patros apoikhomenoio: egoh d᾽ eti neepios eea.
nun d᾽ etheloh katathesthai, in᾽ ou puros ixet᾽ autmee.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe filee trofos Eurukleia:
"ai gar dee pote, teknon, epifrosunas aneloio
oikou keedesthai kai kteemata panta fulassein.
all᾽ age, tis toi epeita metoikhomenee faos oisei;
dmohas d᾽ ouk eias problohskemen, ai ken efainon.
"

teen d᾽ au Teelemakhos pepnumenos antion eeuda:
"xeinos od᾽: ou gar aergon anexomai os ken emees ge
khoinikos apteetai, kai teelothen eileelouthohs.
"

ohs ar᾽ efohneesen, tee d᾽ apteros epleto muthos.
kleeisen de thuras megarohn eu naietaontohn.
toh d᾽ ar᾽ anaixant᾽ Oduseus kai faidimos uios
esforeon koruthas te kai aspidas omfaloessas
egkhea t᾽ oxuoenta: paroithe de Pallas Atheenee,
khruseon lukhnon ekhousa, faos perikalles epoiei.
dee tote Teelemakhos prosefohneen on pater᾽ aipsa:
"

oh pater, ee mega thauma tod᾽ ofthalmoisin orohmai.
empees moi toikhoi megarohn kalai te mesodmai,
eilatinai te dokoi, kai kiones upsos᾽ ekhontes
fainont᾽ ofthalmois ohs ei puros aithomenoio.
ee mala tis theos endon, oi ouranon eurun ekhousi.
"

ton d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"siga kai kata son noon iskhane meed᾽ ereeine:
autee toi dikee esti theohn, oi Olumpon ekhousin.
alla su men katalexai, egoh d᾽ upoleipsomai autou,
ofra k᾽ eti dmohas kai meetera seen erethizoh:
ee de m᾽ oduromenee eireesetai amfis ekasta.
"

ohs fato, Teelemakhos de diek megaroio bebeekei
keiohn es thalamon, daidohn upo lampomenaohn,
entha paros koimath᾽, ote min glukus upnos ikanoi:
enth᾽ ara kai tot᾽ elekto kai Eeoh dian emimnen.
autar o en megaroh upeleipeto dios Odusseus,
mneesteeressi fonon sun Atheenee mermeerizohn.

ee d᾽ ien ek thalamoio perifrohn Peenelopeia,
Artemidi ikelee eee khruseee Afroditee.
tee para men klisieen puri katthesan, enth᾽ ar᾽ efize,
dinohteen elefanti kai arguroh: een pote tektohn
poiees᾽ Ikmalios, kai upo threenun posin eeke
prosfue᾽ ex autees, oth᾽ epi mega balleto kohas.
entha kathezet᾽ epeita perifrohn Peenelopeia.
eelthon de dmohai leukohlenoi ek megaroio.
ai d᾽ apo men siton polun eereon eede trapezas
kai depa, enthen ar᾽ andres upermeneontes epinon:
pur d᾽ apo lampteerohn khamadis balon, alla d᾽ ep᾽ autohn
neeeesan xula polla, foohs emen eede theresthai.
ee d᾽ Odusee᾽ enenipe Melanthoh deuteron autis:
"xein᾽, eti kai nun enthad᾽ anieeseis dia nukta
dineuohn kata oikon, opipeuseis de gunaikas;
all᾽ exelthe thuraze, talan, kai daitos oneeso:
ee takha kai daloh bebleemenos eistha thuraze.
"

teen d᾽ ar᾽ upodra idohn prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"daimoniee, ti moi ohd᾽ epekheis kekoteeoti thumoh;
ee oti dee rupooh, kaka de khroi eimata eimai,
ptohkheuoh d᾽ ana deemon; anagkaiee gar epeigei.
toioutoi ptohkhoi kai aleemones andres easi
kai gar egoh pote oikon en anthrohpoisin enaion
olbios afneion kai pollaki doskon aleetee,
toioh opoios eoi kai oteu kekhreemenos elthoi:
eesan de dmohes mala murioi, alla te polla
oisin t᾽ eu zohousi kai afneioi kaleontai.
alla Zeus alapaxe Kroniohn: eethele gar pou:
toh nun meepote kai su, gunai, apo pasan olessees
aglaieen, tee nun ge meta dmoheesi kekassai:
mee pohs toi despoina kotessamenee khalepeenee,
ee Oduseus elthee: eti gar kai elpidos aisa.
ei d᾽ o men ohs apolohle kai ouketi nostimos estin,
all᾽ eedee pais toios Apollohnos ge ekeeti,
Teelemakhos: ton d᾽ ou tis eni megaroisi gunaikohn
leethei atasthallous᾽, epei ouketi teelikos estin.
"

ohs fato, tou d᾽ eekouse perifrohn Peenelopeia,
amfipolon d᾽ enenipen epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomaze:
"

pantohs, tharsaleee, kuon adees, ou ti me leetheis
erdousa mega ergon, o see kefalee anamaxeis:
panta gar eu eedeesth᾽, epei ex emeu eklues autees
ohs ton xeinon emellon eni megaroisin emoisin
amfi posei eiresthai, epei pukinohs akakheemai.
"

ee ra kai Eurunomeen tamieen pros muthon eeipen:
"Eurunomee, fere dee difron kai kohas ep᾽ autou,
ofra kathezomenos eipee epos eed᾽ epakousee
o xeinos emethen: etheloh de min exereesthai.
" ohs efath᾽, ee de mal᾽ otraleohs katetheeke ferousa
difron euxeston kai ep᾽ autoh kohas eballen:
entha kathezet᾽ epeita polutlas dios Odusseus.
toisi de muthohn eerkhe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"

xeine, to men se prohton egohn eireesomai autee:
tis pothen eis androhn; pothi toi polis eede tokeees;
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai, ouk an tis se brotohn ep᾽ apeirona gaian
neikeoi: ee gar seu kleos ouranon eurun ikanei,
ohs te teu ee basileeos amumonos, os te theoudees
andrasin en polloisi kai ifthimoisin anassohn
eudikias anekheesi, fereesi de gaia melaina
purous kai krithas, britheesi de dendrea karpoh,
tiktee d᾽ empeda meela, thalassa de parekhee ikhthus
ex eueegesiees, aretohsi de laoi up᾽ autou.
toh eme nun ta men alla metalla soh eni oikoh,
meed᾽ emon exereeine genos kai patrida gaian,
mee moi mallon thumon enipleesees odunaohn
mneesamenoh mala d᾽ eimi polustonos: oude ti me khree
oikoh en allotrioh gooohnta te muromenon te
eesthai, epei kakion pentheemenai akriton aiei:
mee tis moi dmohohn nemeseesetai, eee su g᾽ autee,
fee de dakruplohein bebareeota me frenas oinoh.
"

ton d᾽ eemeibet᾽ epeita perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"xein᾽, ee toi men emeen areteen eidos te demas te
ohlesan athanatoi, ote Ilion eisanebainon
Argeioi, meta toisi d᾽ emos posis eeen Odusseus
ei keinos g᾽ elthohn ton emon bion amfipoleuoi,
meizon ke kleos eiee emon kai kallion outohs.
nun d᾽ akhomai: tosa gar moi epesseuen kaka daimohn.
ossoi gar neesoisin epikrateousin aristoi,
Doulikhioh te Samee te kai uleeenti Zakunthoh,
oi t᾽ auteen Ithakeen eudeielon amfinemontai,
oi m᾽ aekazomeneen mnohntai, trukhousi de oikon.
toh oute xeinohn empaxomai outh᾽ iketaohn
oute ti keerukohn, oi deemioergoi easin:
all᾽ Odusee potheousa filon katateekomai eetor.
oi de gamon speudousin: egoh de dolous tolupeuoh.
faros men moi prohton enepneuse fresi daimohn,
steesamenee megan iston, eni megaroisin ufainein,
lepton kai perimetron: afar d᾽ autois meteeipon:
"

kouroi, emoi mneesteeres, epei thane dios Odusseus,
mimnet᾽ epeigomenoi ton emon gamon, eis o ke faros
ektelesoh--mee moi metamohnia neemat᾽ oleetai--
Laertee eerohi tafeeion, eis ote ken min
moir᾽ oloee katheleesi taneelegeos thanatoio:
mee tis moi kata deemon Akhaiiadohn nemeseesee,
ai ken ater speirou keitai polla kteatissas.
"

ohs efameen, toisin d᾽ epepeitheto thumos ageenohr.
entha kai eematiee men ufaineskon megan iston,
nuktas d᾽ allueskon, epei daidas paratheimeen.
ohs trietes men eleethon egoh kai epeithon Akhaious:
all᾽ ote tetraton eelthen etos kai epeeluthon ohrai,
meenohn fthinontohn, peri d᾽ eemata poll᾽ etelesthee,
kai tote dee me dia dmohas, kunas ouk alegousas,
eilon epelthontes kai omokleesan epeessin.
ohs to men exetelessa, kai ouk ethelous᾽, up᾽ anagkees:
nun d᾽ out᾽ ekfugeein dunamai gamon oute tin᾽ alleen
meetin eth᾽ euriskoh: mala d᾽ otrunousi tokeees
geemasth᾽, askhalaa de pais bioton katedontohn,
gignohskohn: eedee gar aneer oios te malista
oikou keedesthai, toh te Zeus kudos opazei.
alla kai ohs moi eipe teon genos, oppothen essi.
ou gar apo druos essi palaifatou oud᾽ apo petrees.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai aidoiee Laertiadeoh Oduseeos,
ouket᾽ apolleexeis ton emon gonon exereousa;
all᾽ ek toi ereoh: ee men m᾽ akheessi ge dohseis
pleiosin ee ekhomai: ee gar dikee, oppote patrees
ees apeeesin aneer tosson khronon osson egoh nun,
polla brotohn epi aste᾽ alohmenos, algea paskhohn:
alla kai ohs ereoh o m᾽ aneireai eede metallas.
Kreetee tis gai᾽ esti, mesoh eni oinopi pontoh,
kalee kai pieira, perirrutos: en d᾽ anthrohpoi
polloi, apeiresioi, kai enneekonta poleees.
allee d᾽ allohn glohssa memigmenee: en men Akhaioi,
en d᾽ Eteokreetes megaleetores, en de Kudohnes,
Dohriees te trikhaikes dioi te Pelasgoi.
teesi d᾽ eni Knohsos, megalee polis, entha te Minohs
enneohros basileue Dios megalou oaristees,
patros emoio pateer, megathumou Deukaliohnos
Deukaliohn d᾽ eme tikte kai Idomeneea anakta:
all᾽ o men en neeessi korohnisin Ilion isoh
ohkheth᾽ am᾽ Atreideesin, emoi d᾽ onoma kluton Aithohn,
oploteros geneee: o d᾽ ara proteros kai areiohn.
enth᾽ Oduseea egohn idomeen kai xeinia dohka.
kai gar ton Kreeteende kateegagen is anemoio,
iemenon Troieende paraplagxasa Maleiohn:
steese d᾽ en Amnisoh, othi te speos Eileithuiees,
en limesin khalepoisi, mogis d᾽ upaluxen aellas.
autika d᾽ Idomeneea metalla astud᾽ anelthohn:
xeinon gar oi efaske filon t᾽ emen aidoion te.
toh d᾽ eedee dekatee ee endekatee pelen eeohs
oikhomenoh sun neeusi korohnisin Ilion eisoh.
ton men egoh pros dohmat᾽ agohn eu exeinissa,
endukeohs fileohn, pollohn kata oikon eontohn:
kai oi tois allois etarois, oi am᾽ autoh eponto,
deemothen alfita dohka kai aithopa oinon ageiras
kai bous ireusasthai, ina pleesaiato thumon.
entha duohdeka men menon eemata dioi Akhaioi:
eilei gar Boreees anemos megas oud᾽ epi gaiee
eia istasthai, khalepos de tis ohrore daimohn.
tee triskaidekatee d᾽ anemos pese, toi d᾽ anagonto.
"

iske pseudea polla legohn etumoisin omoia:
tees d᾽ ar᾽ akouousees ree dakrua, teeketo de khrohs:
ohs de khiohn katateeket᾽ en akropoloisin oressin,
een t᾽ Euros kateteexen, epeen Zefuros katakheuee:
teekomenees d᾽ ara tees potamoi pleethousi reontes:
ohs tees teeketo kala pareeia dakru kheousees,
klaiousees eon andra pareemenon. autar Odusseus
thumoh men gooohsan eeen eleaire gunaika,
ofthalmoi d᾽ ohs ei kera estasan eee sideeros
atremas en blefaroisi: doloh d᾽ o ge dakrua keuthen.
ee d᾽ epei oun tarfthee poludakrutoio gooio,
exautis min epessin ameibomenee proseeipe:
"

nun men dee seu, xeine g᾽, oioh peireesesthai,
ei eteon dee keithi sun antitheois etaroisi
xeinisas en megaroisin emon posin, ohs agoreueis.
eipe moi oppoi᾽ assa peri khroi eimata esto,
autos th᾽ oios eeen, kai etairous, oi oi eponto.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai, argaleon tosson khronon amfis eonta
eipemen: eedee gar oi eeikoston etos estin
ex ou keithen ebee kai emees apeleeluthe patrees:
autar toi ereoh ohs moi indalletai eetor.
khlainan porfureeen ouleen ekhe dios Odusseus,
dipleen: autar oi peronee khrusoio tetukto
auloisin didumoisi: paroithe de daidalon eeen:
en proteroisi podessi kuohn ekhe poikilon ellon,
aspaironta laohn: to de thaumazeskon apantes,
ohs oi khruseoi eontes o men lae nebron apagkhohn,
autar o ekfugeein memaohs eespaire podessi.
ton de khitohn᾽ enoeesa peri khroi sigaloenta,
oion te kromuoio lopon kata iskhaleoio:
tohs men eeen malakos, lampros d᾽ een eeelios ohs:
ee men pollai g᾽ auton etheeeesanto gunaikes.
allo de toi ereoh, su d᾽ eni fresi balleo seesin:
ouk oid᾽ ee tade esto peri khroi oikoth᾽ Odusseus,
ee tis etairohn dohke thoees epi neeos ionti,
ee tis pou kai xeinos, epei polloisin Odusseus
eske filos: pauroi gar Akhaiohn eesan omoioi.
kai oi egoh khalkeion aor kai diplaka dohka
kaleen porfureeen kai termioenta khitohna,
aidoiohs d᾽ apepempon eusselmou epi neeos.
kai men oi keerux oligon progenesteros autou
eipeto: kai ton toi mutheesomai, oios eeen per.
guros en ohmoisin, melanokhroos, oulokareenos,
Eurubatees d᾽ onom᾽ eske: tien de min exokhon allohn
ohn etarohn Oduseus, oti oi fresin artia eedee.
"

ohs fato, tee d᾽ eti mallon uf᾽ imeron ohrse gooio,
seemat᾽ anagnousee ta oi empeda pefrad᾽ Odusseus.
ee d᾽ epei oun tarfthee poludakrutoio gooio.
kai tote min muthoisin ameibomenee proseeipe:
"

nun men dee moi, xeine, paros per eohn eleeinos,
en megaroisin emoisi filos t᾽ esee aidoios te:
autee gar tade eimat᾽ egoh poron, oi᾽ agoreueis,
ptuxas᾽ ek thalamou, peroneen t᾽ epetheeka faeineen
keinoh agalm᾽ emenai: ton d᾽ oukh upodexomai autis
oikade nosteesanta fileen es patrida gaian.
toh ra kakee aisee koilees epi neeos Odusseus
ohkhet᾽ epopsomenos Kakoilion ouk onomasteen.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai aidoiee Laertiadeoh Oduseeos,
meeketi nun khroa kalon enaireo, meede ti thumon
teeke, posin gooohsa. nemessohmai ge men ouden:
kai gar tis t᾽ alloion oduretai andr᾽ olesasa
kouridion, toh tekna tekee filoteeti migeisa,
ee Odusee᾽, on fasi theois enaligkion einai.
alla goou men pausai, emeio de suntheo muthon:
neemerteohs gar toi mutheesomai oud᾽ epikeusoh
ohs eedee Oduseeos egoh peri nostou akousa
agkhou, Thesprohtohn androhn en pioni deemoh,
zohou: autar agei keimeelia polla kai esthla
aitizohn ana deemon. atar erieeras etairous
ohlese kai neea glafureen eni oinopi pontoh,
Thrinakiees apo neesou iohn: odusanto gar autoh
Zeus te kai Eeelios: tou gar boas ektan etairoi.
oi men pantes olonto poluklustoh eni pontoh:
ton d᾽ ar᾽ epi tropios neos ekbale kum᾽ epi khersou,
Faieekohn es gaian, oi agkhitheoi gegaasin,
oi dee min peri keeri theon ohs timeesanto
kai oi polla dosan pempein te min eethelon autoi
oikad᾽ apeemanton. kai ken palai enthad᾽ Odusseus
eeeen: all᾽ ara oi to ge kerdion eisato thumoh,
khreemat᾽ agurtazein polleen epi gaian ionti:
ohs peri kerdea polla katathneetohn anthrohpohn
oid᾽ Oduseus, oud᾽ an tis erisseie brotos allos.
ohs moi Thesprohtohn basileus mutheesato Feidohn:
ohmnue de pros em᾽ auton, apospendohn eni oikoh,
neea kateirusthai kai eparteas emmen etairous,
oi dee min pempsousi fileen es patrida gaian.
all᾽ eme prin apepempse: tukheese gar erkhomenee neeus
androhn Thesprohtohn es Doulikhion polupuron.
kai moi kteemat᾽ edeixen, osa xunageirat᾽ Odusseus:
kai nu ken es dekateen geneeen eteron g᾽ eti boskoi,
ossa oi en megarois keimeelia keito anaktos.
ton d᾽ es Dohdohneen fato beemenai, ofra theoio
ek druos upsikomoio Dios bouleen epakousai,
oppohs nosteeseie fileen es patrida gaian
eedee deen apeohn, ee amfadon eee krufeedon.
ohs o men outohs esti soos kai eleusetai eedee
agkhi mal᾽, oud᾽ eti teele filohn kai patridos aiees
deeron apesseitai: empees de toi orkia dohsoh.
istoh nun Zeus prohta, theohn upatos kai aristos,
istiee t᾽ Oduseeos amumonos, een afikanoh:
ee men toi tade panta teleietai ohs agoreuoh.
toud᾽ autou lukabantos eleusetai enthad᾽ Odusseus,
tou men fthinontos meenos, tou d᾽ istamenoio.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"ai gar touto, xeine, epos tetelesmenon eiee:
toh ke takha gnoiees filoteeta te polla te dohra
ex emeu, ohs an tis se sunantomenos makarizoi.
alla moi ohd᾽ ana thumon oietai, ohs esetai per:
out᾽ Oduseus eti oikon eleusetai, oute su pompees
teuxee, epei ou toioi seemantores eis᾽ eni oikoh
oios Odusseus eske met᾽ andrasin, ei pot᾽ eeen ge,
xeinous aidoious apopempemen eede dekhesthai.
alla min, amfipoloi, aponipsate, katthete d᾽ euneen,
demnia kai khlainas kai reegea sigaloenta,
ohs k᾽ eu thalpioohn khrusothronon Eeoh ikeetai.
eeohthen de mal᾽ eeri loessai te khrisai te,
ohs k᾽ endon para Teelemakhoh deipnoio medeetai
eemenos en megaroh: toh d᾽ algion os ken ekeinohn
touton aniazee thumofthoros: oude ti ergon
enthad᾽ eti preexei, mala per kekholohmenos ainohs.
pohs gar emeu su, xeine, daeeseai ei ti gunaikohn
allaohn perieimi noon kai epifrona meetin,
ei ken austaleos, kaka eimenos en megaroisin
dainuee; anthrohpoi de minunthadioi telethousin.
os men apeenees autos eee kai apeenea eidee,
toh de katarohntai pantes brotoi alge᾽ opissoh
zohoh, atar tethneohti g᾽ efepsioohntai apantes:
os d᾽ an amumohn autos eee kai amumona eidee,
tou men te kleos euru dia xeinoi foreousi
pantas ep᾽ anthrohpous, polloi te min esthlon eeipon.
" teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai aidoiee Laertiadeoh Oduseeos,
ee toi emoi khlainai kai reegea sigaloenta
eekhtheth᾽, ote prohton Kreetees orea nifoenta
nosfisameen epi neeos iohn dolikheeretmoio,
keioh d᾽ ohs to paros per aupnous nuktas iauon:
pollas gar dee nuktas aeikelioh eni koitee
aesa kai t᾽ anemeina euthronon Eeoh dian.
oude ti moi podaniptra podohn epieerana thumoh
gignetai: oude gunee podos apsetai eemeteroio
taohn ai toi dohma kata dreesteirai easin,
ei mee tis greeus esti palaiee, kedna iduia,
ee tis dee tetleeke tosa fresin ossa t᾽ egoh per:
tee d᾽ ouk an fthoneoimi podohn apsasthai emeio.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"xeine fil᾽: ou gar poh tis aneer pepnumenos ohde
xeinohn teeledapohn filiohn emon iketo dohma,
ohs su mal᾽ eufradeohs pepnumena pant᾽ agoreueis:
esti de moi greeus pukina fresi meede᾽ ekhousa
ee keinon dusteenon eu trefen eed᾽ atitalle,
dexamenee kheiress᾽, ote min prohton teke meeteer,
ee se podas nipsei, oligeepeleousa per empees.
all᾽ age nun anstasa, perifrohn Eurukleia,
nipson soio anaktos omeelika: kai pou Odusseus
eedee toiosd᾽ esti podas toiosde te kheiras:
aipsa gar en kakoteeti brotoi katageeraskousin.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, greeus de kateskheto khersi prosohpa,
dakrua d᾽ ekbale therma, epos d᾽ olofudnon eeipen:
"

oh moi egoh seo, teknon, ameekhanos: ee se peri Zeus
anthrohpohn eekhtheere theoudea thumon ekhonta.
ou gar poh tis tossa brotohn Dii terpikeraunoh
piona meeri᾽ ekee᾽ oud᾽ exaitous ekatombas,
ossa su toh edidous, arohmenos eeos ikoio
geeras te liparon threpsaio te faidimon uion:
nun de toi oioh pampan afeileto nostimon eemar.
outoh pou kai keinoh efepsioohnto gunaikes
xeinohn teeledapohn, ote teu kluta dohmath᾽ ikoito,
ohs sethen ai kunes aide kathepsioohntai apasai,
taohn nun lohbeen te kai aiskhea poll᾽ aleeinohn
ouk eaas nizein: eme d᾽ ouk aekousan anohge
kouree Ikarioio, perifrohn Peenelopeia.
toh se podas nipsoh ama t᾽ autees Peenelopeiees
kai sethen einek᾽, epei moi orohretai endothi thumos
keedesin. all᾽ age nun xuniei epos, otti ken eipoh:
polloi dee xeinoi talapeirioi enthad᾽ ikonto,
all᾽ ou poh tina feemi eoikota ohde idesthai
ohs su demas fohneen te podas t᾽ Oduseei eoikas.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh greeu, outoh fasin osoi idon ofthalmoisin
eemeas amfoterous, mala eikeloh alleeloiin
emmenai, ohs su per autee epifroneous᾽ agoreueis.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, greeus de lebeeth᾽ ele pamfanoohnta
tou podas exapenizen, udohr d᾽ enekheuato poulu
psukhron, epeita de thermon epeefusen. autar Odusseus
izen ep᾽ eskharofin, poti de skoton etrapet᾽ aipsa:
autika gar kata thumon oisato, mee e labousa
ouleen amfrassaito kai amfada erga genoito.
nize d᾽ ar᾽ asson iousa anakhth᾽ eon: autika d᾽ egnoh
ouleen, teen pote min sus eelase leukoh odonti
Parneesond᾽ elthonta met᾽ Autolukon te kai uias,
meetros eees pater᾽ esthlon, os anthrohpous ekekasto
kleptosunee th᾽ orkoh te: theos de oi autos edohken
Ermeias: toh gar kekharismena meeria kaien
arnohn eed᾽ erifohn: o de oi profrohn am᾽ opeedei.
Autolukos d᾽ elthohn Ithakees es piona deemon
paida neon gegaohta kikheesato thugateros ees:
ton ra oi Eurukleia filois epi gounasi theeke
pauomenoh dorpoio, epos t᾽ efat᾽ ek t᾽ onomazen:
"

Autoluk᾽, autos nun onom᾽ eureo otti ke theeai
paidos paidi filoh: poluareetos de toi estin.
" teen d᾽ aut᾽ Autolukos apameibeto fohneesen te:
"gambros emos thugateer te, tithesth᾽ onom᾽ otti ken eipoh:
polloisin gar egoh ge odussamenos tod᾽ ikanoh,
andrasin eede gunaixin ana khthona pouluboteiran:
toh d᾽ Oduseus onom᾽ estoh epohnumon: autar egoh ge,
oppot᾽ an eebeesas meetrohion es mega dohma
elthee Parneesond᾽, othi pou moi kteemat᾽ easi,
tohn oi egoh dohsoh kai min khairont᾽ apopempsoh.
"

tohn enek᾽ eelth᾽ Oduseus, ina oi poroi aglaa dohra.
ton men ar᾽ Autolukos te kai uiees Autolukoio
khersin t᾽ eespazonto epessi te meilikhioisi:
meeteer d᾽ Amfitheee meetros perifus᾽ Oduseei
kuss᾽ ara min kefaleen te kai amfoh faea kala.
Autolukos d᾽ uioisin ekekleto kudalimoisi
deipnon efoplissai: toi d᾽ otrunontos akousan,
autika d᾽ eisagagon boun arsena pentaeteeron:
ton deron amfi th᾽ epon, kai min diekheuan apanta,
mistullon t᾽ ar᾽ epistamenohs peiran t᾽ obeloisin,
ohpteesan te perifradeohs, dassanto te moiras.
ohs tote men propan eemar es eeelion katadunta
dainunt᾽, oude ti thumos edeueto daitos eisees:
eemos d᾽ eeelios katedu kai epi knefas eelthen,
dee tote koimeesanto kai upnou dohron elonto.

eemos d᾽ eerigeneia fanee rododaktulos Eeohs,
ban r᾽ imen es theereen, eemen kunes eede kai autoi
uiees Autolukou: meta toisi de dios Odusseus
eeien: aipu d᾽ oros proseban kataeimenon ulee
Parneesou, takha d᾽ ikanon ptukhas eenemoessas.
Eeelios men epeita neon proseballen arouras
ex akalarreitao bathurroou Ohkeanoio,
oi d᾽ es beessan ikanon epakteeres: pro d᾽ ar᾽ autohn
ikhni᾽ ereunohntes kunes eeisan, autar opisthen
uiees Autolukou: meta toisi de dios Odusseus
eeien agkhi kunohn, kradaohn dolikhoskion egkhos.
entha d᾽ ar᾽ en lokhmee pukinee katekeito megas sus:
teen men ar᾽ out᾽ anemohn diaei menos ugron aentohn,
oute min Eeelios faethohn aktisin eballen,
out᾽ ombros peraaske diamperes: ohs ara puknee
eeen, atar fullohn eneeen khusis eelitha pollee.
ton d᾽ androhn te kunohn te peri ktupos eelthe podoiin,
ohs epagontes epeesan: o d᾽ antios ek xulokhoio
frixas eu lofieen, pur d᾽ ofthalmoisi dedorkohs,
stee r᾽ autohn skhedothen: o d᾽ ara prohtistos Odusseus
essut᾽ anaskhomenos dolikhon doru kheiri pakheiee,
outamenai memaohs: o de min fthamenos elasen sus
gounos uper, pollon de dieefuse sarkos odonti
likrifis aixas, oud᾽ osteon iketo fohtos.
ton d᾽ Oduseus outeese tukhohn kata dexion ohmon,
antikru de dieelthe faeinou douros akohkee:
kad d᾽ epes᾽ en konieesi makohn, apo d᾽ eptato thumos.
ton men ar᾽ Autolukou paides filoi amfepenonto,
ohteileen d᾽ Oduseeos amumonos antitheoio
deesan epistamenohs, epaoidee d᾽ aima kelainon
eskhethon, aipsa d᾽ ikonto filou pros dohmata patros.
ton men ar᾽ Autolukos te kai uiees Autolukoio
eu ieesamenoi eed᾽ aglaa dohra porontes
karpalimohs khaironta fileen es patrid᾽ epempon
eis Ithakeen. toh men ra pateer kai potnia meeteer
khairon nosteesanti kai exereeinon ekasta,
ouleen otti pathoi: o d᾽ ara sfisin eu katelexen
ohs min theereuont᾽ elasen sus leukoh odonti,
Parneesond᾽ elthonta sun uiasin Autolukoio.

teen greeus kheiressi katapreenessi labousa
gnoh r᾽ epimassamenee, poda de proeeeke feresthai:
en de lebeeti pese kneemee, kanakheese de khalkos,
aps d᾽ eterohs᾽ eklithee: to d᾽ epi khthonos exekhuth᾽ udohr.
teen d᾽ ama kharma kai algos ele frena, toh de oi osse
dakruofi pleesthen, thaleree de oi eskheto fohnee.
apsamenee de geneiou Odusseea proseeipen:
"

ee mal᾽ Odusseus essi, filon tekos: oude s᾽ egoh ge
prin egnohn, prin panta anakt᾽ emon amfafaasthai.
"

ee kai Peenelopeian esedraken ofthalmoisi,
pefradeein ethelousa filon posin endon eonta.
ee d᾽ out᾽ athreesai dunat᾽ antiee oute noeesai:
tee gar Atheenaiee noon etrapen: autar Odusseus
kheir᾽ epimassamenos farugos labe dexitereefi,
tee d᾽ eteree ethen asson erussato fohneesen te.
"

maia, tiee m᾽ etheleis olesai; su de m᾽ etrefes autee
toh soh epi mazoh: nun d᾽ algea polla mogeesas
eeluthon eikostoh etei es patrida gaian.
all᾽ epei efrasthees kai toi theos embale thumoh,
siga, mee tis t᾽ allos eni megaroisi putheetai.
ohde gar exereoh, kai meen tetelesmenon estai:
ei kh᾽ up᾽ emoi ge theos damasee mneesteeras agauous,
oude trofou ousees seu afexomai, oppot᾽ an allas
dmohas en megaroisin emois kteinohmi gunaikas.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Eurukleia:
"teknon emon, poion se epos fugen erkos odontohn.
oistha men oion emon menos empedon oud᾽ epieikton,
exoh d᾽ ohs ote tis stereee lithos eee sideeros.
allo de toi ereoh, su d᾽ eni fresi balleo seesin:
ei kh᾽ upo soi ge theos damasee mneesteeras agauous,
dee tote toi katalexoh eni megaroisi gunaikas,
ai te s᾽ atimazousi kai ai neeleitides eisi.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus
"maia, tiee de su tas mutheeseai; oude ti se khree.
eu nu kai autos egoh frasomai kai eisom᾽ ekasteen:
all᾽ ekhe sigee muthon, epitrepson de theoisin.
"

ohs ar᾽ efee, greeus de diek megaroio bebeekei
oisomenee podaniptra: ta gar proter᾽ ekkhuto panta.
autar epei nipsen te kai eeleipsen lip᾽ elaioh,
autis ar᾽ assoteroh puros elketo difron Odusseus
thersomenos, ouleen de kata rakeessi kalupse.

toisi de muthohn eerkhe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"xeine, to men s᾽ eti tutthon egohn eireesomai autee:
kai gar dee koitoio takh᾽ essetai eedeos ohree,
on tina g᾽ upnos eloi glukeros, kai keedomenon per.
autar emoi kai penthos ametreeton pore daimohn:
eemata men gar terpom᾽ oduromenee, gooohsa,
es t᾽ ema erg᾽ oroohsa kai amfipolohn eni oikoh:
autar epeen nux elthee, eleesi te koitos apantas,
keimai eni lektroh, pukinai de moi amf᾽ adinon keer
oxeiai meledohnes oduromeneen erethousin.
ohs d᾽ ote Pandareou kouree, khlohreeis aeedohn,
kalon aeideesin earos neon istamenoio,
dendreohn en petaloisi kathezomenee pukinoisin,
ee te thama trohpohsa kheei polueekhea fohneen,
paid᾽ olofuromenee Itulon filon, on pote khalkoh
kteine di᾽ afradias, kouron Zeethoio anaktos,
ohs kai emoi dikha thumos orohretai entha kai entha,
eee menoh para paidi kai empeda panta fulassoh,
kteesin emeen, dmohas te kai upserefes mega dohma,
euneen t᾽ aidomenee posios deemoio te feemin,
ee eedee am᾽ epohmai Akhaiohn os tis aristos
mnatai eni megaroisi, porohn apereisia edna.
pais d᾽ emos eeos eeen eti neepios eede khalifrohn,
geemasth᾽ ou m᾽ eia posios kata dohma lipousan:
nun d᾽ ote dee megas esti kai eebees metron ikanei,
kai dee m᾽ aratai palin elthemen ek megaroio,
kteesios askhaloohn, teen oi katedousin Akhaioi.
all᾽ age moi ton oneiron upokrinai kai akouson.
kheenes moi kata oikon eeikosi puron edousin
ex udatos, kai te sfin iainomai eisoroohsa:
elthohn d᾽ ex oreos megas aietos agkulokheilees
pasi kat᾽ aukhenas eexe kai ektanen: oi d᾽ ekekhunto
athrooi en megarois, o d᾽ es aithera dian aerthee.
autar egoh klaion kai ekohkuon en per oneiroh,
amfi d᾽ em᾽ eegerethonto euplokamides Akhaiai,
oiktr᾽ olofuromeneen o moi aietos ektane kheenas.
aps d᾽ elthohn kat᾽ ar᾽ ezet᾽ epi proukhonti melathroh,
fohnee de broteee katereetue fohneesen te:
"

tharsei, Ikariou kouree teelekleitoio:
ouk onar, all᾽ upar esthlon, o toi tetelesmenon estai.
kheenes men mneesteeres, egoh de toi aietos ornis
eea paros, nun aute teos posis eileeloutha,
os pasi mneesteersin aeikea potmon efeesoh.
"

ohs efat᾽, autar eme melieedees upnos aneeke:
papteenasa de kheenas eni megaroisi noeesa
puron ereptomenous para puelon, eekhi paros per.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"oh gunai, ou pohs estin upokrinasthai oneiron
allee apoklinant᾽, epei ee ra toi autos Odusseus
pefrad᾽ opohs teleei: mneesteersi de fainet᾽ olethros
pasi mal᾽, oude ke tis thanaton kai keeras aluxei.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"xein᾽, ee toi men oneiroi ameekhanoi akritomuthoi
gignont᾽, oude ti panta teleietai anthrohpoisi.
doiai gar te pulai ameneenohn eisin oneirohn:
ai men gar keraessi teteukhatai, ai d᾽ elefanti:
tohn oi men k᾽ elthohsi dia pristou elefantos,
oi r᾽ elefairontai, epe᾽ akraanta ferontes:
oi de dia xestohn keraohn elthohsi thuraze,
oi r᾽ etuma krainousi, brotohn ote ken tis ideetai.
all᾽ emoi ouk enteuthen oiomai ainon oneiron
elthemen: ee k᾽ aspaston emoi kai paidi genoito.
allo de toi ereoh, su d᾽ eni fresi balleo seesin:
eede dee eeohs eisi dusohnumos, ee m᾽ Oduseeos
oikou aposkheesei: nun gar katatheesoh aethlon,
tous pelekeas, tous keinos eni megaroisin eoisin
istaskh᾽ exeiees, druokhous ohs, dohdeka pantas:
stas d᾽ o ge pollon aneuthe diarriptasken oiston.
nun de mneesteeressin aethlon touton efeesoh:
os de ke reeitat᾽ entanusee bion en palameesi
kai dioisteusee pelekeohn duokaideka pantohn,
toh ken am᾽ espoimeen, nosfissamenee tode dohma
kouridion, mala kalon, enipleion biotoio:
tou pote memneesesthai oiomai en per oneiroh.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus
"oh gunai aidoiee Laertiadeoh Oduseeos,
meeketi nun anaballe domois eni touton aethlon:
prin gar toi polumeetis eleusetai enthad᾽ Odusseus,
prin toutous tode toxon euxoon amfafoohntas
neureen t᾽ entanusai dioisteusai te sideerou.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe perifrohn Peenelopeia:
"ei k᾽ ethelois moi, xeine, pareemenos en megaroisi
terpein, ou ke moi upnos epi blefaroisi khutheiee.
all᾽ ou gar pohs estin aupnous emmenai aiei
anthrohpous: epi gar toi ekastoh moiran etheekan
athanatoi thneetoisin epi zeidohron arouran.
all᾽ ee toi men egohn uperohion eisanabasa
lexomai eis euneen, ee moi stonoessa tetuktai,
aiei dakrus᾽ emoisi pefurmenee, ex ou Odusseus
ohkhet᾽ epopsomenos Kakoilion ouk onomasteen.
entha ke lexaimeen: su de lexeo tohd᾽ eni oikoh,
ee khamadis storesas ee toi kata demnia thentohn.
"

ohs eipous᾽ anebain᾽ uperohia sigaloenta,
ouk oiee, ama tee ge kai amfipoloi kion allai.
es d᾽ uperoh᾽ anabasa sun amfipoloisi gunaixi
klaien epeit᾽ Oduseea, filon posin, ofra oi upnon
eedun epi blefaroisi bale glaukohpis Atheenee.


Book 20
-------

autar o en prodomoh eunazeto dios Odusseus:
kam men adepseeton boeeen stores᾽, autar uperthe
kohea poll᾽ oiohn, tous ireueskon Akhaioi:
Eurunomee d᾽ ar᾽ epi khlainan bale koimeethenti.
enth᾽ Oduseus mneesteersi kaka froneohn eni thumoh
keit᾽ egreegoroohn: tai d᾽ ek megaroio gunaikes
eeisan, ai mneesteersin emisgeskonto paros per,
alleeleesi geloh te kai eufrosuneen parekhousai.
tou d᾽ ohrineto thumos eni steethessi filoisi:
polla de mermeerize kata frena kai kata thumon,
eee metaixas thanaton teuxeien ekastee,
ee et᾽ eoh mneesteersin uperfialoisi migeenai
ustata kai pumata, kradiee de oi endon ulaktei.
ohs de kuohn amaleesi peri skulakessi bebohsa
andr᾽ agnoieesas᾽ ulaei memonen te makhesthai,
ohs ra tou endon ulaktei agaiomenou kaka erga:
steethos de pleexas kradieen eenipape muthoh:
"

tetlathi dee, kradiee: kai kunteron allo pot᾽ etlees.
eemati toh ote moi menos askhetos eesthie Kuklohps
ifthimous etarous: su d᾽ etolmas, ofra se meetis
exagag᾽ ex antroio oiomenon thaneesthai.
"

ohs efat᾽, en steethessi kathaptomenos filon eetor:
toh de mal᾽ en peisee kradiee mene tetleeuia
nohlemeohs: atar autos elisseto entha kai entha.
ohs d᾽ ote gaster᾽ aneer poleos puros aithomenoio,
empleieen knisees te kai aimatos, entha kai entha
aiollee, mala d᾽ ohka lilaietai opteetheenai,
ohs ar᾽ o g᾽ entha kai entha elisseto, mermeerizohn
oppohs dee mneesteersin anaidesi kheiras efeesei
mounos eohn polesi. skhedothen de oi eelthen Atheenee
ouranothen katabasa: demas d᾽ eeikto gunaiki:
stee d᾽ ar᾽ uper kefalees kai min pros muthon eeipe:
"

tipt᾽ aut᾽ egreesseis, pantohn peri kammore fohtohn;
oikos men toi od᾽ esti, gunee de toi eed᾽ eni oikoh
kai, pais, oion pou tis eeldetai emmenai uia.
"

teen d᾽ apameibomenos prosefee polumeetis Odusseus:
"nai dee tauta ge panta, thea, kata moiran eeipes:
alla ti moi tode thumos eni fresi mermeerizei,
oppohs dee mneesteersin anaidesi kheiras efeesoh,
mounos eohn: oi d᾽ aien aollees endon easi.
pros d᾽ eti kai tode meizon eni fresi mermeerizoh:
ei per gar kteinaimi Dios te sethen te ekeeti,
pee ken upekprofugoimi; ta se frazesthai anohga.
"

ton d᾽ aute proseeipe thea glaukohpis Atheenee:
"skhetlie, kai men tis te khereioni peitheth᾽ etairoh,
os per thneetos t᾽ esti kai ou tosa meedea oiden:
autar egoh theos eimi, diamperes ee se fulassoh
en pantessi ponois. ereoh de toi exanafandon:
ei per penteekonta lokhoi meropohn anthrohpohn
nohi peristaien, kteinai memaohtes Areei,
kai ken tohn elasaio boas kai ifia meela.
all᾽ eletoh se kai upnos: aniee kai to fulassein
pannukhon egreessonta, kakohn d᾽ upoduseai eedee.
"

ohs fato, kai ra oi upnon epi blefaroisin ekheuen,
autee d᾽ aps es Olumpon afiketo dia theaohn.

eute ton upnos emarpte, luohn meledeemata thumou,
lusimelees, alokhos d᾽ ar᾽ epegreto kedna iduia:
klaie d᾽ ar᾽ en lektroisi kathezomenee malakoisin.
autar epei klaiousa koressato on kata thumon,
Artemidi prohtiston epeuxato dia gunaikohn:
"

Artemi, potna thea, thugater Dios, aithe moi eedee
ion eni steethessi balous᾽ ek thumon eloio
autika nun, ee epeita m᾽ anarpaxasa thuella
oikhoito proferousa kat᾽ eeeroenta keleutha,
en prokhoees de baloi apsorroou Ohkeanoio.
ohs d᾽ ote Pandareou kouras anelonto thuellai:
teesi tokeeas men fthisan theoi, ai d᾽ eliponto
orfanai en megaroisi, komisse de di᾽ Afroditee
turoh kai meliti glukeroh kai eedei oinoh:
Eeree d᾽ auteesin peri paseohn dohke gunaikohn
eidos kai pinuteen, meekos d᾽ epor᾽ Artemis agnee,
erga d᾽ Atheenaiee dedae kluta ergazesthai.
eut᾽ Afroditee dia prosestikhe makron Olumpon,
kourees aiteesousa telos thaleroio gamoio--
es Dia terpikeraunon, o gar t᾽ eu oiden apanta,
moiran t᾽ ammorieen te katathneetohn anthrohpohn--
tofra de tas kouras arpuiai aneereipsanto
kai r᾽ edosan stugereesin erinusin amfipoleuein:
ohs em᾽ aistohseian Olumpia dohmat᾽ ekhontes,
eee m᾽ euplokamos baloi Artemis, ofr᾽ Oduseea
ossomenee kai gaian upo stugereen afikoimeen,
meede ti kheironos andros eufrainoimi noeema.
alla to men kai anekton ekhei kakon, oppote ken tis
eemata men klaiee, pukinohs akakheemenos eetor,
nuktas d᾽ upnos ekheesin--o gar t᾽ epeleesen apantohn,
esthlohn eede kakohn, epei ar blefar᾽ amfikalupsee--
autar emoi kai oneirat᾽ epesseuen kaka daimohn.
teede gar au moi nukti paredrathen eikelos autoh,
toios eohn oios eeen ama stratoh: autar emon keer
khair᾽, epei ouk efameen onar emmenai, all᾽ upar eedee.
"

ohs efat᾽, autika de khrusothronos eeluthen Eeohs.
